                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon Jo

1)  
Which Side Do I Stand On?  
<Summary of the Words> How many capable young people will emerge from among us? I am not calling you here to make you work for the sake of expanding our church's foundation. If you could succeed elsewhere without going through such hardships, I wouldn't do this. If we talk about difficulties, there is no need to speak in the most difficult place in the world, Korea. However, you must understand that there is a heavenly providence for the Korean people.  
You need to endure some hardships. You need to feel hunger. If the will is fulfilled, what can't be done? It's not a matter of recognition. Jesus said that only those who do the will of the Father are my brothers and sisters.  
If you are obsessed with food because you are hungry, you are nothing more than a child of a servant. The greatest enemy eats and sleeps.  
In the deep realm of virtue, one does not eat and sleep excessively.  
It is good to attend this gathering, but while attendance is voluntary, you must take responsibility afterward. We must establish the tradition of the training session.  
If you cannot receive what is given at the right time, you may lose it after it has been given, and that will lead to serious problems. In such cases, the future of descendants, clans, and the entire village will be blocked, resulting in hindrances for all outstanding individuals.  
December 3, 1960 (Saturday), Former Headquarters Church (Cheongpa-dong 1-ga, Seoul).  
* These words were given to the trainees attending the 4th Association's 40-day evangelist training session, and they were organized based on notes taken by Chairman Yoo Kwang-ryeol of the Association's Historical Compilation Committee at that time. The title was added by the editor.  
8   Which Side Do I Stand On?  
It is pitiful to see this nation without hope through the eyes that understand the will.  
I want to call young people like you to vent my anger on Satan. I will do that for three years.  
It would be good if you receive this will well, but if you cannot, it is better to leave altogether.  
A fledgling chick eats whatever its mother gives it. If you start to criticize and analyze this and that, you will all die. So there is no other way.  
If all 30 million people were like that (with the attitude of fledgling chicks), I believe the will would have already been fulfilled.  
You must not doze off. If you doze off, Satan will follow.  
Before heaven, I am in a position to blame Satan. Is there anyone who can claim that?  
The question is whether heaven believes in you.  
It is not about others; the first question is whether I can believe in myself.  
The teacher can endure any hardship. However, there is one problem: what will happen to humanity if the teacher is not here?  
You must pray to resolve and decide. In that sense, there is also a side where the teacher takes care of his body.  
One issue as a trainee is which side I am on. Even if I die, I must have something that does not change.  
Do you think God will help you while you are in a comfortable position?  
The youth of the Unification Church must have the mindset to do anything.  
During this period, while learning the principles, you must also internalize which side you stand on.  
The words I want to leave as a will are this: Until this will is fulfilled, until this life ends, I will only do what does not make heaven feel regret, with all my loyalty. That is enough. Whether I succeeded or failed is not the issue. Good things may be invaded, but the results are good, and bad things may have good promotions, but the results are bad.  
To achieve ten promotions, you must practice twenty times. *  
2)  
We Who Stand on the Frontline of God's Work  
Matthew 25:29-46  
<Prayer> (Unable to record for about 3 minutes due to a power outage)  
You have gathered humanity whenever they scattered throughout history, and whenever they lost their direction, you sent enemies to strike them down to show them the way.  
Two thousand years ago, you sent the Messiah as the leader of all people to gather the scattered multitude, the nations, and the world to glorify heaven, but the Messiah and the Israelite nation could not unite, and the scattered Israelite nation and the Messiah were divided, leading to two thousand years of bloody history and the continued suffering of the cross.  
Today is like the 40 years when the Israelite nation wandered in the wilderness, unable to find their way, and like the time when the history of the Israelite nation was concluded under heaven's whip due to their disbelief. In every aspect, I believe that the modern age is such a time.  
The Father hopes for a history that can manage such a time, and we also hope for it, but if we cannot manage our hearts and determine the direction we should go, even if someone appears to teach us the way and tells us to go there, we will know that we cannot go.  
December 11, 1960 (Sunday), Former Headquarters Church.  
10   We Who Stand on the Frontline of God's Work  
The problem is not that everything on this earth is scattered, but that the center of my heart is scattered, and I have lost my position and direction. We, who look at the phenomena of the end without knowing our position and direction, now that we know that the Father is the center, must kneel down and humble ourselves to align with the position and standard that the Father desires.  
At the end, we must anoint our heads and enter the secret place to pray, so let us establish ourselves in a position where the Father's emotional standards and our emotional standards align, and let us become those who seek the conditions for victory in our lives and discuss their value. If we cannot do that, let us realize that we cannot stand before the Father.  
We are in such a position, looking at such a society and the phenomena of the world, and we are in such an environment where our bodies and hearts are suffering, so please reshape us and establish the standard of heart, present the central work of the Father, and sanctify the center of our hearts. Please sanctify our bodies and environments so that we can connect with you.  
Father, please grant your merciful hand and grace to this nation. However, if you have a will that must be fulfilled through the oppressed and chased multitude, please let this nation be further oppressed and chased. In that, we understand that you hope for young people who want to take responsibility for the suffering and difficulties of this nation to emerge.  
Let us understand the sorrow of the Father who looks at humanity struggling on the front lines of death and the sorrow of this nation and people. May those sorrows be emotionally tied together and come before this nation with the cries of heaven's blood and the sighs, and may we realize that a fearful time is coming. We earnestly hope and desire for this, Father.  
Before the nation faces difficulties, we must first face difficulties ourselves, and before humanity faces difficulties, we must first cross the path of the cross. Jesus also walked the long road toward his heavenly nature in a chaotic environment and told us to walk that path. We know that this is the essence of the gospel that Jesus left behind, so let us become those who can take responsibility for everything standing at the forefront of this historical journey. Let us not be those who break and fall but become those who firmly establish a heartfelt connection with the Father every time we face challenges, so that we can stand before the Father. We earnestly hope and desire for this, Father.  
Please bless this day. I do not wish to say anything while standing on this platform today, but since you have allowed this time out of concern for these people and their path, please be with us. Please raise the work of grace that can connect hearts and harmonize minds and bodies, and let the hearts of the speaker and the listener become one. May our bodies and hearts become one with you, so that when you move to the right, we also move to the right, when you move to the left, we also move to the left, when you move, we also move, and when you are still, we also remain still, so that we can prepare the foundation of your holy life in our hearts. We humbly present our insufficient selves before you.  
Through the words we have read today, let us understand that Jesus himself, looking at the scattered multitude two thousand years ago, was pitiful and earnest. Jesus was hungry, Jesus was thirsty, Jesus became a stranger, Jesus was naked, Jesus was sick, and Jesus was imprisoned. The path that goes for the sake of truth has not been severed and has been inherited to us today, and we too are hungry, we are thirsty, we have become strangers, we are naked, we are sick, and we are imprisoned in the prison of death.  
Even in such hunger, nakedness, and miserable environments, let us help one another, connecting from heart to body, from body to heart, from hand to hand, and let us raise the name of the Father, sing the glory of the Father, and create a movement that swears before the Father to arise in this place. As time goes on, may this connection deepen, and I earnestly request and desire that you grant us the grace of love.  
12   We Who Stand on the Frontline of God's Work  
We entrust everything to you, so please do not let this time become one where Satan takes advantage. I earnestly request this in the name of the Lord. Amen.  
<Words> The title of the message I want to share with you at this time is "We Who Stand on the Frontline of God’s Work."  
We feel deeply that there must be a center in the universe. Even when looking at individuals, everyone hopes to maintain their personality centered on an absolute ideology or principle that cannot be questioned by anyone. The same goes for families. In any organization, that organization also moves together toward a single purpose through the struggle, united with its center. The same applies to nations. A nation with a center that cannot be moved by any force is a nation that cannot be defeated.  
All people living in this world possess a conscience. Historically, humanity has lived according to this conscience, striving to follow the path of good and create a new history. Nevertheless, we see the reality that humans suffer from the pursuit of good while being unable to escape the bonds of evil. When we see this, we cannot deny that there is an unchanging center that moves the world, seeking to connect humanity to an absolute standard.  
If that is the case, from my small self to this vast world, although the forms and phenomena connected to that center may differ, the principled direction must be consistent. We must find ourselves in that position, and the world must be in that position as well.  
Therefore, the world’s humanity and the universe must establish an unchanging center and an immutable foundation to find the solution to the problem.  
13  
If the world is like this, the absolute creator who created heaven and earth is the same. The created world can be seen as a reflection of the absolute creator's ideals. Therefore, the created world must become one with the creator and find an unchanging center to hold an eternal position, so that it can move when heaven moves and remain still when heaven is still.  
When the created world finds such an absolute and unchanging center, our conscience will find its position, and we will achieve our ultimate purpose and enjoy it even without thinking about it.  
So, does today’s world, and furthermore, heaven and earth, that is, all entities existing in the universe, have an unchanging center and are living in accordance with that position? They do not. Even the smallest particles exist in relative relationships with a center. This absolute principle cannot be denied by anyone. If the absolute creator created the created beings, it is an inevitable fact that the absolute creator and the created beings must have an inseparable and unchanging relationship.  
If it had been so from the very beginning, humanity would not have experienced painful environments, and the words anxiety and fear would not have been related to us, nor would there have been historical tragedies or terrible wars and struggles. If that were the case, we would have lived achieving the values we aimed for, and we would have entered an environment where the values we aimed for bore fruit, allowing us to enjoy them. Additionally, an infinitely peaceful and infinitely free ideal world would have unfolded before us. However, this is not the reality you, your families, your societies, your nations, and your world are facing.  
The Reality of Humanity  
What is the reason for the unavoidable tears in fulfilling the providence's will? It is because humanity has not captured the position that the absolute creator aims for and has not established an unchanging relationship from that position. Therefore, we must conclude that such results have occurred. No matter how capable someone is or how they can proclaim their name throughout the world, when they stumble, they too will find themselves in a fate of downfall. Thus, there have been leaders who guided nations throughout history, or patriots who expressed truths that could approach the world before heaven, but they too became subjects of historical criticism and disappeared as sacrifices of history.  
So, what are the current ideologies or thoughts we hold, the concepts we possess, the life goals we establish? Until those things manifest an unchanging, thorough, and principled center, they are one of...
It can only be a process. The processes do not come together as one. When a perfect center is established, one must realize that boasting about what one has accomplished in front of the world will only lead to shame. Even a successful person who can move the world cannot help but feel something coming in waves that shakes their heart. This is because an absolute, perfect existence, a distinct core being that cannot change, is penetrating this world and is moving even in this time. Good people with a conscience are advancing toward that.

You are humans who have lost your center. In religious terms, this can be called the retribution of the fall. It is the retribution of a fallen state that is unjust and resentful. This is something that our ancestors, who have gone through the history of the fall since creation, did not want, something that current humans do not want, and something that future generations will not want either. With this lamentable stain and the retribution of the fall, humanity has been tossed around, falling here and there, being torn apart and crushed, walking the path of death. It is painful because we were born into such a situation. We must recognize that we are in this position.

Then, since the fall, which heaven does not want, has occurred, what should we do about it? If there is no God who can resolve this, it is an extremely sorrowful matter. Today, the world is divided into two opposing camps, but it cannot solve this historical pain. We are in a position where we must give birth to a new world, which is impossible with anything conceived and planned by humans. Our hearts, soaked in ideologies, thoughts, and doctrines, cannot be turned back. We cannot mobilize all the cells and nerves of our bodies and run toward a new garden, a new ideological world with all our strength. This can only be resolved through an absolute being who can determine the value of the center of heaven.

Therefore, what is grateful is not any ideology of this world, nor any organization, nor any leader. It is the fact that there is an absolute being who has the method to resolve this tragic environment. There is no greater gratitude than the fact that there is a God who can save humanity, which has lost its center and homeland, and is in a state of complete destruction without being able to find any value. Therefore, one must respect God beyond any ideology or thought, beyond one’s own personality and value. As long as there is a conscience, one cannot deny this.

For whom do I exist? 

Thus, history has turned upside down. The left becomes the right, the right becomes the left, the front becomes the back, and the back becomes the front, turning upside down in all directions. Is it not so? Your daily life has been such, and your year and your entire life have been the same. Family life and social life are also turning upside down in such an environment. 

The left becomes the right, the right becomes the left, the up becomes the down, and the down becomes the up, while the front and back turn upside down and change in the historical process. Heaven is looking for a solution. The question for us is for whom we live and for whom we work. Even if the up becomes the down and the down becomes the up, and even if the front and back are reversed, we must become people who exist for heaven.

Even while falling and collapsing, humans did not know that there is a God who has carried out this operation. Therefore, those who have aimed for goodness, that is, good people who have followed the way, have suffered terrible things in every age. They became the fertilizer whenever the positions changed, and they became the fertilizer whenever the times changed. They shed unjust amounts of blood, sweat, and tears according to the changes of the times. At that time, they seemed to be the ones who were ruined, the ones who were pitiful, and the ones who deserved to be blamed, disappearing as enemies of the nation. However, their goal, their center, and their emotional life were solely directed toward the center of providence seeking one ideology, and further, toward God. Those who have held onto this meticulously have turned history upside down. Those who seemed to be failing broke through history, and those who seemed to be ruined managed history, as the historical process proves.

Where are we today? No matter how chaotic the environment may be, where it is impossible to find a center, even if one is in a position of death, one must know for whom one exists. This is what God wants to teach. To teach this to all people, God has brought forth the history of religion, the concept of the Messiah, and the idea of salvation. Therefore, for whom must we exist? We must exist for heaven. Whether we die or live, we must live for heaven. Such a person is not truly dead even if they die.

After all, history is something that turns upside down and breaks through the centuries and eras. No matter how great a success one achieves in that era, if it cannot connect with the center of heaven and does not align with God’s purpose, it will break. Even if it does not break at that time, there will only be a temporal difference, and ten years, a hundred years, or even a few centuries later, it will inevitably break. You are in such a historical process.

Because you are in this historical process, no matter how much you hold onto your family and children and claim to love them, that too will change at least once. Having gone through six thousand years of history, the center of this heart must change at least once. In the historical process of humanity until now, the circumstances of life have changed every year, every century, and every era. Everything has changed at least once. The end is when the emotional center changes without the human being even realizing it. At that time, everything in this world will change.

Until today, human morality has been that parents love their children, children are filial to their parents, and couples must be loyal to each other. This has been the cornerstone of the Three Bonds and Five Relationships passed down to this day, but this too is changing. The day will come when existing customs and norms will naturally change and penetrate into the social environment and living environment. If a global leader or Messiah appears on this earth, that person must resolve this issue. That is why Jesus came to this earth and said to love me more than anyone else.

Then, at this time when everyone is saying it is the end, you must know for whom you exist. You should not exist for yourself. You must exist for your country, for the world. Furthermore, you must exist for heaven and earth based on some ideology or thought. You must become a group that appears with the pride of existing for heaven and earth.

Today, all religions consider the earth as an enemy. However, we should not treat the earth as an enemy but as an object to achieve one purpose. Thus, you must be able to say that heaven and earth are mine, and I exist for heaven and earth.

If there is an absolute being, what kind of ideology and thought does He want to establish? It is to exist for heaven and earth. Furthermore, it is to exist for God and humanity, to respect that value, to highly evaluate that position, and to confidently declare that they will thoroughly pursue that direction. Such groups must emerge on this earth. This is what heaven desires, and this is what the history of humanity has longed for.

Until the Second World War, there was a struggle for material possession, and since then, until today, there has been a struggle for human possession. Now, in the end, there will be a struggle for the possession of God. To take God away, people claim that I am orthodox and you are heretical. You may have seen in yesterday's newspaper that even greater problems will arise in the future. Until now, heaven has left religious organizations alone, but from now on, it will swirl and create a vortex around global trends and global fortunes. It will either solve the problem from a motivational standpoint or push it into a relative position to resolve it. Therefore, many sects will break apart until that work is fulfilled.

In order for God's providence to conclude, 

In the process of human history moving toward a world of purpose, many nations have been broken and changed. God's providence, which seeks to establish a single conclusion, also goes through such a process. The ideology that can remain until the end to manage history is the ideology that exists for heaven, for earth, and for humanity. Therefore, those who have a heart standard that can connect through humanity, through God, and through heaven and earth, who can boast and sing of their value in heaven and earth, must emerge. Furthermore, there must be groups that can confidently say that heaven, earth, and God are ours, that God is our Father, and that I am His child.

How joyful it would be if God, who has never had a family, who has never had a nation, and who has never moved the world, found such individuals! God can establish the form of family, which is the foundation of society, centered around that person, and can form society around that family, and can establish a nation centered around that society to embark toward a new sovereign world.

God sent the Messiah to this earth, calling him the bridegroom, and humanity is called his bride. What does this mean? It means that God has established the first standard of the father and son, that is, the True Parents and True Children, in the historical process to record a new page in history.

Now is the time to wake up. It is time to reconsider what you have. You must think again while holding onto your spoon. You must critically reassess all the phenomena you see before your eyes. You must reorganize all your living conditions. Through a sincere heart, you must coldly judge and decide what is right and wrong, and be able to take the right and cut off the wrong.

Such things must happen in the final days. For whom? Not for oneself, but for God. In serving God, one must cut off oneself if one is wrong, cut off the family if the family is wrong, and be able to cut off and surpass the nation, the people, and the world without hesitation. One must be able to abandon all that is wrong within oneself and establish a position and direction that can connect with an unchangeable center, and be able to sing of the value of God, who is the subject of purpose, in life. If such a person exists, they are a great victor in the path of life. Humanity must go through such a process. Even if many people perish and many nations are destroyed, in order for the will of God's providence to conclude, one must go through such a core process.

You are fortunate, whether by fate or luck, to have been born in a good era that benefits from the times. Even if you are beaten, you are beaten directly, and even if you receive rewards, you receive them directly. You have been born in a time when you can hear words directly and receive admonishments directly. You have been born as the Korean people, but you cannot escape the position of being a nation that represents the world. The time of living only for my nation and my country has passed. Now is the era of globalism. In the process of mutual confrontation and struggle, unless you emerge with a value position and direction that surpasses the ideologies or thoughts of a single society, you cannot possibly move toward a new era. Moreover, even if you are a subjugated nation, you cannot become a dominating nation.

What have humans on this earth dominated until now? They have devoted all their efforts to dominating material and the body. On the other hand, religion has cut off material and the body and has dominated the conscience. This is the two-pronged historical process. Although we did not know, in the historical process, God has come forth with the intention of expanding the connections of conscientious history to establish a being with a core ideology so that humans can unite with it. Two thousand years ago, after four thousand years of the fall, a person appeared before humans who had lost the direction of their conscience, like a magnet, a person with a positive conscience, who is Jesus. He was the true person, the good person.

What will happen to this history? What will it culminate around? Historical perspectives or ideologies centered on material and the body cannot become the foundation of the world. Those who have cut off worldly connections and have aimed for goodness according to their conscience, that is, those who walk the path of the way, can become the foundation of the world. Their path is pitiful. They are poor. Even looking at their faces or their situations, they are pitiful people. The path they walk is desolate. Their families cannot follow them. It is a path that must be walked alone, a path that, once taken, cannot be returned from. On that path, if one does not achieve their purpose, they will collapse and perish. That is the path of the way.

If we look back at the history of Israel, we will know that it is a path that cannot be returned from once taken. On the day of return, one dies. When the Israelite people joyfully escaped from the palace of Pharaoh in Egypt and ran vigorously toward the desolate wilderness, they were filled with indescribable hope and expectation, but that path was a miserable one. It was a path where they could not even take a bundle with them, a path where they could not even take a single blanket to sleep comfortably. It was a path that required them to abandon everything. It was a path of hunger, thirst, wandering, nakedness, and a path of death where they fell ill and collapsed. Until today, many people who love the way have walked such a path in the historical process of humanity. It is a path where one must abandon beloved sons and daughters, a path where one must die even if they have a heavenly connection, a path where one must stake their entire life. It is a path of destiny where one must turn back and walk alone, shedding tears of pain that pierce the bones and flesh while leaving behind beloved family. Yet, there is no clear purpose in walking this path. It is an ambiguous path. Those who wander in search of the way are truly pitiful. At the same time, families that seek such a path are pitiful. If there is such a nation, that nation is also pitiful.

The Israelite people have directly betrayed heaven, and they have also ruined the works of heaven. They are a pitiful nation. With the ideology of the one true God, they have not lost their center anywhere, yet they have been massacred and abused wherever they go, and they have been wandering until now. It is a pitiful historical process. We must understand that heaven's history is like that. That path cannot be traveled by two. It is a path that can only be traveled alone.

In this historical process, the world will not go as the world does, nor will heaven go as heaven does. We must establish a standard that can say that individuals have been established and families have been established, and then we must pull that individual out and send them back. The one who has been sent back to represent the entire value of those who have walked that path for four thousand years is the Messiah. That person is the Messiah. This Messiah is the embodiment of the blood shed by our ancestors, the embodiment of sacrifice, the embodiment of suffering, the embodiment of tears, and the embodiment of sweat. He is also the resurrected body of our ancestors, the central being who must strike down the enemies and resolve the grievances of our ancestors, and the one who has inherited the promise of Canaan.
The Era of Divine-Human Equality Must Come

Today's world is a world that fights for the body and material. No matter how much economics, science, and ideology develop, they cannot bring peace to humanity. It is not enough. Unless some ideology or divine movement that can re-evaluate this body and material appears in the world of the heart, this world will perish. Now, heaven has reached the final era where it must decisively determine a single center. Living in such an era, how will we resolve and settle these many issues? This problem has emerged globally in two ideologies: one is materialism, and the other is idealism. They have been distinctly divided. If we go along with the earth and the body, we will perish. Therefore, we must settle with God.

What we must advocate here is the heart, but who is the subject of this heart? We must bring this out. The subject of the heart is God. However, it is not an abstract God. 

The time has come to focus on God. After thousands of years of historical progress, when has an ideology or thought that centers on God emerged? It has not. No nation or ideology has centered its thought on God. The vague shadow of democracy is what we see today. Moving forward, we must go beyond the era of human rights advocacy and gender equality to a place that defends divine authority and asserts that God and humanity are equal. Until now, God has not been able to act as God.

What does it mean that God has not been able to act as God? It means that God and humanity have not entered into an equal position. This is a mistake. Divine authority must be defended. We must advocate for divine authority. How can we talk about equality and freedom when we are in a position where we cannot even relate to the subject who created us? We must go to a position of equality with God. To reach that position, it cannot be done without tears, and we must not go without repentance and striking our hearts. We must go beyond the position where we cannot see God correctly and reach a place where we can sing, "My Father!" and hear Him say, "Yes!" When Mary Magdalene tried to hold onto Jesus after His resurrection, He said, "Do not touch me, for I have not yet ascended." The end is the time when God spreads His loving hands and comes to embrace all people, saying, "My sons and daughters!" Therefore, we must cry out for the defense of divine authority and the equality of God and humanity. When the time comes for God and humanity to unite and sing together in a land of freedom, God's work of restoration will also be completed, and the hopes of humanity will all be fulfilled.

Until now, humanity has been unaware of God's movement for this purpose and has been asleep. While living loving their own children, they did not know that there is a God who weeps while looking at such people. Humanity has sung of peaceful families and free families, but God has come forth with tears.

"You are my sons and daughters, yet you sing of peace in the enemy's family. You have become sacrifices for the enemy and toil." This is what has made God weep. When He sees people who are embraced by the arch-enemy Satan, not knowing the path to take while living with their children, it is as if He is going mad. Who knew of such things?

God's Desires and the Path Walked by Central Figures

What does God want to show before the enemy? It is the human figure that can say, "You are my beloved son, and you are my beloved daughter." He wanted to boast before Satan of the human figure that has become one with the heart of love, united in the relationship of father and son, more than any other person in the historical process. However, this desire of God has not been fulfilled from the creation until today. 

All of humanity was meant to live happily in a garden filled with freedom and peace as God's sons and daughters, singing of the defense of divine authority and the equality of God and humanity, but now they are struggling in lamentation and despair. They are caught by the enemy that blocks the subject of hope, the enemy that confuses the path of conscience.

Our ancestors, who silently sought the truth and quietly sought the good, longed for a day of hope that could please God throughout their lives, yet they have not met that day even until this end time. If we do not meet and serve the one who will fulfill that day, what will happen to humanity? When we think of this, we must awaken anew. We must make a new resolution and determination. We must recognize that there is a God who is indignant and resentful, that there are our brothers who are pitiful and miserable, and that there remains a resentment for not establishing the sovereignty and ideology that God wanted to establish. 

Those who seek the truth have not had families. They are all wanderers, naked. They are a pitiful group. They are people who have walked a path where they cannot even sleep comfortably for a single night, yet they call God their Father. It is a tragic and lamentable situation.

Noah of old was indignant, and Abraham was indignant. Moreover, those who were chosen as subjects of the circumstances and situations, even if they did not know the details, walked a path of resentment. Jacob, who was moving forward with the single-minded thought of serving God, went to Haran and had to sleep with a stone for a pillow while shedding tears. It is a lamentable situation. Moses was the same. All the splendid external conditions of Pharaoh's palace could not bring peace to his heart or make him happy and satisfied. The place he was in was the position of the enemy. Therefore, you must know that Moses, who knelt before heaven with a single heart and shed tears that no one knew, did not cease to pray.

Moses' heart became fervent toward heaven, and he finally broke away from the palace. He was waiting for the time when heaven would allow him, and at the age of 40, when he could discern the world and distinguish between right and wrong, he broke away from the palace toward the Israelite people. What kind of path did he take? He, who used to eat luxuriously and wear splendid clothes, went to find the suffering Israelite people, who were tormented, with a heart filled with shining loyalty and purpose, wearing simple clothes and simple shoes. You must understand that Moses' steps were solemn.

Moses' 40 years of life were lamentable, but it was even more lamentable to be betrayed by the Israelite people he went to. Therefore, we must think of the sorrow of Moses, who could not even stay in the enemy's land of Egypt and went out to the wilderness of Midian. However, despite the changing environment and his own miserable and insignificant condition, his single-mindedness did not change. Knowing that the path he was taking was the path of historical sacrifice, and that it was the historical path left by the saints, Moses worked for 40 years as a shepherd to become a friend of the people walking the historical path and to pioneer the path of truth that countless future humans would have to walk. He looked at the pastureland as the land of Canaan and thought of the sheep grazing as the Israelite people, weeping as he embraced the sheep. You must understand that God, who saw Moses holding onto that land and the sheep, was able to bless the foundation of Moses' heart, saying, "Take off your sandals, for the place you are standing is holy ground." 

Moses was in a pitiful position, but it was his earnest heart that cried out that connected him with God. We have come to know that the path of serving God is such a lamentable one. This path is not one that only Moses walked.

The Path of Saints Who Must Walk a Lamentable and Resentful Path

Jesus, who was sent as the Messiah, the culmination of 4,000 years to resolve the history of the Israelite people and to fulfill God's resentment, was joyful in one aspect, but his situation on this earth was sad and lamentable. Why did he not have a nation like others? Why was he not born with power? It was because he had to walk the inevitable path of indemnity. God, who knows this, is indignant but sent Jesus to the cross and sent the Holy Spirit as a central figure on this earth. The earth symbolizes the mother, so the Mother Spirit must come in place of the ascended Jesus. Thus, the history of Christianity until now has been about coming to this earth, building altars, shedding tears, and establishing the relationship between humanity and the mother. It is a lamentable and resentful situation.

While longing for a day of hope, the Christian believers are like orphans, like wanderers, wearing tattered clothes and struggling throughout the 6,000 years of history. They are a group that cannot sleep comfortably for even a single night.

The Israelite people, who once said, "I am better than you," have become food for ravens and eagles in the wilderness. When we think of this, we must awaken today. Let us awaken and resolve the resentful historical facts in our time. Let us put all our energy into it. We must become offerings before the ideologies that discuss democratic society and assert that there is a God.

Who will receive the blessings of heaven in this era? It will not be those who sleep comfortably. If we know that heaven has not yet rested, we cannot rest here. The group that walks the lamentable path before this world can dominate this world. We must feel resentment. For whom should we feel resentment? Not for ourselves, but for God. The end is the time to resolve grievances. God is resentful for not being able to share the heart of love that He wants to express, for not being able to establish the people He wishes to establish, and for not being able to find the family He seeks. We must think of God, who is so resentful, and with a heart that aches, we must become a group that can raise the torch toward the world. God desires such a group to appear.

History is colliding and returning to establish a single conclusion between East and West. We must not fall here; we must rise from the center of this terrible whirlpool and say, "O God! Please send me to your path of sorrow, pain, and resentment." God is waiting for a group with the integrity of Moses, who tended sheep in the wilderness. He is looking for a group of people like Abraham, who was loyal to God in Ur of the Chaldeans, and like Jacob, who prepared to face God for 21 years in Haran. Surely, such a group must emerge.

Dear ones, do not be discouraged by shedding tears today. Even if you sweat blood, do not be discouraged. The fate of the world is now at a point of life and death. At such a time, where will you go? Will you remain in the palace? The place we live is not our hometown. There is surely a homeland we must go to. From our ancestors, Adam and Eve, to the enemy, there is a homeland where we can say, "Hallelujah!" We must know that there is a path left to go to that homeland. Those who leave this behind will perish. They will perish.

We Must Prepare Ourselves with Heart

Dear ones! Clarify yourself. Re-analyze yourself. You must know whose blood runs in your veins, whose flesh you are made of, and whose bones you have. "Oh hands, you are the hands that God has grasped. Oh body, even if you fall, all people may mock you, but God will hold you and shed tears."

You must become those who can claim this. Even if the body is torn, beaten, and imprisoned, you must be the one whom God can reach through the bars and say, "My son!" If you wish to transcend the historical ideologies, you must surely become that.

The time will come. We must understand that while we are busy waiting for the time, God, who comes to find the time, is even busier. You must know that God's heart, which must remain in the place of patience, is more anxious than those who are exhausted and collapsing.

Do not understand this only as the words of a young person standing here; establish logical arguments and critically evaluate based on that perspective. There must be something different from what has been until now for humanity to live again. If there is nothing, it will perish. Live as you wish. Try to live as if you have a foundation of happiness, even if it is done hastily. It will perish. Who would have known that a vulture would suddenly descend upon the carcass that Abraham was to offer to God? Do you think it is easy to build an eternal palace of peace? It is not easy at all.

Now is the time to establish such a world, so just as Moses prepared himself, Jacob prepared himself, Abraham prepared himself, and Jesus prepared himself, we must also prepare ourselves. For what purpose? Not for my country, but for the world, and furthermore, for heaven, we must prepare ourselves.

O brides who must welcome the bridegroom! You must equip yourselves inside and out. Preparation is not done with material things. It must be done with the heart. You must prepare with the hearts of humanity, the heart of God, and the heart of the Lord. The heart of heaven must be the motivation within me, and the heart of the earth must be the result within me, so I must prepare as the embodiment of the heart of Alpha and Omega. Thus, God, who was looking far into history, can pull it closer and see it, and humanity, which has been seeking hope, can abandon all previous ideologies and thoughts.

Unless a person appears on this earth who can say, "You cannot change the world even if you give it," the world will perish. This is not a public discussion. Now is the final time when life and death are intertwined. It is the time to stand on the front line of God and make the final decision and determine victory and defeat. In other words, we are standing on the front line of God. Then, what kind of battle is that? It is not a material or external battle. It is a battle of the heart, a battle of the mind. There are many enemies in this heart. All the external matters that appear in the world are enemies. 

The Purpose of God's Front Line and the Purpose of Creating That Front Line

Noah fought alone for 120 years against numerous enemies, wanting to blame, accuse, curse, and test Satan. He fought alone against countless enemies. He did not fight with a spear; he fought with his heart. He did not suffer wounds from the spears of enemies but suffered wounds in his heart. He stood in a position where God could have compassion for him because he bore the wounds that God had suffered for 1,600 years since Adam. Therefore, God sought him. 

After that, for another 1,600 years, God did not allow His front line to be taken by the enemy. Because he did not lose the high ground of the ark to Satan, God was able to mobilize angels and carry out the judgment of the flood centered on that. Thus, God established Noah's ark as the ultimate front line that only He could take, but again, a front line of Satan emerged there. How must God's heart have felt? It is too lamentable that after being unjustly attacked and receiving the arrows of Satan for 1,600 years, a front line of Satan emerged again in Noah's family, which was supposed to establish a victorious front line and build a garden of peace. 

Ham's mistake was not just a personal mistake but a historical mistake, and Noah...
The anger of Ham was not a personal anger but a universal anger. However, Ham did not understand this fact. Noah, chosen and established as an individual, also did not realize that he was being used so greatly and that he was a being of such great value. Even after God judged the earth and swept countless nations away as food for the flesh, they did not understand God's profound love that saved only Noah's eight family members. The place where Noah's eight family members were was the frontline of God's love. It was the frontline of God's love. That is why Ham's mistake brought such a great grievance. Once the frontline of God's love was violated, God could not remain there, so He handed them all over to Satan and endured injustice for 400 years with that nation.

Thus, after 2,000 years, God sought and established Abraham. God intended to set humans in place of Himself on the fragile frontline He had established, so that humans could subdue Satan. Therefore, God established Abraham and then Isaac and Jacob, laying the groundwork for a strategy to deal with humanity. Finally, during Jacob's time, He established a true commander who could move a family on earth in place of God. The family of Jacob became the frontline of God.

Who was Moses, who was sought and established through individuals, families, and nations, and what kind of nation was Israel? Moses was the chief commander of God's frontline, and the Israelite nation that followed him were the soldiers who were to protect God's frontline. However, the Israelite nation did not heed God's command to sound the marching trumpet and fight, and they rejected the earnest words of their chief commander, Moses. Thus, we must recognize the unfortunate fact that they were buried in the lonely wilderness as a sacrifice of sorrow.

God, who sought and established a nation, left Satan in charge of that nation and merely watched, choosing not to fight. However, because the nation failed to fulfill its responsibilities, God intervened and brought history forward again. It was God's intention that He would not engage in the frontline of the battle against Satan but that humans would gather together to defeat the city of Satan and establish one world. Therefore, the Israelite nation should not have acted as if they had God's authority just because God was with them; instead, they should have stood in the position of the most pitiful nation. To lead a nation, one must stand in the position of the most pitiful within that nation. To lead the world of Satan, one must stand at the end of the world of Satan. God established Moses as the leader of the nation, expecting him to express His heart from the most pitiful position.

After carrying out 1,600 years of history and meeting the time, God finally established Noah. Next, He established a family, then a nation, and finally the nation of Israel. In this process, God had to remain in a position where He did not lose the individual frontline, the family frontline, the national frontline, or the state frontline. Because of this, God has endured increased suffering. When the nation fails to take responsibility, what is not fulfilled before God adds to the family’s failures, and what is not fulfilled by individuals adds to that as well.

God sent Jesus to this earth to take responsibility for the frontline of God as a human being and to engage in spiritual battles as tangible battles. However, by killing Jesus, the humans on earth caused a separation between Jesus and the Holy Spirit, leading to an ongoing spiritual battle, compounded by physical battles. Therefore, we are told to strike the flesh. The Satan within this flesh is writhing, and we are called to strike it. It is a lamentable situation.

The Final Frontline
After 2,000 years, the end has come. It is time for God to establish a new Second Israel that can move with Christian believers and cross over into a new era. The Israelite nation was to become the chosen people of heaven, constructing the kingdom of heaven through the words of Jesus, but they missed that time. Thus, God, Jesus, and the Holy Spirit—the Trinity—bear the pain of the nation's suffering, the nation's suffering, the family's suffering, and the individual's suffering. Until now, the Trinity has come forth as the Father of the wronged on this earth and as the Lord of the oppressed; how pitiful and lamentable is this fact?

You must first understand what kind of Father you are seeking blessings from, what kind of Lord you believe in, and what kind of Holy Spirit you believe in. If you understand this, you cannot pray, "God, please heal this wound in my hand," nor can you easily ask God for help even if you are beaten and fallen. 

In this global end time, God must find the final heavenly frontline to establish the standard of victory along with historical destiny. At such a time, we must raise the beacon before all humanity. We must hang up banners that say, "Christians of the world! Daoists! Unite. Those with a conscience, gather!" We are approaching the time when we must rise as God's soldiers to the frontline and stand in the final battlefield against Satan. It is a grateful and thankful thing. Although it is somewhat frustrating, unjust, and lamentable, it is a good thing that the time has come to take responsibility and repay the enemy. This is precisely that time. It is historically that time.

Heaven will ask each of you, "Are you, so-and-so, the heavenly people of the Second Israel, occupying the enemies on this earth and possessing the land of victory and the people of victory?" Now is that time. It is not a time for fighting over who is better or worse. It is time for religious people around the world to gather and seek the ranks of Israel.

So what kind of perspective must be established? As I mentioned earlier, whose am I, and for whom do I exist? For whom are my eyes and all my senses? The body is the enemy, but the heart is heaven. You are the frontline of good and evil. This has unfolded vertically from the individual to the family, society, nation, and world. Now, you must take this vertical development and expand it horizontally, standing in the same position as Noah of old, Abraham, Jacob, Moses, Joshua, Caleb, and even Jesus. Will you stand in such a position? That time has come. There is no doubt about it. You must make a firm resolution. This is not just the words of someone standing here.

The Korean nation, which has come forward with many grievances! This nation has said, "Be hungry. Be naked. Be a beggar." They have done everything according to the Bible. People of old who advanced for heaven did the same. If it is God's will to establish a global Israel in this end time, then a sacrificial nation that is oppressed and chased must emerge. The time has come for the cries of hunger to be heard. The time has come for the sighs of thirst to be heard. A nation that has become a wanderer with no place to stay must emerge. Is our nation not like that now? We are wanderers. So, can we survive by begging for food? We are hungry and sick. And we are trapped. This is true regionally.

If God in heaven sees this, He will establish such a nation as His heavenly soldiers before the world according to the trends of the times. What kind of appearance should the thirty million people of this nation take before such a destiny? Even if they are the smallest of the small, they must become the pitiful sons and daughters who hold onto God's bleeding heart, shedding tears and moving together with God's heart. Only then can this nation have a way to live.

You! Do not be discouraged. Our nakedness is not for ourselves, our hunger is not for ourselves, our thirst is not for ourselves, and our wanderer status is not for ourselves. Our sickness is not for ourselves. It is for the world. For this nation in such a position, there is only one way: let us not cry out for not being able to eat. Let us not cry out for being naked. Let us not sigh for being sick, and let us not be discouraged for being trapped. The footsteps of those who sought God's will and goodness over the course of 6,000 years have been like this, and God has also labored through this history from the day of the fall until now. Therefore, this thirty million people must become God's people who can remove the sad footprints of God laid over the course of 6,000 years and comfort Him.

Holding onto God as a nation, for the sake of our Father's nation, to pave the way for our Father to dwell, to build a house for our Father, and to prepare the land for our Father's arrival, if we move while being hungry, how great will that glory be? We must pioneer the foundation for our Father with the situation of being hungry and thirsty. Even if we appear to be an indescribably pitiful wanderer, we must walk the path of suffering beyond that wanderer, worrying about our Father who comes to find His sons and daughters, forgetting our own circumstances, and becoming a group that labors to comfort our Father. You must become those who can comfort God's heart, which is pained as He looks upon the decaying world of death, and relieve God's pain and suffering. If you do that, you will never perish.

Unification believers! The person speaking here does not wish to advocate for any particular denomination. The issue is not the label of a denomination. It is not about being good-looking or not, nor is it about being knowledgeable or ignorant. The only issue is whether we have an offering to present before God. To prepare that offering, you must know the hungry condition of God the Father and, shedding tears, be able to offer a piece of bread to God even in a state of hunger, and be able to offer a sip of water to God in a thirsty state. You must be able to sell even the only piece of clothing you have as a wanderer to offer to God, and you must be able to struggle to bear God's suffering even from a sickbed, and you must be willing to suffer on behalf of God even in a confined and uncomfortable environment.

God the Father will come to this nation, but who will He seek among them? He will seek the hungry. He will not come as the Father of those who eat and dance in luxury, but as the Father of the hungry. Therefore, we must become the hungry. He seeks the thirsty. This is because He has gone through such a historical path. He seeks the wanderer. Therefore, you must pass through the position of a wanderer. He seeks the imprisoned. He seeks the sick. This is because God's heart can dwell in such places. You must understand this. He is a Father who struggles with humanity, centered on His true heart, heavenly principles, and heavenly heart.

I want this nation to be so, I want our denomination to be so, and I want our believers to be so. From one perspective, I may seem like a cruel teacher or a cruel leader, but from the perspective of heavenly principles, I must push you into such a position. If I fail to do this, it will bring disaster to all humanity, and that is why it must be so. You must understand this.

Stand on God's Frontline and Become Victorious Soldiers
What is the purpose of pushing you like this? It is not for my own good. It is to call you as victorious soldiers on the path to building the kingdom of heaven, to sing the song of triumph as soldiers on God's frontline, and to give glory to God. If we do not go, God must go Himself, so He cannot help but command us to go.

If there is anyone who turns back on this path, thinking their life is precious, they will become the enemy of the millions of heavenly family members who have become martyrs and gone to heaven. If they take out their anger, it will not be directed at the enemy but at those who push them here. Therefore, this is a path that one cannot avoid.

I, as a heavenly offering, must be embraced in the bosom of God the Father, shedding red blood with God, and as a soldier standing on God's frontline, I must hold onto the hands of my comrades, embrace their bodies, shed tears, and even resolve to go to the place of death while seeing blood. If there is anyone who can make such a resolution, they will dominate the world. If there is someone who acknowledges God as their Father and dedicates their sincerity before heaven, they must understand that they can be recorded as apostles on the first page of a new history.

Our red blood is urging us to go down a path we do not even know, whether we are awake or asleep. Humans are beings who cannot escape their destined path, and ultimately, they must resolve the issue of life and death. Therefore, we must decide where to go. We know that the fierce battle at Baekma Hill has been highly regarded. This will be recorded in history and remain forever. Now is the time when sacrifices like those who fell at Baekma Hill are needed for the construction of the kingdom of heaven. You, who must eventually die and become a handful of dust, and whose body must fill a few pyeong of a graveyard.

You, who bear the grievances of history, must conclude the last remaining history and unfold a new history. The thirty million people who have inherited the great achievements of the heavenly struggle that heaven has cherished and kept for a long time must achieve victory in this one remaining battle, even if we have failed in ninety-nine previous battles. We must wash away the grievances of past defeats and strike down Satan, who boasts of historical victories, and give glory to God. You must clearly understand that you must become such people.

The environment you are facing is a battlefield. Every bite of food you eat, every piece of clothing I wear, and everything you see in the world is entangled in the conditions of battle. Know that all these things are eagerly awaiting the day they will be freed from the sighs of battle through your hands, and I ask that you establish the dignity of being God's frontline soldiers and become victorious soldiers who receive God's blessings.

<Prayer> Father! We have come to the place You commanded us to go. As we have come, we have realized that the final battle remains. Just as the Jordan River stood before the Israelite nation, who were joyfully looking toward the promised land, Canaan, the final battle lies ahead of us as well. We have understood that there was a three-day struggle to cross the Jordan River for that group who received the command to go toward the foundation of hope.

We know that the horrific bloodline of history that has been passed down until today must be reaped as a victory today. We have understood that the tears Jesus shed in the Garden of Gethsemane must be gathered to become a new Garden of Gethsemane, and the blood Jesus shed on Golgotha must be gathered to become a global Golgotha of victory.

This moment is a serious moment when we must solemnly step toward the throne of God the Father with a determined resolve, having received a final special mission. We have realized that our bodies and minds are not our own. For whom are we here? We are Yours, Father, and we exist for You. We have understood that our supply is not of this earth. While the supply of the body is equipped with four directions, the supply of the heart is one of poverty, sorrow, and grief. If we do not break through this and establish ourselves...
We have come to the moment where we must reach the final stronghold and wait for the last charge command. We earnestly hope and wish that at this moment, we may be filled with the solemn determination, vow, and conviction to bloom and fall. 

We fear that the cries of this day may become the conditions for judgment against these people. As we stand on the front line of God's work, like Elijah, we fear that the appeals of this day may become the conditions for judgment against them, just as our prayers were slandered. 

Let us become those who can fear the Father who punishes those who betray His will and add sorrow to the sad history. Even if our flesh is cut and our bones are broken, let us remain steadfast in our determined resolution until the end. If we dedicate our whole body and heart for the unchanging center, what hardship could we not endure? 

We know that the foundation where heaven and earth settle and rest is both the Father's throne and the place where our bodies and hearts find rest. We understand that where the Father cannot hold us and we cannot hold the Father, there lies Satan. Now we must subdue that Satan. Centered on the Father, let our bodies and hearts start toward the world of peace and victory, and let us be granted to sing of the Father's glory on the day that world is realized. 

Whether we sleep or wake, eat or starve, let us not forget that we are the soldiers who must guard God's front line. Even if we are in the state of a hungry, thirsty, and sick wanderer, let us become those who can embrace each other, shed tears, comfort, and share. Also, let us earnestly wish that they become a group that swears toward the Father in unity. May Your will be done according to the Father's desire, and may the counsel given bear fruit among them. We pray in Your name. Amen.

Jesus and Us Looking at Heaven and Earth
Matthew 26:1-
<Main Point> If one does not understand the inner suffering until the Messiah appears, they will have nothing to do with that Messiah. 

Jesus, feeling unworthy, could not pray to God as the Messiah. He prayed for forgiveness as a member of the betraying nation. Jesus must not be invaded by Satan. If He were to be invaded by Satan, He could not become the complete Messiah. Therefore, Jesus could not stand as the Son of God and died as a son of the Israelite nation. Jesus came as the Savior but died as a son of the Israelite nation. Jesus came as the Savior but worked as a sacrificial offering on behalf of the Israelite nation before He died. If He had been dignified as the Messiah, why would there be a need for resurrection? Jesus, looking at the earth, was solemn. Therefore, how furious must Jesus have been when He was slandered before Satan! 

When He said, "Not my will, but Yours be done," it shows that Jesus had His own will. Thus, He fought while carrying His will in His heart, adjusting to the circumstances of the Israelite nation. 

Jesus had to fulfill His own will. He came to unite the divided world through the love of parents, spouses, siblings, and children. Jesus, who took the place of sinful Israel, was the main character of historical repentance. 

Jesus became the historical offering and the offering of the age. 

Jesus has a heart that is blocked by the cross of the heart. He wandered among opposing groups to establish historical connections. 

Jacob, Moses, John the Baptist, and Jesus all went through wilderness experiences. The fight always takes place in the most difficult places. 

You all must be able to say that you are the ones who represent all the noble ancestors. 

4)
You Belong to the Father
<Main Point> We are at a significant turning point in the providential course. We are also in a position to connect the past, present, and future. There has been a long historical course until now, and today there are countless people living on this earth, as well as an infinite spiritual world. However, when looking at all of this, is there anything that God can joyfully accept? There is not a single thing that God can joyfully accept. 

Now God is searching for His beloved sons and daughters and desires to have them. Until now, you have not been the sons and daughters of God, but now you can stand as the sons and daughters of God. This is indeed good news. What you can be proud of is the fact that you can become the sons and daughters that God wants to find and have. 

Whose are you now? You are the unchanging Father's. Therefore, you must go toward the will that the Father desires. The more you recognize that there is a Father who has worked for 6,000 years to raise you, the more you become the eternal heirs of His heart. You become the representatives of the Father. You can only meet this Master again by walking that path. 

You must take pride in this. There are many people on this earth, but there are no sons and daughters who know the heart of God in any country. God is only seeking to conclude the providence through you. 

You are the sons and daughters of the Father, and thus the sons and daughters of this world. However, first, you are the sons and daughters representing this nation, so you must go out to your assigned regions and say, "The sons and daughters of the Father have come here," and you must be entrusted with the task of planting the sign of the heart here. You must do this. You must never think that you are alone just because you are by yourself. You must feel that the Father is always with you, whether you are working, eating, or sleeping. 

If you feel the Father's heart that makes you walk a path you do not want and act with a sense of shame so that you do not leave any worries for the Father, then you can go anywhere. The Father will never lead you to a place of ruin. Even if you die while walking the path of His will, you will become a great victor in heaven, and that will be inherited by your descendants. Therefore, if you live with the Father, feeling the circumstances in which He was hungry, naked, and rejected, you will not fall, no matter where you go or what difficulties you face. 

Your purpose is to conquer the world of Satan. You must never lose to Satan, no matter where you go. You must never lose in goodness or patience through the past, present, and future. Generally, one loses when they are close to death. However, we must cross the line of life and death. Thus, we must become victors. The same goes for work. 

Where are the sons and daughters of God in every corner of this land? They do not exist. Now you are the sons and daughters of the world. The goal is the world, but the first step is the nation. God will bless you only after removing Satan's slander. When that happens, you will become sons and daughters who can rule not just one town but heaven and earth. 

Always remember that you are never alone. Our Father has come through all difficulties. You must bring that Father into the garden of rest. Our going out to enlighten others is also to bring the Father. We must move forward until this world can welcome the Father. Only then can we become filial sons and daughters. 

God is searching for sons and daughters from the very front line. He is coming from the very end. God needs church members who have a spirit of the lowly. You must walk from the bottom of the nation. Look clearly at this world. The world situation revolves with the movements of heaven, so now you must have conviction. 

The Father is pioneering this path with a three-year term to make you the final victors and is training you. 

5)
Jesus Who Came as the Substance of Hope
<Main Point> When Jesus came to this earth, He came as the substance of God's overall hope. Although He was born in a stable, it was an unprecedented event in history. Until now, many babies have been born, but there are few who were born as pitifully as Jesus. However, Jesus was born inheriting the overall will of God. It was a shame that He was not welcomed with the utmost honor. 

God intended to resolve all historical grievances through Jesus. It is a lamentable matter that Jesus could not fulfill His purpose. Jesus was a being who could be both a joy and a sorrow to God. 

Jesus was someone who could not be exchanged for the whole world. It was not the angels who praised the baby wrapped in swaddling clothes lying in the manger, but they praised Him centered on God's hope. However, on earth, no one could bless Jesus from the hopeful perspective of heaven. The Eastern Magi, Anna, and Simeon were all the same. When heaven rejoices, the earth should rejoice, and when heaven mourns, the earth should mourn, but that was not the case on earth. 

Neither Joseph nor Mary felt sorry before heaven for Jesus's pitiful birth. Jesus was not blessed as the substance of the purpose from the moment of His birth. Therefore, today we must celebrate Jesus's birth instead of the Magi, shepherds, Anna, and Simeon. Otherwise, there is no meaning in celebrating today. 

Jesus had God's purpose, but He also had His own purpose. God's purpose was to inherit His will to Jesus, and Jesus's own purpose was to fulfill God's purpose through His life. Thus, Jesus had the mission to resolve the 4,000 years of sinful history internally and also had an external mission to fulfill. 

Today, we must do what can fulfill and celebrate God's historical purpose and Jesus's life purpose. However, we have not yet done so. We have not been able to say, "We have accomplished everything," while calling God our Father and humanity our family. In the position where we have not achieved this, we do not have the qualification to give complete congratulations to Jesus. Only those who can release the grievances of His life have the qualification to celebrate Him. You must now take on the providential mission of God and the purpose of Jesus's life. You must ask God to bless you for fulfilling the purpose of Jesus's life. 

We must fulfill God's will and Jesus's will. To achieve this, we must complete the mission that Jesus could not finish. Otherwise, there is no meaning in congratulating Him. Although the time, place, and customs may differ, God's purpose and Jesus's purpose cannot change. Jesus fought for this, and you must inherit it. Only by manifesting as the substance that fulfills that purpose can you become a historical being who can find the True Parents. 

If there had been children with substance before the True Parents, humanity's history would not have turned out this way. You must take on the mission that Jesus wanted to establish. You must keep in mind that you must replace Jesus's historical mission. 

You must make a significant promise today. You must have the conviction that the path you walk is the path of going out in place of Jesus and must reap the fruits of victory. Only then can God's purpose and Jesus's own purpose be fulfilled. If you know and act upon this fact, you will be able to achieve the final victory. I hope you keep this in mind as you go out. 

<Benediction> Heaven and earth, all peoples, all things, and the entire universe shall return under God's sovereignty. They shall return. They shall return. Amen. Amen. Amen. 

6)
Let Us Become the Representatives of the Father
John 17:1-12, 17:24-26
<Prayer> Until You come to this peninsula of three thousand ri, we acknowledge that Your history is stained with Your blood, sweat, and tears. 

O Father, who loves this pitiful nation among countless nations, please allow the day to come soon when we can reveal the heart that You love to all the world. 

We understand that choosing this nation, which has been pushed into a pitiful position, is part of Your great providential will, and we know that we must bring You before all people as our Father. 

We must realize once again at this time that the sorrowful Father is our Father, the suffering Father is our Father, and that Father who has held and wept over countless children who have fallen, bleeding and shedding tears as this nation walks through a difficult historical course is indeed our Father. 

You have personally opened the hands of love and life to find Your sons and daughters, and as the pioneer among pioneers, the King of pioneers, You have worked personally, yet today this thirty million nation does not know You. This nation should be one that anticipates the day to welcome You, yet it is not so. Please forgive us. 

We know well that this nation, called by the Father's will, has left a historical blemish throughout the ages. Today, as this nation reflects on its past, it should uphold Your heart even more, yet we find ourselves in a position where we cannot do so. Please forgive us. 

The more Your efforts to find this pitiful nation until the day You come are great, the more we feel unworthy before You. 

Father, since we have formed a bond of life over this pitiful nation, please work. Let this nation, which has been a pitiful nation before all humanity, be able to take pride in its suffering. Please allow the day to come soon when this nation, which could not rely on or take pride in anything on this earth, can take pride in being with heaven. 

Now, Your sons and daughters gathered here have understood this will and this mission, so please pioneer the path of restoration through them. Even if our blood and flesh are torn apart, we know that we must become living sacrifices to welcome the day of rest where we can offer up to the Father who has worked hard to find this nation in our generation. Today, we represent this nation, this world, heaven and earth, and the countless spirits who have fallen while walking the path of righteousness. We earnestly ask that You renew and resolve us at this time, Father. 

All things must sing with Your heart, and all creations must harmonize with Your heart. We know that for six thousand years, they have mourned and sighed, having lost their original positions and places due to human fall. 

Even until this time, You have not lost the heart of restoration and have fought, endured, and persevered even in sorrowful and difficult places to fulfill the day of wish fulfillment. 

Now, as we serve the Father, we must build a mountain of peace, love, and joy from our hearts. However, even now, there is evil before us.
There are many Satans, and environmentally it is not permissible for that to happen. However, we understand that we have the responsibility to connect the entire universe by establishing an environmental stage in our lives, where our ancestors can glorify and rejoice before the Father from our hearts. We ask that those of us gathered here today examine ourselves to see if we are in a position to welcome you without hesitation when you personally appear and call us, Father. How much have you longed for such sons and daughters? How eagerly have you awaited for these sons and daughters to bow their heads and receive blessings before you?

Today, allow us to truly embrace you as our Father. And we earnestly hope and wish that this time, with you present here, will be a moment suitable for all of heaven and earth to offer songs of glory.

The labor of the Father is immeasurable. Many ancestors have come to fulfill your will, but they have disappeared as a chapter in history without resolving the sorrow of the fall. When they realize that they are still waiting for the day of resolution from the heavenly realm, watching this insignificant group on earth, we cannot help but feel the weight of our responsibility.

Today, let us realize once again that we are not here just for ourselves. Centered on our own selves, let us understand that heaven and earth are connected, and that we are linked with our ancestors in the heavenly realm, our descendants to come, and our family members in the present.

Human history is a history of restoration through indemnity, and we understand that we have a historical responsibility to establish conditions for resolution and to restore. If we fail today, it will become a sorrow for heaven, a sorrow for this age, and a sorrow for the future.

We realize that our position is the same as that of Adam and Eve standing before God. From this year onward, may we be able to self-verify before the Father and become sons and daughters who can be offered to the Father with the new will of the Father.

Let us be the representatives of the Father. Thus, by resolving the grievances of our ancestors and the many nations of this age, may we prepare a foundation that will allow countless descendants to be embraced as beloved sons and daughters of the Father. We earnestly hope that this time will be a morning where we can establish new traces and foundations that can illuminate this period.

Father, at this time, there are over a thousand family members gathered across South Korea. Father, while many fight and give up everything for their own happiness in this age, we know that there are few who fight and give up everything for the day of your rest. However, your young sons and daughters are gathered in various places, fighting to stand closer to your heart, which is striving to conclude a global mission.

Are there family members who are lying down in bed, shedding tears at this time? Father, please be with them. You are the Father who leads the lonely, and we know you are with them in such places, and when they are about to fall, you encourage them. Therefore, we believe you will be with us at this time. Please guide us and hold us.

Allow us to be pioneers who can lead this nation, which does not know where to go, into the embrace of the Father by fulfilling the new mission and responsibility we must bear. We earnestly hope and wish that we can become your sons and daughters who bear the priestly responsibility to resolve even a part of your heart that is filled with deep sorrow. In this place where your sons and daughters are gathered, Father, please appear personally, give us your commands, protect us, strengthen us, and grant us wisdom.

You know that there are family members overseas who are shedding tears and praying while longing for this one hour.
