Today, we who are gathered here ask that this day be a time of new beginnings with a renewed determination and resolution. We will strive to take responsibility for all remaining purposes, so we ask that you entrust them to us. May everything be fulfilled among us. We pray in your name. Amen.

<Words> The theme we must carry as our slogan for this year is "Let us be the representatives of the Father." I will speak on this theme.

You have, of course, been doing this until now, but especially for this year, I hope you will personally experience being the representatives of the Father.

God and the relationship with humanity and the fall
God created the earth as the counterpart to heaven and created our human ancestors as the substantial object representing Himself. He created humanity in His image and, symbolically, created all things first in the image of humanity. All creatures, broadly speaking, are one entity, and narrowly speaking, they are all created as representatives of God.

To stand in the position of a representative, we must first clarify the center. In other words, if we are representatives of God, we must clarify who God is and what our relationship with Him is.

What is the original relationship between God and us? We must not forget that we are one. God and I are in an inseparable relationship. If heaven is the head, we are the body; if heaven is the body, we are the limbs. God is in a position that is inseparable from us.

The fact that we, who should be in such a position, are unable to become one with God is the fall, and not living as one with that unity is also the fall.

Therefore, from the day humanity fell, God has been longing for a being who can manifest the central value of supreme goodness before all creation, holding the will of restoration. The absence of such a being has become an element of lament. Thus, we must understand that God has carried out a providence, sacrificing many beloved children to bring fallen humanity into a position where they can be inseparably one with God in heart and body.

What must become one to achieve this unity? First, the will must become one; second, the circumstances must become one; and third, the hearts must become one. In other words, when heaven rejoices, I must rejoice; when heaven is sad, I must be sad; when heaven moves, I must move; when heaven is still, I must also be still. Thus, the heart, circumstances, and will must all become one.

If we humans had a point of agreement in heart, circumstances, and will with God, we would have no sorrow. This is because when the heavens and earth were created, no being was created with the purpose of sorrow. God is good, and therefore, the purpose of His creation is also good. Since goodness encompasses satisfaction, happiness, and joy, if humanity had not fallen, we would not have been able to experience sorrow. Even if we entered a place of pain and difficulty, it could serve as a condition to deepen the alignment of our hearts, circumstances, and will with the deeper heart of the Father, but it could not be a condition to separate us.

Thus, if humanity had not fallen and had a point of agreement with God's heart, circumstances, and will, then God would move for the overall purpose and we would inevitably feel everything that God perceives for the overall ideal. If that had been the case, even if our individual living environment is extremely narrow, we could have lived feeling everything from a position that represents heaven and earth.

All emotions we experience in relation to all things and people are connected and move through heaven and earth. In such places, only God's absolute goodness, which is exceedingly high, deep, and wide, cannot help but connect and move with us.

However, because humanity fell, all of this was severed. And we humans did not know what the will of heaven was, nor did we know what it meant to live with heaven. We fell into a position that has no relation to the heart that can eternally sing with heaven and determine an eternal bond with heaven.

Therefore, fallen humanity must seek hope and search for ideals. The purpose of this is to become one. Furthermore, the purpose of wanting to communicate circumstances in interpersonal relationships is also to become one. The heart resolved around true goodness for the sake of a true purpose is eternally unchanging and cannot be moved by anyone. If such a decisive resolution had been established, we would not be living in such difficult and struggling circumstances today.

However, because we lost that standard due to the fall, countless humans are struggling. Because of the responsibility and mission that remain for humanity to unite with heaven, we are placed in a position where we cannot avoid the difficult path. Therefore, we must continue to struggle until the day we can emotionally unite with heaven.

The final path humanity must take
So, did heaven leave humanity in such a position? No, it did not. Originally, God created humanity as His own sons and daughters. Even though humanity fell and lost that value and connection, He did not abandon us. We must understand that God has worked tirelessly to elevate humanity back to the original standard of heart and to re-establish that value and connection.

Heaven has worked to give hope to humanity that had no hope. Therefore, it has manifested the hope of one day in the scriptures. It has promised the hope of the day when we can welcome the returning Lord and a new historical world, pushing us toward that day.

Even if many nations are in different circumstances, heaven has worked infinitely to lead them toward one ideal and one world of hope. Moreover, it has not left the differences in traditions, nationalities, and living circumstances as they are but has worked to establish a global environment where humans can communicate with one another.

Not only that, but God has also brought humanity to a place where we can share hope, share circumstances, and where heaven, earth, God, and humanity can hold hands and communicate in heart.

Then, what is the final path we must take? It is to become one with God. This is what Jesus emphasized when He was in a position to leave behind His beloved disciples: "Become one!" Become one! But who should we first become one with? He did not insist that brothers become one with each other. His wish was for us to become one with God as He is one with us, and for us to become one with each other.

If we are to become one, where should we begin? It is not just in our daily lives. From the moment we are born until we die, our goals are the same. Our paths are the same. They cannot be different. From the day we are born, the path we take in life is the same. We carry our lives and struggle along our life paths, but the destination we are all heading toward is the same. Since we started from the Father, we must go to the Father.

What must we do while we go? We must work as representatives of the Father, doing the Father's work and loving all things created by the Father in place of the Father. Since we started from the Father, we must also conclude with the Father, and we must go until we are connected with the heart of the Father. This is the path we must take. The beginning is the Father, and the end is also the Father. That is why He is called the Alpha and the Omega. Since the beginning is one, the end must also be one. This means that our circumstances must connect, and our wills must be the same. Otherwise, we cannot possibly become one.

To become representatives of God
Now, with such a great will placed before us in this time of global chaos, we must reflect once more on what the original central goal was when God created humanity. The Father and we are one. Heaven and earth are one. They are not two. Therefore, we must recognize that we are in an inevitable position where we must become one before one central purpose, whether we live or die. If there are any circumstances or hearts that can connect, then to achieve that purpose, our wills, circumstances, and hearts must be the same. Otherwise, we cannot fully realize that purpose.

If God has the responsibility to lead fallen humanity to a garden of hope where circumstances can connect and hearts can unite, then for humanity standing in a position to become one with God, the will must also be one. It cannot be two. It must be God's will and my will, God's circumstances and my circumstances, God's heart and my heart. Unless you personally experience this and stand in such a position, you cannot be a representative. To be a representative, you must become one. If you do not become one, you cannot be a representative. Therefore, the goal fallen humanity must pursue is to become one with God. What are the necessary conditions for unity? Our hopes must be the same, our circumstances must be the same, and furthermore, we must establish a point of emotional unity. Otherwise, fallen humanity cannot achieve oneness with God.

Those of you present here have understood what the will is. You have understood what the purpose we must pursue is. You have understood what the purpose humanity must pursue today is. You have understood what the purpose this humanity hopes for is, and what each individual must hold as their purpose. You have also understood what kind of circumstances we must have. Furthermore, you have understood what kind of heart we must possess.

So, how can we ensure that our circumstances can be the same, our hopes can be the same, and our hearts can be the same? We must be able to recognize that God acknowledges us as His sons and daughters, and we must also acknowledge ourselves as God's sons and daughters. Moreover, we must reach a place where we can recognize that all things created before heaven and earth are undoubtedly children of heaven.
You must become a child. Before that, we cannot stand as representatives of heaven.  
We humans must become one with God. After that, you must feel that God is our Father, God is the center of our hearts, and God is one body that can be with me forever. Originally, humans were born centered on God, so we must understand that God Himself is our Father, and that this Father created Adam and Eve, who are our human ancestors.  
Now, fallen humanity is in the process of knowing God's will, understanding God's circumstances, and seeking God. No matter how devout a believer may be, until now, they have not known God's heart. Even if they claim to believe well, they have only known a part of God's circumstances. They did not know the whole situation. They knew God's will but did not know the overall will.  
What remains in the end is God's heart, and to reach this place of heart, you must be able to say, "You are our Father, and I am Your son." For fallen humanity to advance to such a position, it is essential to establish a connection with the True Parents. The ones who came to establish this connection with the True Parents are Jesus and the Holy Spirit.  
To become one with God, Jesus is the representative of the unfallen human ancestor, the True Adam, and the Holy Spirit came as his unfallen counterpart, working hard to elevate humanity to a position where we can share hope, circumstances, and heart.  
Until now, the history of heaven has been a history that leads to a position where we can share the heart of the parents, which is why angels and spirits in the spirit world could not cooperate. When it comes to the heart issue, it is essential to pass through the heart of the parents, which remains with fallen humanity. Therefore, to resolve this heart issue, we must go through the connection of father and son centered on the parents.  
To connect to God's heart, we must go through the heart of the True Parents through Jesus and the Holy Spirit.  
Although you have been practicing your faith for many years, you have not known who Jesus is or who the Holy Spirit is. Jesus and the Holy Spirit are the True Parents of humanity. Without passing through the heart of these True Parents, we cannot advance to the position of God's heart.  
Thus, we must be united with God. For fallen humanity to be united with God, we must be united with the True Parents. And to be united with the True Parents, who must we be united with? We must be united with our siblings.  
If humanity had not fallen, we would have been united with God, and the sons and daughters born there would have been united with God's heart, united with the heart of the True Parents, and united with the heart of true siblings. However, due to the fall, we have become disconnected.  
To be united with the heart of the True Parents, we must be united with our true siblings, and after being united with our true siblings, we must also be united with the True Family and the True Nation. Just as humanity spread from the human ancestors Adam and Eve to families, tribes, nations, and the world, we must stand in a position to rise back up.  
Now, for us in such a position to ultimately become one with God, we must align our hopes, circumstances, and hearts. To do this, we must develop today's world into a time of global hope, a time of global circumstances, and a time of global heart. Therefore, countless people must unite under one hope, one ideology. They must also connect through one circumstance. Furthermore, what must connect on the foundation where one hope and one circumstance can resonate? The heart must resonate.  
What I love most is not just myself but also everyone, and that nation, and furthermore, all of humanity around the world must love, and heaven and earth, and all things must love. What is that? It is not one's own beloved children, nor spouse, nor parents. It is God.  
The central subject of the heart that can root itself in the most loving heart, which no one can move, change, or take away, is God.  
There is no national gap in loving this God. There is no traditional gap. There is a subject that transcends nations, transcends traditions, and transcends environments, which all people can love in common, and that is God.  
Today, because humanity does not know what kind of being God is and does not know the relationship between God and themselves, they stand in a position where they do not love God. However, if they come to know this relationship and enter into a position of forming this connection, they cannot help but love God. Therefore, God is working to establish a place of unity.

However, this world cannot be governed by democracy nor by communism. Ultimately, it must be united under a better ideology. In the past, it took several years for events that occurred in Korea to be known worldwide. Any circumstance that takes on a global nature must resonate with a certain ideological heart because all of humanity must live under the same circumstances.

The world is on a path that can meet the time of hope, and it is also on a path that can meet the time of circumstances, but what concludes this is the heart. To connect with this heart, what path must we take? We cannot connect with just any circumstance. We cannot connect with just any ideology or hope. To connect with this, we must go through the door of parents. We must pass through this standard of parents.  
The day that God promised at the end is the Day of Parents. It is the day we can welcome the True Parents. In other words, it is the day when countless humanity on this earth, who lost their parents due to the fall, can once again meet their original parents and fulfill God's blessing.  
When humanity sets a goal for restoration and moves toward God, the inevitable condition is that it must go through the door of parents. Before passing through the door of parents, we cannot connect our hearts.  
To become one, we must have the same will, the same circumstances, and the same heart. If God has worked throughout history to make all of humanity one today, then this humanity must be led to a unified world.  
Now the world is divided into two factions fighting against each other, which means the time to become one is near. It has become a time when significant global circumstances are connecting with our circumstances. Although the conditions for circumstances and hope to resonate globally have been established, the time to resonate in heart has not yet come. To connect this, we must know God's heart and form a relationship with God's heart, and the mediator that connects this is the True Parents. They have known how this time is unfolding and how the circumstances of that nation are developing, but they have not known anything about the heart. They have been completely in the dark about God's heart.  
What must ultimately be resolved? It is the heart issue. To resolve this, each of us must have a bridge to the True Parents. We must go through the True Parents.

Whether you like it or not, history will go through such a process. No matter how much you deny it, you cannot escape the fate of going through that process.  
Fulfilling the unity of hope, unity of circumstances, unity of heart, and unity of ideology  
Fallen humanity must inevitably go through the path of restoration. This is not a position where we can live happily on this earth. This earth is a place we pass through.  
There is a place we must go, and that place is the position that represents God's will, the position that represents God's heart, and the position that represents God's circumstances. Only by going to that place can you unload your burdens and take a position where you can proudly proclaim the value of humanity before all things in heaven and earth; otherwise, you cannot remain anywhere. This mission to walk that path remains before us today.  
If we know what the Father's will is and what the Father's circumstances are, we must connect that will and those circumstances to our own will and circumstances. The Father's will is to achieve the purpose of creation, and the Father's circumstances are to engage in a fierce battle against Satan in this fallen world. We must understand that we are in such a bloody situation.  
If we escape from this place of suffering and go to a place of rest, God cannot love us. He cannot truly love us. When the sons and daughters who have received God's love are being violated before Satan and being trampled by the wicked, God wanted to love us.  
When God loves once, that love is eternal, and once God forms a heartistic connection, no one can move away from it. To prepare that place, He has driven humanity through various hardships and adversities until now. We must understand that He is still leading us toward that place.  
If we understand that the place where God can freely form a heartistic connection has not yet been established, we must first resolve God's circumstances. If there is a sad situation, we must take the place of that sadness and be joyful in that sad place. Even if the path for the Father's will is a path of death, you must be able to be grateful in that place. Otherwise, you cannot possibly transfer the Father's will to your own will.  
Through this process, only after passing through this fallen world will the time come when we can eternally and unchangingly live with all things, singing praises to the Father centered on God's eternal love. We must surely advance to that place.  
Therefore, we must struggle. We must ask ourselves whether we can carry out the unity of hope, unity of circumstances, unity of heart, and unity of ideology. We must understand that without going through this process, we cannot claim to be representatives of God.  
When Jesus came to this earth and was opposed by the Israelite people and crucified, he came as a representative of God on earth. The point that the Father's will is my will, the Father's circumstances are my circumstances, and the Father's heart is my heart has not changed.  
Can you stand before heaven and claim yourself?  
Today is the first day of 1961 and the first Sunday. Do you believe you stand confidently before heaven? Can you claim to be a representative who can stand in a position of responsibility and mission before heaven as one called by heaven? You must think deeply about this. What is the will and hope you hold in your heart? Whose circumstances are the circumstances you are in? If the will you hold is your own will, then it has no relation to the Father. If the circumstances you are in are your own circumstances, then they have no relation to the Father. We must have a point of unity with heaven's will and circumstances. Until that unity is achieved, we cannot have a unity of heart.  
God wants to establish an eternal and inseparable relationship with you, to love you and sing with you, no matter what path of suffering or difficult environment you go through. That is the heart of the Father. When you realize that this purpose has not yet been fulfilled on this earth and in this world, you must make a new determination and resolution today.  
You must become one with God, but you have not yet achieved that unity. How are the will you hold and the circumstances you are in?  
Even if there are joyful things, you must rejoice centered on the will; even if there are sad things, you must mourn centered on the will; even if there are grievances or anger, if there is someone who feels those emotions centered on the will, then that person is undoubtedly a son or daughter of heaven, even if they live in the world of Satan on earth.  
You have followed the will until now. That will has been growing larger as time goes on. The circumstances have become more complicated as time goes on. The heart has become more earnest and fervent as time goes on. As the time approaches, it deepens and strengthens.  
If you understand that this is the heart and will of heaven that has been coming, then your own will must also become more earnest as the Father's will, and the circumstances you face must also be connected to the Father's deeper circumstances. When the will and circumstances connect, the heart issue will inevitably connect.  
Even if I am in a pitiful and unjust position, the Father must not be in such a position. The Father must not be in such an environment. This heart must be deeply felt. Only then does the heart connect from there. Therefore, you must make a new determination this morning.  
Men and women are the embodiments of God's masculine and feminine qualities.  
We are the representatives of our Father and the representatives of the coming True Parents. Men are the embodiment of the Father, and women are the embodiment of the Mother. In other words, God exists as the central subject of the duality of masculine and feminine qualities, so men are born to represent God's masculine qualities, and women are born to represent God's feminine qualities.  
In essence, our individual beings have been the members of the True Parents since birth. Therefore, Jesus also said, "I am the vine, and you are the branches." (John 15:5) Men are the members of the Father, and women are the members of the Mother. Men are the embodiment of the Father.
God, women are the embodiment of their mothers. Therefore, if God sees that they can indeed be the embodiment of their fathers and the embodiment of their mothers, no matter how far apart they may be, there must be God's love present there. For those who live centered on the circumstances and will of their father, God's heart naturally connects with them. You must deeply feel that you are in such an environment this year.

God's will is to come to this earth. The will that has come to you today is not for each individual but for the world. The circumstances are also not meant to be centered on individual situations. Those circumstances are meant for all people to hold hands and live joyfully together. You must understand that this heart can also connect everyone with a shared purpose. Only when this happens can we be happy.

No matter how much you cry, shout, and make a fuss about what the will or heart is, there is nothing greater than the father's will, nothing greater than the father's circumstances, and nothing greater than the father's heart. Therefore, you must stand in such a position and manage your environment.

God's will is for the world.

What will you do about today's environment that does not align with the will? What will you do about this will? Will you abandon it, or will you establish the will and organize the environment to submit to it? The same applies to circumstances and hearts. Unless there is an environmental stage where if I am happy, they are happy too, and if I am sad, they are sad too, the will of heaven cannot be fulfilled. You should not be bound by your own circumstances but must be able to connect with the will and circumstances of heaven.

We must naturally subdue Satan.

God's purpose is to reclaim fallen humanity and to naturally subdue Satan. To unite with such God, we must not seek comfort. We must go to places where Satan is and to those who do not know heaven. If we cannot do this, neither God's will nor God's circumstances can become ours. The time to fulfill a global mission is approaching us.

To subdue Satan, we must eliminate the conditions for accusation. We must march for this purpose. We must go to places where others do not want to go and do what others do not want to do.

Let us become the representatives of the father.

Now that we understand the will and circumstances, we must place the father behind us and take the lead. We must be able to say to the father coming to Korea, "Please rest assured about Korea." Even in our actions, we must act on a global stage. To do this, we must organize the national environment and go to our fellow countrymen who are crying with the will of heaven in the remaining two years. We must go to more difficult places than they are in and ask, "Please give me the strength with which you fought." We must go to difficult places rather than good places to receive blessings. Whether we are good or bad, we must unite.

To step over the difficult environment that collapses at the end, we must go through all experiences. To advance to the position of the father's heart, to receive the father's love, we must subdue Satan, who caused the fall of humanity, and be recognized as heavenly sons and daughters from Satan. Otherwise, blessings will not be granted.

The reason for placing sons and daughters in the place of suffering.

The way to indemnify the history of 6,000 years of struggle at once is to place God's beloved sons and daughters in the place of suffering and then mercilessly drive them. The degree to which one has participated in the place of suffering determines the recognition of heaven. Heaven blesses those who take responsibility for difficult and painful tasks.

Behold, the Lamb of God, who takes away the sin of the world. (John 1:29)

Those who are driven before millions will receive the blessings of millions; those who are driven before humanity will receive the blessings of humanity; and those who are driven before heaven and earth will receive the blessings of heaven and earth. Therefore, any responsible person must be driven mercilessly. This is to fulfill the will.

We must all go the path that others cannot go. If we are loyal and devoted in places where everyone does not want to go, we cannot help but be blessed. The seven-year great tribulation is to give a century of blessings.

We are the advance guard. The ones behind us should be able to walk a smooth path because of us. We must prepare for this work and prepare to shorten that day. Until now, the Father, the Son, and the Holy Spirit have been working. It is regrettable that until now, there has been no time when we worked in the name of humanity. It is a sad fact that we have worked in the names of the Father, the Son, and the Holy Spirit.

From now on, you must have the time to work in your own name. You must be able to subdue Satan without prayer and without the cooperation of God. Only such a person can become the ancestor of the new era. Satan also caused humanity to fall without the cooperation of God.

To independently take responsibility and fulfill the will, we must first know God. We must know the historical God, the God of the times, and the future God, and then attack Satan to make him unable to move.

Now is the time to mobilize the spirits of the spirit world without prayer. Even Satan and wicked people must be made to bow their heads, saying, "Only you can do this."

Those who take responsibility must go out to the place of suffering. Thus, as the representatives of God, they must fight well, win, and receive blessings. Only then can we finally reach the point of heart's return. There, the ideal of oneness is completed.

… You must not die with a heart full of regret saying, "If only I had done it." Those who can say, "I have given my utmost sincerity," are those who live eternal lives. Even if countless people do not recognize you, if you can say, "You alone will recognize me," you will become the greatest victor in the path of life.

The time to draw near to the Father.

Religion is forming a global shape.

The heart of the Father toward Abraham, Moses, and Jesus remains. Therefore, He can judge those who betrayed such predecessors. Judgment is done with heart.

To be a filial son, one must become the representative of the Father. When Mary Magdalene tried to touch the resurrected Jesus with a joyful heart, Jesus rejected her. Why was that? Unless we have a heart greater than Mary Magdalene's, we cannot rejoice and harmonize with the Lord. We must become the neighbors of the poor. The restoration providence has been built upon the backs of the poor.

The reason Jesus died on Golgotha was to fill the skull place with the bones of goodness.

Be the final victor.
<Summary of the message> This summer, report the chosen evangelism areas. Before leaving for a nationwide tour, I plan to arrange the evangelism areas. This year, we must produce more than 1,500 to 2,000 area leaders. Prepare from now on.

Limit the evangelism costs.

If we leave sadness before God during this period or fail to fulfill our heavenly mission, it will become a regret for eternity and a source of shame. The teacher has planned for this work for decades.

After the three-year evangelism period ends, blessings will be given. Rejoice infinitely in the historical benefits of being able to participate in evangelism. This is something to boast about for eternity. Even if you go out with a cane, you must see the mountains and rivers and shed tears. If a parent cannot present their child in such a position, it will leave a regret for eternity.

The responsibility of the members at the headquarters is significant.

You must become qualified to speak before this nation.

During this three-year period, rearm yourselves with the Principle and heart.

To become the final victor, you must endure and withstand all difficulties. God's heart must penetrate to the bone. After the three-year period, the first, second, and third plans will be implemented.

Why must we do such things? Because there is heaven and earth, there are people, and there are hearts and bodies. However, due to the fall, heaven and earth, people and people, hearts and bodies are separated from each other. God's providence is to unite these.

You must elevate your value compared to the prophets and sages.

The teacher has devoted more effort than any person who has been loyal before God in history.

The teacher has not commanded until now. However, now we must command. We must bear the enormous mission of whether or not to turn the historical focus around, so the teacher cannot help but command. Therefore, the teacher's resolve in commanding is solemn.

Do not respect the teacher's individual self. Love the will. The will of God that must be restored, that is, the father's will, must not change. However, until now, this will has not been established.

Until now, what God has desired was to establish a standard of heart. Therefore, He has worked hard to bear the alpha heart with the omega heart. In other words, He has labored to determine the substance of the heart. However, Israel has changed with the times.

God takes out the person who is most loved in the satanic world, the person who is most loyal in the satanic world. The alpha heart must be tied to the omega heart with God.

What kind of person is a good person, a person who will go to heaven? It is a person who is unchanging, the same from the beginning to the end. The one who comes as the substance of the heart of good people, the culmination of the heart, is the Messiah. Only such a Messiah, the subject of the heart representing God, has the right to judge heaven and earth.

Jesus had a deep desire to bless individuals, families, and nations. However, He left without establishing a connection of heart. The teacher has also cried out for three years centered on this heart issue. To establish this connection of heart, many sincere hearts must come forth.

You must understand how precious the value that connects with the heart is. If you lose this standard of heart, it will be difficult to find it again.

Not only did Jesus pray, but God also prayed. He wished for His desire to be fulfilled, that is, to replace the heart of creation with substance.

Be the final victor.

Until now, there have been people who lived looking forward to hope, but today is the day of hope, so heaven and earth, rejoice! No one has shouted this. Jesus also said that the kingdom of heaven was near.

Those who move according to the word are infinitely happy. Why? Because until now, heaven and earth were not theirs, but from now on, if they live according to the word, heaven and earth will be theirs, and humanity will become one family.

The teacher has prayed countless times for this mobilization. Yet, I am at peace because I believe in myself, believe in God, and believe in you. A filial son can have a filial son, and a loyal person can have a loyal person.

While all sorts of people may act, the final victor is one person. We must appeal to the heart. If one is moved here, it is unchanging.

Mobilize everyone, regardless of whether they are knowledgeable or not, young or old. The blessing is determined during the fight.

The teacher has not lived a single day in peace for 40 years. However, from now on, because the standard of heart has been resolved, it is okay even if I am struck by lightning.

It cannot be based on the heart standard of friends. It must be based on the heart standard of parents. The standards of children and spouses must be established through the standards of parents.

Since the beginning of last year, we have entered a significant year. Therefore, I have told you to do the best work of your life.

Now, we have reached a point where we can bear the name of the True Father in place of heaven and earth.

The substance of the desires of God, Adam, and Eve is children. God intended to establish the full authority of heart through the descendants of Adam, not Adam himself. This is precisely that time. Therefore, we must establish children. It must be by the lunar calendar until next April. Until now, we could say that heaven is our heaven, the earth is our earth, and humanity is our humanity in the created world, but we could not boast before the Father. However, now we can boast before God.

Because we have a Father who represents heaven, a Mother who represents the earth, and one who represents all humanity. Therefore, we can say, "Please bless us. Satan, retreat from here."

The entire spirit world is forming the day of the son when it can be mobilized. If you understand this, you will weep.

For whom will you suffer?

Father—East, Mother—West, Son—South, you—North. In the past, Satan was in the north. Now you must push Satan away. After that, you must face the relative son in the south.

The formula for going to heaven is simple. It is enough to have the condition of having loved heaven and earth. We must suffer for this. Until now, no one has truly worked.

God never suffers loss. The teacher found you at the cost of abandoning parents, siblings, and children for this path. The teacher has loved you more than parents, siblings, and children. You must also love the teacher more than parents, siblings, and children.

How many prophets and sages have fallen to fulfill God's will until now? What kind of attitude should you have? From now on, it is a time of prayer. You are spending a solemn time now.

Overall, you are Abel, and the world is Cain, but internally, God...
The son of God is Abel, and you are Cain. If the teacher uses the secret method of fighting against Satan, there will be no one left standing. Now is the time to unite. To become a companion of the heart, one must endure hardships. Your pride is to love heaven on behalf of your father, to love the earth on behalf of your mother, and to love humanity on behalf of the son who can embrace God and dance. By doing so, even the spirits who died unjustly will bow their heads toward the earth in shame.

Until now, we have worked for the resolution of the Triune God. However, from now on, we must work for the resolution of the historical figures who have labored for the sake of God's will. Therefore, you should establish conditions for blessings and dedicate yourselves with sincerity and loyalty. Starting tomorrow (the 23rd) until the teacher returns, bathe and pray every night. This will be the last tour with such significance. Even if it’s just a meal, prepare it with sincerity and live harmoniously to become the final victors.

It seems that the family has not prepared for this tour. No one has discussed the cost of the tour. Until the time when the teacher is expected to speak in the region, do not sleep late and each of you should exert yourselves sincerely.
