Become a loyal subject, filial child, and virtuous woman of God.

<Summary of the Message> When the heart becomes earnest, the surroundings will move. Why do the surroundings move? Until now, they have not moved because the direction of the heart was wrong. Now, the emotional standard must be at a 90-degree angle with God. The most urgent problem for all humanity is to establish a foundation with an ideological direction. The person who establishes such a position and moves forward without changing is the most frightening.

God's sorrow after the fall of humanity was due to the severing of the firm connection of love. True heart, true love, and true emotion must all be established in earnest places. I am grateful for the prayers offered to establish emotional connections over the past week. What I felt during the four-day tour was that while there have been many loyal subjects, filial children, and virtuous women for kings historically, there have been none for God's will. However, we are different today. They all dedicated themselves for the liberation of freedom based on earthly standards. They may have been subjects of concern before God, but they could not be subjects of comfort or joy.

So far, there has been no one whom God has boasted about as a loyal subject, filial child, or virtuous woman.

January 29, 1961 (Sunday) night worship, at the former headquarters church.
* This message is organized from notes recorded by former Chairman Yoo Kwang-ryeol of the Association, and the title was added by the editor.

Becoming a loyal subject, filial child, and virtuous woman before God is the way of humanity, but there has been no such person. While there may have been such individuals for kings and parents, there has been none before God. How much has God longed for the loyal subjects, filial children, and virtuous women of the world to become loyal subjects, filial children, and virtuous women for Him?

God wants to care for, long for, love, and see us. He wants to do everything. There is nothing that God does not want to do. My smile and satisfaction must be in unity with God. Going out for God without caring for oneself is the path of faith and the path of virtue.

Everything of humanity is in opposition to God. All people on earth were shameful beings before the heavenly kingdom. Our hope is to give and receive, to move, to sleep and wake, and to eat in a way that pleases God. No human dares to step forward and assure God. Many have revered God until now, but not a single person has claimed to be without shame.

There is a difference between good and bad. If one goes down the path that humanity likes, the way will be blocked, but if one goes down the path that is disliked, they will meet God; this is the path of religion. Are your features something that God can boast about? Neither spirits nor earthly saints are in the position that God desires.

Ask! And it will be given to you... This biblical verse does not mean to ask humans. It means to first ask God. The Lord has advised us because this center is established. The biblical commands to refrain from or to do something are infused with God's essence.

God longs for us. What kind of person does God seek? He seeks those who seek Him on earth. He seeks those who search, knock, and ask infinitely. God has not changed before or after the fall of humanity. When He left humanity, He left with tears, and when He comes to us, He comes with tears. Therefore, those who seek God must go with tears.

God and humanity cannot meet without suffering, weeping, and tears. Until now, human actions have been in opposition to God's position. What kind of subject will you be before God? You must become one who has a desperate heart that bows down and sheds tears.

When will the father release his heart? When the son or daughter who says, "Your pain, circumstances, and heart are mine," is born, it will be released. In a place where there is nowhere to turn, one can establish a connection of heart with God.

We must diligently cross the remaining path. Even if we lack strength, we must go. We must be prepared even if it is with friends or neighbors. Your position can be determined by yourselves. You must pledge to do as you wish, even if it seems like you are not aware of it. What was the standard of the son whom God wanted to see and love? Who was the one who could inherit the heavenly authority?

After the resurrection, Jesus rejected Mary. God placed a veil over the temple for the people of Israel. There was a reason why God had to do so. Even if one is oppressed, bullied, and chased a thousand or ten thousand times, they must say, "Thank you." Since humanity has been a historical enemy, they must have a sense of shame before God. When appearing before God, one must feel the shame of their body and features.

It is normal to accept the relationship with God even in a position of shame and disgrace for being expelled from God. The one who died to cover the shame of all people is the Lord. One cannot say, "I have done enough with my own achievements." There are those who can boast and those who can rejoice, but there is only God.

Who is the one who seeks and longs for God's blood-stained hand? Who is the one who can inherit God's heavenly authority? You must not become someone who is insignificant. Whether you become a people or a son, you must become one.

If you are to boast, it should be of your imperfect appearance, but you must say that you will not be bound by any conditions. God wants to instill emotions in your blood and flesh. When you fall, do not mourn for your body falling, but rather mourn for God who cried with blood and tears.

Desire to be seen before God. Do not seek approval from the teacher. Our path is a narrow one. You must not speak or gesture to those beside you. The teacher has a conviction. He has the confidence to do anything. Do you have such conviction?

A leader must establish connections not in a place of joy but in a place of sorrow and tears. You must know what God wants to see, long for, and seek. You must not only know it with words.

The teacher has been truly miserable until he found this path. It is not for himself. He had to come forth despite feeling ashamed to present his limbs and everything before God. In such a position, God wishes to show mercy and grant blessings.

Do not mock with your heart, do not glance with your eyes, and do not defile the sacred things with your hands; such people should not participate in this path. If the teacher does not drink, then drinkers cannot attend, and if the teacher does not smoke, then smokers cannot attend.

There are dozens of conditions to be upheld, but I will not mention them. Those who lack the strength to be loyal to the will for more than three years should not participate. Those who cannot assure that they can pass on their possessions to their descendants as a will should also not participate.

Wash away all conditions of past regrets and return to the position of a child. A child has no self. Forget the consciousness of self and the concept of possession. If you go against what is taught here at this time, it will remain as a condition of your life and you will receive accusations from Satan. You may have to go through the historical course of the teacher's journey—the process of retribution that must be established as a condition of one-on-one indemnity.

Become the most abandoned among the orphans. This time, those aged 18 to 60 must participate in evangelism.

<On the Infant Dedication Ceremony> 
<Summary of the Message> God's providence begins with the external. I blessed the three sons of faith, but I could not do so for Seongjin. The more I treat him well while seeking the three sons of faith, the more unfortunate he becomes. Today is the day to dedicate the baby to God. Last year, we discussed an important matter, and today, with the conclusion of the 40-day evangelism, that matter comes to an end.

Daughters are dedicated on the seventh day after birth, and sons on the eighth day. At this time, we must stand on the standard of having loved our children in the past. In fact, anyone must set the condition that they have loved someone other than their own child. The meaning of the saying that a woman in labor has anger is found here.

Going out for enlightenment is to establish emotional connections. When a person who participated with joy loses the joy of the event due to their own sorrow, they are allowed to participate under the condition that each takes responsibility. Therefore, even if they fall away, they will not receive accusations from Satan.

Today's ceremony is on behalf of women. Men can expect to stand because of Seongjin, but there will also be a ceremony on behalf of men. The foundation must be built with blood, sweat, and tears. This is true in the world of Satan, but it is also true in the heavenly world. Even if I go to prison for doing something wrong, I will not regret it because I did it with sincerity.

When a virtuous person comes, I sacrificed everything for him. This is to treat such a virtuous person well. When he bears witness, the position will be reversed.
is divided into factions. Here, what should we pursue?  
We must pursue the boundless inner aspects. However, does that mean that God is outwardly guiding democracy? No, He is pushing from behind. But if this democracy does not advance centered on a global ideology, it will perish. (Up to this point, I have organized notes that could not be recorded due to a power outage.)  
We cannot deny that there is something that heaven must do until today's democratic factions unite and form a new inner shape. We must not be submerged in the trends of the present age and be content with them. We should not live enjoying the cultural benefits or social leisure that appear on the surface, but rather take a step further to study and seek a religion that can connect with our hearts and resonate with our minds. You must not forget that the time will come when we must do so. Therefore, in the end, only those who discover the fact that there is an absolute being who works to embrace this world without abandoning this land will become the princes of the new era.  
The doctrines of sects or denominations that have appeared on the surface until today cannot represent the whole in this age, and if we cannot acknowledge that they are related to the Creator God, we must sever our ties with them. If God exists, He must surely have a purpose, a single ideology that leads all humanity to a place where they can serve Him.  
From this perspective, God's providence is not a sect that appears on the surface, nor is it any ideology of the current reality that is manifest. We can infer that God is working behind the scenes to weave a new history of the new era. If we leave this world as it is, it will perish.  
Then, if there is something that God directly governs, what could it be? Here, we must advocate for humanity. It is not just words; we must find a God that we can personally experience and feel in reality. The God we call upon is not an abstract being but a concrete existence. He is not just an object of faith but the center of our lives. If a group that lives in connection with such an absolute being does not appear at the end of days, we cannot help but see this world facing its ultimate crisis.  
However, as long as the Creator God exists, He will never abandon this world to perish. Therefore, to prevent it from perishing, the form of providence in which God and humanity work together must manifest somewhere. Then, what kind of form should you first take? You must be able to call God your Father emotionally, rather than just acknowledging Him as the Creator, the Master. It must be felt deeply in your body and mind that indeed God is my Father. A providential form that can evoke such an experience must surely appear.  
God, who wishes to establish a relationship of father and son  
Until now, we have called upon God in an abstract way. We have called upon Him only as a religious subject. But that is not the case. God is the subject of life and at the same time the subject of our daily lives, and also the subject of ideology. However, no matter how broad and great that ideological subject may be, it must be analyzed and experienced in the emotional reality of life. If there is someone who can stand in a position where they can boast that the value of that ideology, experienced in life, cannot be exchanged for anything that exists, then that person must be the one God is seeking.  
If there is something we should be grateful for, it is that we can call God our Father and establish a relationship with Him. There is nothing more valuable than this. God wants to redeem fallen humanity and bestow the greatest value upon it, which means He wants to call this humanity His sons and daughters. You must experience that He comes to you with such a heart. It must not be just in words; it must be experienced.  
We are destined to surely welcome this God who comes to us. If you have any leader, that leader is not someone you will serve forever. Even if there is a representative who wishes to present some ideology on this earth today, that representative is not someone you will serve forever. Who is the one we must serve forever and live with eternally? It is the God Father who exists eternally. You must move toward such a position. You must advance to a place where you can live with God from one to ten million things.  
In the world, people take pride in being the sons and daughters of some sovereign. They take pride in being the children of a company president. But that is not the issue. That is something that exists and then disappears. If there is something truly worth boasting about, it is that you can call the Creator God, who personally created heaven and earth through the ideology of goodness, your Father, and that Creator can call you His sons and daughters. Where can there be a position greater than that?  
God is love. Indeed, God is the God of love. Why is God the God of love? Because He promises the highest things that humanity seeks and leads humanity out. We have been calling God our Father in words, but in reality, we do not know that content. In fact, we must grasp that content. Until now, we have called the true Father in heaven, the Creator who created the universe, our Father. However, have we truly embraced that Father as our real Father? We have not. God is not satisfied with just a name. We must understand that God is the one who longs for a relationship of father and son as the center of reality. Salvation is not obtained by a name. It is obtained through the substance. It is not about being connected by a name but being connected by the substance. A connection based on the name of the Creator cannot be decisive.  
God is our true Father.  
Then, can you truly enter a position where you can call the absolute being God your Father as a substance, not just a name? The problem lies here. If humanity had not fallen, what would have happened to God? If humanity had not encountered the sorrowful fate of the fall, what would have happened? Without a doubt, they would have been happy. That happiness would not have centered on people but on the Creator. It is an undeniable fact that happiness must be claimed centered on the Creator and that the ideology of goodness must be claimed. When that happens, the Creator will be with your hearts and bodies. It will be the same in your lives and throughout your life journey. Our thoughts, emotions, and senses cannot help but be connected with the Creator.  
Human beings, who should be like this, are living centered on themselves due to the fall. They are living centered on some ideology or nationalistic ideology proclaimed on this fallen earth. While many people are loyal and filial there, there are no true and sincere sons and daughters who regard the absolute God as their Father on this earth. We must understand that God is the Creator of the entire universe and at the same time our true Father.  
That true Father will come to find us. Regardless of the twists and turns of fate, we must hold onto the hand of that true Father, nurturing the historical desires and the heartfelt wishes of our lives, and until we leave the final word of "My Father!" we must go. Even if the path of death lies ahead, we must go that far. When a group of people emerges among the end-time humanity who can call the Creator, the Absolute, their Father, the new providence of God will begin from there.  
God is the subject of the heart. Therefore, God also has infinitely deep and broad emotions of sadness and infinitely joyful emotions. God does not only possess joyful and good emotions. If He is sad, He possesses a sorrow that is so deep and wide that humans cannot reach it.  
Human beings have given God immeasurable sorrow as a gift due to the fall. They have given Him pain as a gift. They have given Him persecution as a gift. They have given Him death as a gift. They have entrusted all the things that humans hate the most to God. Until now, God has not received gifts of goodness, joy, satisfaction, or happiness from humanity.  
Sin is committed by humans, but the one who must forgive that sin is God. This is an undeniable fact. If one commits a sin, the one who committed it should be the one to be forgiven; however, the sin is committed by humans, and the one who must forgive the sin is God. What is the reason for this? It is because of the relationship of father and son.  
God's goal in establishing a relationship  
God created heaven and earth and established the ancestors of humanity to govern all things, placing hope in them. He looked at Adam and Eve centered on the ideology of creation. He looked at them as the embodiment of hope. After Adam and Eve grew, God wanted to approach them. Where? He wanted to enter their hearts. Not only their hearts but also to settle deep within their emotions. The purpose of God's creation of humanity was to plant His heart deep within the hearts of humans. He came hoping that that heart would be planted, but it was broken along the way. This is the fall.  
Jesus said to fallen humanity, "Do you not know that you are the temple of God and that the Spirit of God dwells in you?" However, God has not been able to be like that until now. Why? Because it is a land of sin, an environment invaded by sin. Because humanity has become unable to live a life that can communicate with the ideology and heart that God established at the time of creation, they may have called upon God conceptually, but in reality, they have not been able to live with God. You must understand that God will come to resolve all of this and find a day when He can settle in the hearts of humans and live with them.  
If God comes to find humanity, to what extent will He come? He will come to the depths of human hearts. That is why He said, "You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart, with all your soul, and with all your might." We must not leave even a small part of our hearts behind. We must give all our hearts. God wishes to come to the depths of our hearts. After that, He will come to our bodies. He will come to each cell of our bodies. Furthermore, He will come to our lives. You must understand that God is the one who seeks to connect with us in the most detailed aspects of our lives, as well as in our hearts and bodies. This is God's goal in establishing a relationship centered on love.  
When you love someone, the more you love them, the more you want to connect with them deeply. If there is even one word that opposes or contradicts your desires, you cannot accept it. Isn't that so? Therefore, when the God who has the fundamental heart that can move heaven and earth comes to find us, He wishes to connect with us from a place that is free of blemish and fault in the depths of our hearts, and He wishes to connect with us from such a place in our bodies and in our lives.  
The ultimate solution is centered on God.  
Then, we must deeply reflect on what position we are in as we are destined to welcome the Father who comes to us. When we say, "God, I have this, and is this good for You?" and if God acknowledges it with "Yes!" then there is no worry. If it is acknowledged, we can possess it, but if it is not acknowledged, we cannot possess it.  
God does not acknowledge our bodies. Why? Because our bodies are the descendants of the fall, born with the bloodline of the fall. Also, God may tolerate your conscience to some extent, but overall, He does not accept it. Your conscience is governed by the environment. The standard of the original conscience that God established is not the conscience you have now. It is God's conscience that is the standard. Also, your body is not the standard; it is God's body that is the standard. Furthermore, your life is not the standard; it is God's life that is the standard. There will be an environment through this life, and there will be a world of ideology through this environment.  
Since the day of the fall, humanity has not been able to establish a relationship with heaven. Our individuals have not been able to establish an absolute relationship with heaven, and the lives we live have not been able to establish an absolute relationship with heaven, and the society, nation, and world we live in have not been able to establish an absolute relationship with heaven. We cannot deny this. If we just cling to this and go before God, we cannot be recognized by Him and cannot establish a relationship with Him. Why? Because that is how the principles of heaven are set.  
Then, what should we take as the center of our relationship? What is the condition that can solve and handle all problems? It is neither our conscience nor any ideology on this earth. It is God. God wishes to establish the world He desires through the standard of His heart, His mind, and His body, which are one. If there is an absolute being, He must surely govern this world centered on that. What is the ultimate solution that all humanity scattered across the globe must know? It is not any ideology. It is not a developed country like the United States. It is not any hero. It is not any sage. The ultimate solution is God. God's love, God's life, God's heart, God's emotions, God's world, God's sovereignty—this is where the problem lies. It is not a world through people.  
The history of restoration is the history of salvation.  
There are countless people living on this earth. However, among them, there is no one whom God can say, "You are indeed my heart and your heart, my emotion and your emotion, my body and your body." Therefore, God must send a representative who can say, "My heart is your heart, my emotion is your emotion, my body is your body, my ideology is your ideology" to humanity. Shouldn't that be the case? That is what God is. That is the God who has a providential will for the salvation of humanity, and unless He sends such a representative before humanity, that God cannot be trusted.  
The one who was sent as that representative is the Messiah. The Savior. What kind of Savior? The one who not only pulls us out of the place of death and saves us but also brings us to God's side on behalf of God, in other words, the Savior who can fulfill the wishes of all humanity. Then, what kind of Savior is God? He is the Savior of the heart, the Savior of the body, the Savior of the emotions, the Savior of life, and the Savior of ideology.
Oh, Lord of Heaven. The history of restoration is the history of salvation. God has been working providentially for that purpose. However, because God is an incorporeal being without a physical form, He sent the Messiah as a substantial representative to relate to us, the beings with substance, who do not know whether God exists or not. Thus, we are to choose individuals, families, and a world centered on the Messiah. This form is what we call today's democracy.

If we say that the one who came as the Messiah on this earth is Jesus, then He had to connect the highest central heart of God's love with humanity, but He could not accomplish that before He left. Therefore, Jesus promised all humanity that He is the bridegroom and that they must return to the Father as brides. Until now, Christians have thought that just meeting the Lord is enough, but that is not the case. If you meet the Lord, what must you do? You must return to the Father. It means you must return to God. The Lord is necessary because you cannot approach God without going through the Lord. Once you have gone before God, you no longer need the Lord. That is why Jesus said, "I am the way, the truth, and the life. No one comes to the Father except through Me." (John 14:6) He did not say that no one can come to Him but that no one can come to the Father.

Today, the world has the external form that allows God to come, but the world of heart is not prepared. This world can provide an environment that can communicate through circumstances, but it cannot provide an environment that can communicate through heart. Now, if God were to come, what would He bring? He would come with heart. If there is a nation that can represent this world and dominate all of humanity, what kind of nation would it be? It would be a nation that establishes God's heart as its tradition. Furthermore, what kind of culture will dominate the world in the future? It will not be a culture that comes from the hearts of people but a culture that comes from God's heart. The ultimate issue lies there. Until we find the world of ultimate purpose that can establish a world where hearts can connect, you cannot unpack your burdens here and live in eternal peace.

God comes with heart. Therefore, we must seek the Father whom we want to meet with all our heart, with all our sincerity, and with all our will. We must treat that Father as our Father and seek an environment where we can enjoy values beyond the world with Him. You must understand that this place is where you welcome the Father.

Now, you must reflect on yourselves. Where is your heart inclined? Where is your body inclined? Where is your life inclined? Where is your ideology inclined? You must reflect once again on what kind of position the God you wish to serve is in right now. God must be with you in your heart, in your body, in your life, in your environment, and in the ideologies you advocate. If He is with you in that way, your words will represent God's words, your actions will represent God's actions, and your way of living will represent God's way of living. However, if that is not the case, you must understand that your heart, body, and life have no relationship with God.

God is the most holy being, and He is in the highest position. Therefore, your emotions and consciousness must be centered on the Father. Who is the one who serves the Father? It is the one who lives through the Father, dies through the Father, and acts through the Father. However, fallen humans live through themselves. That is why they have no relationship with God. The saints of the last days who must serve God must live through the Father. Whether they eat, sleep, or act, they must do all things through the Father. This must not be merely conceptual; it must be actual. You must enter a position where you can experience that.

What is the desire of the Father? My individual self is the desire of the Father. My individual self is a desire, and the family centered on me is a desire, and the society centered on the family is a desire, and the world centered on the society is a desire, and the heaven and earth centered on the world is a desire. You must understand this. Who is the one who becomes a filial son before the Father? It is the one who discusses everything with the Father, even in the most detailed matters. A filial son is someone who acts together with the Father in times of difficulty, sadness, and joy.

Why has God been unhappy until now? Why has God been sighing until now? It is because there have been no sons and daughters who have shared in His suffering. God does not dislike suffering. If there are beloved sons and daughters who share in His suffering, He appreciates that suffering. If there are sons and daughters who can share in His sorrow and pain, then when they are in unbearable sorrow and pain, He is the Father who comforts them. If there is someone who participates in the pain of death, He is the Father who has the authority to transcend death and disregard its power.

What is God's sorrow? It is that there is no one who suffers when God suffers and no one who grieves when God grieves. For thousands of years, God has embraced humanity and has suffered alone. He has experienced injustice alone and has faced sorrow alone. When God suffers, there has been no one to share that suffering, and when God grieves, there has been no one to share that grief. That is why God has suffered greatly and grieved greatly until now. You must understand this.

Today, in these last days, no matter how evil the world is or how much the waves of death sweep over it, if there is someone who can block all of this and comfort God, in other words, if there is someone who can roll with God in suffering, that person will become a valuable existence and a true filial son or daughter of God. If such sons and daughters exist, God will not be disheartened or saddened in that position but will encourage and comfort those sons and daughters who are in such a situation with hope.

Therefore, you must now truly serve God. Where should you start serving? You should not serve from a place of joy but from a place that embraces historical sorrow and understands that heart. You must know that God is laboring because He cannot find such true sons and daughters, and when we step forward to share in God's sorrow and take responsibility for everything, God will finally grant us new joy as an object of hope.

You cannot serve God from a place of joy. You must approach the saddest place on this earth, the most painful place, the place that people dislike the most, and know God's heart, hold onto God's heart, and serve God in that place of suffering. Only by receiving comfort from God in such a place and being recognized as His sons can the eternal ideal world be realized, and at that time, God will proudly present you as His sons before heaven and earth, and you will be able to live serving God. As long as you do not receive recognition as God's sons in such a place, you will only be able to connect with one aspect in the afterlife. Even if you go to heaven, you will go to the most difficult place. No matter what problems arise, you will not be able to consult with God.

God is searching. He is looking for sons and daughters who can serve Him not in hope but in the midst of sorrow and suffering. There are many sons and daughters who serve God in hope, but there are very few who serve God in a painful place. It is very few. Who truly serves God? It is not the one who serves in joy and hope but the one who serves in suffering. By understanding God's situation and heart, God Himself will hold you and say, "My son, my daughter, I am here, endure and fight." You must understand that unless you serve God in a painful place, you cannot recognize Him as your eternal Father.

True sons and daughters with the heart of loyalty in tribulation. God has foretold that there will be a seven-year great tribulation at the end of days. This period of tribulation is when the sad twists of heaven collide with the saints in the 6,000 years of history. It is a time when human relationships break apart, and people face environments they cannot trust. No matter how conscientiously one lives, it is a time when one cannot assert their life based on that conscience. It is a time when one cannot assert their life based on faith or any doctrine. The more one has thoughts and intentions, the more they feel pain everywhere they look. That is the time of the seven-year great tribulation at the end. It is a time when hope shakes, when the center of the faith we believe in shakes, and when the leaders we have believed in and followed shake. Not only the Lord but also religion, conscience, and even the hearts of parents are all shaken.

Then why does God create such a world? It is to give value to those who have participated with the true God, the God who has labored historically. God has seen countless tragedies and endured many twists over 6,000 years, so at the end, He causes people to face environments where they cannot establish their center with conscience, doctrine, or faith. Such a time comes to find true sons and daughters who love God, even in such tribulation.

Therefore, do not be saddened by seeing the church shake, do not be saddened by seeing any doctrine waver, do not be saddened by seeing any ruler fall, and do not be saddened by seeing your parents change or your siblings fall away. Even if everything you have relied on and believed in shakes, your heart must remain calm. No matter what pain comes from the world, your heart must remain calm. You must know that God is not shaken and is still seeking you at this time. You must understand that the pain God gives us is a great promise to connect us with the precious day He has passed through and the suffering He has endured. Such a world is necessary to find those who will cry out, "Let us go together, let us fight together, let us act together."

So, do not be disheartened if the path ahead is blocked. Do not be discouraged if this nation is in turmoil. God is not dead. No matter how much this world boils over, do not be discouraged. God is not dead. God will surely come. Even if everything shakes, do not let your single-minded devotion to heaven be shaken. Do not let your heart of loyalty to heaven be shaken. Do not let your hopeful heart that relies on and looks to heaven change. Even if God places you in any painful position to change that heart, you must have a sincere heart that can call upon the Father in that place. No matter where you fall, you must strive to hold onto the cord of heavenly heart and rise up. Even if you feel the pain of falling into hell, if you stand in a position to share in the Father's suffering and believe that the Father will understand your suffering, and if you feel the responsibility and duty to go even to such a place, you will not perish.

Today, there are many Christians, but how many of those believers are there truly? In serving the Father, we must serve not the Father who sits on the heavenly throne with countless angels but the Father who is laboring to find true sons and daughters amidst the waves of death. We must recognize that Father as our Father, make His situation our situation, make His heart our heart, and make His desire our desire. We must boldly approach the Father who comes to us, knowing that it is His hope to find His sons, and understand that it is His situation to unravel His historical twists, and that it is His heart to embrace and love the lost sons. No matter what kind of hardship, tribulation, or difficulty we face, we must be able to confidently declare, "I am the embodiment of Your hope, the embodiment of Your situation, and the embodiment of Your heart."

The true attitude of serving. Today, you have come to this place not to be lifted up in glory to meet the Lord. You have not come to meet the Father who commands countless angels from the heavenly throne. You have come to serve the Father who fights amidst tribulation and endures suffering. If God is a fair being, who will He bless? He will bless such a person.

So, if you truly want to serve the Father in your heart, what should you do? God does not wish to be served in a good environment just because you are living well. He does not wish to be served amidst a luxurious life like a millionaire. So, where does He wish to be served from? He wishes to be served from the most miserable place. Just before Jesus died on the cross, He cried out, "My God, my God, why have You forsaken me?" but even in the place of death, He did not seek to meet God. He sought to meet beyond the place of death. Why? Because Satan had invaded even to the threshold of death. Jesus had to transcend that threshold of death.

Today, if we are to meet the Father, we must serve Him from the place of suffering that humanity tries to avoid. In that place, we must not seek comfort for ourselves but rather strive to comfort the Father. We must not call upon the Father for our own desires. Before we hope that the Father will fulfill our wishes, we must declare that we will fulfill the Father's desires. We must not stand in a position saying, "Father, please do this for me." Even when we face the Father in difficult places, we must have the heart to say, "I will become like this before You." We must have the desire to offer ourselves before the Father. Jesus left the words, "My God, my God, why have You forsaken me?" in the Bible as a grievance. When He went to heaven, He saw the final meeting with the Father as He transcended.
Father, even a single word, may You receive glory. I should have said, "I am grateful for fulfilling the desires of the Father." Isn't that a more beautiful expression? 

You all must bear the position of having to serve the Father, who has endured for thousands of years, day after day, so you should not think of your own suffering as painful. You must even discard the thought of it being painful. When you pray, do not pray centered on yourself. 

Do not pray, "Please let me avoid this." Such prayers should not be made. You should pray, "May the suffering I endure be a suffering that is worthy before Your will." You must have the mindset that being in this situation is all according to the Father's will and for the fulfillment of that will. 

You must remove your fundamental concepts. Have the people who have believed in God until now ever comforted God even once? They have only asked for things. What kind of thief mentality is that? No matter how much you pray like that, it will not be fulfilled. I have prayed, and that is not the way. 

What do You require of me? Prayer should be like this. However, fallen descendants, sinful people, only ask for blessings. What do You desire? If my body must suffer for Your will to be fulfilled, then let me suffer. If my body must be torn for Your will to be fulfilled, then let it be torn. Let the blessings and glory be Yours, and let the punishment and suffering be mine. That is how we should pray. 

The greatest gift to give to God 

Members of the Unification Church should not only serve the Father in glorious places. I am doing that myself. You must be able to receive the Father who comes to you from the saddest places. You must embrace the heart of the Father who comes with a sorrowful heart and become the object of His heart, so that He can say, "You are my son, you are my daughter." It is fundamentally different. If God were to bless us from the depths of hell, we must have the heart to go to the depths of hell. If you have that heart and establish the center of your faith, you will never go to hell. 

When you go to the spiritual world, it is not as the people who shout to go to heaven thought. Those who boasted of anything in the world may think it will be good in the spiritual world, but that is not how it is. 

The Father we want to serve, we must serve Him. You have longed for that Father to come to you, and you have longed to meet Him. Then what kind of preparation are you making to meet Him? Do you want to prepare a luxurious and splendid place to meet Him? Heaven does not meet you in such places. Heaven is not looking for good places. You must understand that Heaven desires to meet in places of blood and tears. The Father we will meet is not the Father of laughter but the Father who is wounded. Though He is wounded, He comes to comfort His children who are wounded with a face of compassion. 

From here, it becomes a matter of who is the true child. Such sons and daughters will stand in the highest places, while those who are not will stand in the lowest places. 

You have many gifts to give to the Father. Even if you have nothing and possess nothing, there is a gift you can give to God, and that is to appear before Him with the one appearance of shedding blood, tears, and sweat. That is the greatest gift before the Father of suffering, the Father of sorrow, the Father of injustice. 

God does not ask for gold and silver from those who come out according to His will. Rather, He is the God who holds hands with those in the same circumstances, who comforts the son who is grieving. Only those who can call Him Father in such places will have no one to oppose them wherever they go in heaven and earth. Even if they are seated at God's right hand, they will say, "It is right!" If someone unworthy is seated on God's throne, even the heavenly hosts and countless saints, as well as the Satan on earth, will accuse them. 

That is why the path of a true Christian believer is the path of death. The path of a true believer is the path of suffering. The path walked by true believers was a path of injustice, a path of endurance, a path of misery. However, it is never miserable. Heaven, which comes to us to establish a connection in such miserable places, does not neglect us but rather establishes a connection with us. Such a connection will become a condition for us to stand proudly as eternal sons and daughters of God in the heavenly realm. 

Therefore, when you call the Father in the valley of tears, you must become sons and daughters who can receive a response. When you are in a place of tears and call out, "Father!" He will say, "Yes! I am here, so endure." When you are in a place of suffering, where blood and sweat are pouring out, and you call out, "Father!" He will say, "I have endured, so you must endure too." You must be able to hear those words. 

In such places, how much have you served the Father, how much have you discussed with the Father, and how much have you lived with the Father? That is what matters; it is not a problem whether you called on the Father in a glorious place. The reason is that the Father has not yet seen the day of glory. 

Until today, advanced countries like America have led the world with external missions, but now they must come down. They must go down carrying bundles of money to find the poor nations. Not only money but also hearts and feelings must be brought down. Otherwise, other nations will take over that mission. Therefore, it is impossible not to provide aid. But do you think it is enough to just provide money? Absolutely not. 

As a nation established as the center of the Christian ideology representing all countries in the world, America must help by adding hearts and feelings to that ideology. Otherwise, other nations will take that mission away. 

The path that Unification Church members must take 

Given that historical currents have flowed like this, knowing this will, where must we go? We must go not to glorious places but to miserable places. If the seven-year great tribulation has not yet come, we must seek out places in reality that are like the seven-year great tribulation. Where will the great tribulation come? It will come from the places that people dislike the most. It does not come from the places that everyone in the world likes, but from the places that people dislike the most, so if you become victorious in such places, there will be no problem. 

The historical currents are moving into this stage. Communism has held onto workers, farmers, and the poor, and has reached a stage where it can shake the world in a short time. However, that is only external. They have not stood in such places with true hearts. They have not stood in such places with true hearts, so to dominate the world in the future, they must stand in such places with true hearts. If that happens, this world will be overturned. 

So what path must Unification Church members take? It is not the place where people are shouting about the peace flag waving, but rather the places that humans dislike the most, the places that humans avoid the most. How should we go there? We must go in the shape of the Father who has been seeking for 6,000 years. We must know that the Father is the one who sheds tears with us when we shed tears and wants to comfort us. Therefore, even if you are in a place of tears, you must embrace that heart and comfort those who are suffering, saying, "Do not cry. There is hope ahead of you, so do not cry." You must become a group that can convey happiness, hope, circumstances, and feelings to them. Only then can you inherit heaven's blessings. You will be able to inherit the blessings of heaven and earth. Only then can you have dominion over the powers of heaven and earth, as well as the powers of hell. 

That is why we must go. It is a fact that the historical currents are approaching us, so wherever you go, you must go with all your heart, will, and sincerity. Wherever your heart, will, and sincerity go, any problem can be solved. Everything in the world can be resolved. Other matters are not a problem. You must go in place of the Father, and when you go to such places, if there is someone who knows your heart and holds you and sheds tears, you must be able to comfort them in place of the Father. Only then can you truly become the sons and daughters of God; otherwise, you cannot be true children of God. 

The path of suffering you are taking is a path of return. It is only for a moment. It is not a path toward hope and purpose. It is a path of return from the other side of hope. It is only for a moment. We Unification Church members must go the path that this nation cannot go on behalf of this nation. Furthermore, we must move this nation to go the path that the world cannot go. What must we center on as we go? We must center on true hearts and the heart of God. Then you will dominate the world. 

Even if the ideology you are shouting for, the position you are in, and the value you are proud of are great, they must connect with values and relationships that are greater than the value of the universe. Where does that relationship begin? It begins from the most miserable places, the most difficult places, the most sorrowful places. In such places, those who can disregard sorrow, digest sorrow, and comfort those who are grieving are the ones who truly serve the Father. 

Those who go out with such a heart will never suffer for long. They will never perish. Even if the body encounters suffering, beyond that place, an infinite world of freedom unfolds. Now we are in a transitional period where we must go beyond such places, so you must surely go beyond that place. Therefore, you must embrace the heart of the Father and become the pioneers of suffering, the pioneers of sorrow, and the pioneers of difficulty, so that you can comfort those who follow that path. If you do so, you will undoubtedly become the sons and daughters of heaven and represent the whole world. Also, if this nation becomes such a nation, it will become a nation that receives heaven's blessings on behalf of countless nations, so I ask that you become those who can serve the Father in such places. 

<Prayer> Until now, we have known the Father as one who is in glory and joy. We believed that He could freely give us all blessings and riches and grant us the joy of liberation and the fulfillment of purpose. However, knowing the circumstances behind heaven, we have come to understand that there are internal difficulties that prevent Him from giving blessings even if He wants to, and we have realized the tremendous fact that we must indemnify the sorrowful history of 6,000 years. Therefore, let us not become those who know and sigh, but let us become those who sigh over our inability to act. 

Let us know that the Father is the Father who is coming to find this nation and the Father who is coming to find all humanity. We have come to understand that His footsteps are still soaked with tears of sorrow and that there are still barriers of suffering remaining. Today, we must become the walls of the Father's suffering and the city of His sorrow, and whether the Father recognizes us or not, we must embrace the Father's injustice and resentment and fulfill our responsibilities and missions, becoming those who can fight on the battlefield against resentment, sowing blood and tears. 

Father, do we have anything precious? That is not originally ours. Even if we have something to boast about, that too is not ours. It belongs to heaven, to the nation, and to the world. To return it, we must establish a heartfelt connection with heaven, so let us become those who can empathize with the heart of humanity. 

When we look at the mountains and rivers, we must be able to look at them with tears, embracing the heart of the Father, and when we look at the people, we must do the same, and when we look at humanity, we must also be able to do so. 

You have taught us many things during this time. We have received that as heaven's eternal legacy, so now we must become the ancestors who pass on what heaven has left behind to our descendants for generations to come. We must become the individuals that the Father desires and establish the families that the Father desires, and based on those families, we must build the ideological world that the Father desires. 

We have come to understand that the larger the scope of construction, the more tears and blood we must shed. We must shed tears to find individuals, families, and nations, and furthermore, we must not mind if blood and sweat flow. Let us take pride in consuming everything in serving the Father until the end of our lives. At this time, let us once again resolve to be those who can sing the Father's glory with tears in that place. 

Father, have compassion on the thirty million people. Although this nation does not know the hardships You have gone through to find it, let us at least know. Although many people do not know the injustices of the 6,000-year history of restoration, let us who are being chased and oppressed know. Let us truly be those who can call the Father "Father," and may that Father truly regard us as His sons and daughters, longing for a place where we can comfort and be comforted. 

We must not fear the remaining path of tribulation but become those who can take the lead. We have come to understand that we must build a breakwater to block the waves of death and that we must resolve for this work, swear for this work, and devote all our sincerity to the fulfillment of this work. 

If there are those who pray with tearful hearts for heaven, Father, please embrace and love them. This path may seem unjust, resentful, and painful from a human perspective, but because it is the path You have walked, we must turn this into a path of joy, gratitude, and glory. We understand that You have compassion for those who are destined to walk the opposite path, so we earnestly hope and desire that we can run this path with You until the end. 

Please hold the hearts of the young sons and daughters participating in this 40-day training starting today, Father. May they prepare to serve the Father in the most difficult places more than anyone else and receive training to become true sons and daughters who genuinely serve the Father.
. Please let these individuals be able to make resolutions and take action under such standards. 
May Your glorious hand not depart from the remaining time, and may we, while directly treading the footsteps You walked, shed tears of gratitude and become true filial sons and daughters who can comfort You. I earnestly ask for this. I hope that everything will be done according to Your will and that a day of victory will manifest in this world. I pray in Your name. Amen. * 
14)
Let Us Become Victors
<Summary of the Message> Here, various people with different circumstances have gathered. I believe they have participated with their own special resolutions and vows. From now on, we cannot act according to our own hearts. We must respond to the guidance of the organizers. The significance of this training session is to ensure that when we appear before the nation after completing the 40 days of training, we do so as individuals of character. 
Our Standard of Victory
Today, I would like to particularly share a message titled "Let Us Become Victors." Throughout history, and in reality, we live amidst an endless struggle between good and evil. If individuals experience this, how can we expect to achieve victory in the unfolding of the overall ideology of heaven without going through struggles? 
This 40-day period is a time to cultivate historical victors. Our goal of victory is not in individual or partial aspects but in the overall victory. We must become overall victors. We must become individuals with a firm belief that we can win in any environment. 
On February 12, 1961, at the former headquarters church. 
* This message was delivered at the opening ceremony of the 5th National Evangelist Training Session and is compiled from what was published in <Seonghwa> No. 4 (February 28, 1961). 
Jacob's victory in wrestling with the angel by the Jabbok River was not a victory obtained in that moment of struggle. It was derived from the unwavering belief and experiences gained over 21 years of fighting with a purpose. Even though his shepherd life in Laban's house did not suit him, he endured for 7 years, then another 7 years, and then another 7 years, totaling 21 years, during which he internalized his ideals. If the Israelite nation, having endured 400 years of oppression in Egypt, had gone out with the spirit of Jacob, they would have had no problem returning to Canaan. However, only Moses, with a single-minded heart longing for his homeland and embracing the Israelite nation, was blessed as the leader of the remaining people. His act of striking the Egyptian was out of love for God and his people. If the entire Israelite nation had not lost the spirit of Moses, they would not have fallen in the wilderness. 
They were disciplined every time they lost this spirit. If they had inherited the spirit of Jacob and Moses, the Jews would not have betrayed Jesus. The one who came as a representative of the nation and the world, inheriting the spirit of Jacob and Moses, is Jesus. However, the Israelite nation could not uphold Jesus. Thus, the first Israel perished.

Today’s gathering is a precious occasion that happens only once. If we do well, we become victors; if we do poorly, we become losers. Now is the age of globalism, and God is working on the restoration of Israel centered on Christians at this time. If we win in this struggle, we can become the third Israel. 
Now is the time that matches the era when Jacob fought, when Moses fought, and when Jesus fought. In this age, we stand at a crossroads of victory or failure. We must win. Therefore, we must stand in a position that does not yield to any nation or anyone. 
I must be able to say that I have the conviction of Jacob, the conviction of Moses, and the conviction of Jesus. Only then can I be presented in any position before heaven. Heaven demands victors.

Let Us Fulfill Our Duty of Loyalty
<Summary of the Message> Many people have rushed toward good. But there is still a way to go. 
Where should we go? We must go to a place where we can always rejoice, or to the One who can always bring us joy. This One is the absolute God. God exists in the world of motives and the world of results. He exists as cause and effect. Therefore, He is called the Alpha and the Omega. 
When humans understand that they are in the process of cause and effect, they will understand the relationship between God and humans. History is moving from the world of causes to the world of results. Therefore, human conscience is walking this path of process, and because the flow of history is rapid, the conscience that seeks to follow it is doubly busy. 
The motive must be God, and humans must be established as results. If humans had not fallen, they would have been the causes of history. However, the inability to possess causes is the fall. 
Due to the fall, the world of purpose is far, and the conscience within the realm of motives is closer to the cause, so establishing the conscience is the mission of religion. Of course, Buddhism also belongs to this category. 
When we come to know the stable point of the heart, peace comes. The world of love has no observation. It transcends observation. The overall value is related to partial values, and because love represents the overall result, humans who have no connection to the world of causes and purposes are without value. Therefore, let us go to the place that teaches us about causes and purposes. 
When it is said that history has an end and to believe in me, we can know that God exists. Among all religions, the only religion with a historical connection that aims for the end times is Christianity. 
If Christianity cannot stand in such a position, it will perish. Therefore, a religion or church that has a fear of the times will perish. Christianity did not perish because it boldly moved forward even amidst the persecutions of the Roman Empire. 
We must make a global decision. A religion that is in the middle of the left and right wings must break through this. Love is something that God, people, animals, democracy, and communism all like, so we are trying to establish love and build something emotional. 
Now humanity must clarify the existence of God and know itself. If we ask why the will has not been fulfilled despite having raised many people until now, God will not answer. Because there is still room to ask more questions. If we ask whether God could not fulfill His will because there were no people, He will nod His head with tears. If we ask whether there is no one who is fully loyal, God will weep.

To be loyal to the point of risking death is not bad at all. There are many loyal people, but the reason the will has not been fulfilled is that the content of their loyalty differs from what God desires. No one is loyal without hoping for something greater than today. In other words, they have been loyal for themselves. 
God has also set a standard of loyalty, which is why He has asked for loyalty. To become the king of loyalty, that is, to become a child of God, one must establish a standard of loyalty like God. God has been loyal for the sinful humans of this earth. This loyalty is an unending loyalty, a loyalty that becomes minus the more it is practiced. Therefore, we must also practice such loyalty. In other words, we must practice a loyalty of despair. 
Heaven and glory are not desired; I should be one who can spare my loyalty and bear the pain. Moses, who stepped away from the glory of the palace, was loyal to the nation and to God. 
God intends for pain to be His own and for glory to belong to the saints.

There is no tradition, ideology, or name. There is only the principle of True Parents.

Our Father is the Father of tears, blood, and sweat. Until now, the Father has been blocking Satan while shedding the tears, sweat, and blood that you have not shed. 
On our shoulders rests the fate of the historical first Israel, today’s second Israel, and the future third Israel. To complete the history of restoration, we must fill the measure of tears, sweat, and blood. Before we die, we must fill the measure of tears, sweat, and blood to give to the first, second, and third Israel. Until we fill the measure of tears, sweat, and blood, we cannot become the sons and daughters of God. 
We must shed tears, sweat, and blood for the first, second, and third Israel to be able to call the Father, Father.

This path is the path that heaven and the teacher walk. Therefore, from now on, you must weave the history of heart to become the ancestors of the third Israel.
You must have the love of your children, the love of your spouse, and the love of your parents. Otherwise, you cannot stand in a historical position. There are no collaborators on the final path. Now that you understand the will, you must fulfill your responsibilities as the Third Israel before the First and Second Israel. Even if you set aside the responsibilities of the First and Second Israel, you must fulfill the responsibilities of the Third Israel.

You must go out with the representatives of the Second Israel. This is because of the relationship between Cain and Abel. Both Cain and Abel were born at a time not permitted by heaven, but Cain is closer to Satan, while Abel is closer to heaven. Therefore, you must love those on the side of Cain more than your own direct descendants. Right now, you are going out to find Cain. The Third Israel is born from the Second Israel, which has received heavenly blessings. This is the path of destiny. What Jesus hoped for was to have sons of faith, from Seth, twelve, to 120. These must be blessed and bear sons and daughters to become heavenly sons and daughters.

In restoring people, you must first seek the precious children of others or the most respected young men or women in that village. You must find the best Cain. You must advance through the position of children and the position of spouses to the position of parents.

To revive the whole, you must take the sons and daughters of Cain who can die in place of others. If they are not outstanding, you must obtain faithful people. Only then can you establish a foundation to give birth to excellent second generations. If you fail to achieve your will, you will have to return like Jesus, but from now on, there will be no second coming, only the handling of that matter.

Even when the teacher was shackled and heading to prison, he went with hope. This was because it was the path to find the people of the will. So you too must live as those entrusted with the great work by the Father who has been seeking for 6,000 years. You must take responsibility for this. I do not want even one of you to fall away. I hope each of you will fulfill your responsibilities and advance to the position of receiving blessings. Only then can you become the sons and daughters of God and become the owners. You can only become the ancestors of the Third Israel by advancing to the position of the true owner.

When you go to the local area, you must pray with a heart that surrounds that district or village. You must practice with the conviction that you are in me, and those in me must live like this. If we fight silently, we cannot help but use the methods that God and the teacher have fought with until now. In other words, you must practice like a servant to be recognized as the master of your heart, the master of your actions, and the master of your feelings. It is no longer difficult. The time has come. If you go just a little further, it will be easy. So, what must you do to become the true owner? First, you must establish the concept of ownership that everything belongs to the Father, and therefore it is mine. Second, you must have a strong sense of responsibility. I must take responsibility for everything. And I must have the heart to help my neighbors with the strength that remains. Third, after fulfilling my responsibilities with the consciousness that everything is mine, I must dedicate it to the Father as my own. It must be offered as my own sacrifice.

By doing this, you can become a victor at the end of your life.
