Worship and Time
At this time, the teacher has prayed for you. You must walk the path of life according to this time. What are you thinking about day and night? Where are you going, for whom are you living, and what are you doing? Everything you do, everything you seek, and everything you live for must be for my purpose. As the scripture just read states, God is calling you not to worry about what to eat, wear, or drink, but to seek His kingdom and His righteousness. He is telling you to do everything for heaven and to participate in the way heaven goes.

When have you truly worked for the will and for the kingdom and righteousness? Have you sought God when He was hungry, when He was thirsty, when He was naked, or when He was a stranger? The first place to seek for the will must be here.

So when you come to find the Father, what kind of heart should you have? You should not come with the heart of doing worldly work, establishing worldly achievements, or harboring worldly intentions, but with the heart to clothe the naked, to feed the hungry, to give drink to the thirsty, and to welcome those who are like strangers.

What does the will mean? Until now, humanity has not been able to harbor the will of heaven. We have not had the qualifications to harbor the will. However, heaven is asking this fallen lineage, which deserves to die a million times, to harbor the good will of heaven on the foundation of heaven's hard work. We have no nation. We have no will. No matter how much we have harbored the will until now, that will has had no relationship with God. Even if we had a nation, that too had no relationship with God. We have no nation and no will. Furthermore, you have nothing to establish before heaven.

What is the purpose of your coming to this place? It is to deepen the will, to care for the righteousness of that kingdom, and to cultivate a heart for the people of that kingdom. But what can you do if you cannot even keep time?

The person speaking here has been shedding blood and sweat for you until now. No matter what anyone says, I can swear before heaven and earth. I have fought with all my heart for you until now. Think about it. I have prepared for this one day as one who is responsible for your path before heaven. Do you think I treat you based on the connections I made on the street? Even when I pray, I do so with the heart of, "Father, you have been with me for 40 years!" Today, I feel the responsibility to present a life before the Father or let it be mocked by Satan. I am not someone who prepares sermons by setting a topic like the people of the world. I want to speak the words of the Father that are needed at this time. If that standard is not established, I pray with struggle and tears. I pray while worrying about your path.

I have shed blood and sweat for you. Think about it. You came out here under such conviction and determination, but can I speak in front of you who cannot even keep time properly? I wish you would just be turned upside down. Among you, there are parents and children, but when you go before God, time is more important than anything else. The timing is more important than anything else. If you miss the time, you will perish. If you cannot find the time, you will perish. God requires a highly sanctified environment and a sanctified heart, but you cannot even keep time and are singing praises from behind. Heaven does not want such praises.

You must understand that your responsibility is heavy. If there are many people who look to you and follow the will, do you want them to become like you? Do you want them to become mere spectators? What can you say in front of heaven as someone who swore to fulfill responsibility? How can you pray for blessings? 

"God! Please grant them the glory hidden in heaven. Please grant them the realm of life in heaven." Can you do that?

To make the teacher a teacher, you must fulfill your responsibilities. Even when you pray before the Father, you must be able to say, "Father, your sons and daughters whom you called have come. The sons and daughters you wanted to meet have come." You must create an environment that allows you to pray.

Originally, if the time is exceeded, the door should be locked. I do not want to gather people like you and talk. I have to talk for two or three hours to raise you to a certain standard. Only then can I connect to the emotional standard I prayed for and prepared before heaven.

Everyone, worship time has passed, but how many of you have gathered? If you have such a mindset, the teacher does not want to guide you on Sundays. It would be better to go to the local church. That would be more comfortable. My heart matches with the local members. When I occasionally visit the local areas, you must understand that there are people who walk hundreds of miles just to attend that one hour. Compared to such people, you deserve to be cursed before heaven. There are people who want to come but cannot afford the fare, so they go without food for three or four days and walk a hundred or two hundred miles. You must understand that.

What the trainees felt in common when they came to the headquarters is that all the members of the headquarters are not fully developed. You all must do better than the members of the local church if you want the teacher to have a standard to speak on your behalf in the local church. To be in a position where I can speak on your behalf in the local church, you must do better. What kind of people are living for the will like this?

You, who are shouting for heart unity, action unity, ideology unity, and lifestyle unity, do you not feel ashamed to come so late? How can you lift your face? And what grace do you expect to receive? Such people will never receive grace. Moreover, it has been said that in the end, you should strive to gather. You should strive to gather. But have you strived? Therefore, in the future, if such people exist, I will try to finish Sunday worship within 30 minutes. I will pray once, read the scripture once, and only talk about the main points of the sermon. Even if the teacher is here, I will no longer lead Sunday worship. Let’s see how things are going. The people here are not the ones you should treat like that.

When we go before heaven, promises must be absolutely kept wherever we go. What grace can a person who does not keep promises receive? Such a person will stop halfway. In the future, the teacher will guide you according to your movements. If you dislike it, quit. Let’s see who fails. Who will fail?

Heaven responds to those who earnestly desire and strive. Heaven is not just anyone who responds. Therefore, you must absolutely keep time. In the future, if you break time, I will put you in front of me and embarrass you one by one. Do you understand?

The title I wanted to speak to you today is "True Oath." This message is necessary for this time. Everyone, now is the time to swear. It is not the time to be vague. It is the time to swear. Know this and pray. If heaven permits, I will speak again next week; if not, I will not.

Everyone, there are people who incite you to swear, so swear that you will take responsibility for heaven and earth. How blessed you are to have come to such a time. Do you have friends with whom you have sworn? Do you have a family bound by oaths? Even the teacher must be energized while guiding you, right? To be energized, the heart of hope must arise through you. But if I give this message and still feel empty, and after teaching, I feel regret, how can I be energized? This will not work. Let us pray.

<Prayer> Father, I know that the Father I know is the one who desires responsibility. I know that the Father I serve does not accept anything but the blood sacrifice. The nation I admire is a nation formed by people unrelated to enemies. The group I desire is one that pours out blood and flesh for the Father and still weeps.

Father, we live in a fallen world, so we are easily influenced by habits and institutions, and it is difficult to escape from this environment we are living in. Even those who harbor the will cannot live a life that moves beyond the past, present, and future like sinful people, and they cannot escape the reality of their environment, so they just live as they are. However, since each of us has a center before the Father and has made a vow to do this, please allow us to realize that no matter what difficult circumstances we encounter, we must take responsibility to the end so that the Father will not be saddened.

Let us feel ashamed if we break a promise, even for a moment, and let us understand that only those who can bow their heads without maintaining face and prestige can become heirs of the Father's joy. We have been too negligent today. We have been too irresponsible. Please forgive us.

The meaning of the promise and the providence of the administration have come close to us, and we are afraid that we may leave a grievance for eternity because of our shortcomings. If we had not been born, the Father would not have been wronged, but since we were born, we must fulfill the Father's will.
I am afraid that I may not be able to fulfill my duty, so I earnestly hope and wish to become your son or daughter who will be more loyal, more earnest, and able to take on more responsibilities for you today than in the past, and for the future more than today.  
Father, I know that there are many lonely groups kneeling before your presence at this time, so please have compassion on them and bless them. I earnestly hope and wish that you will embrace them and allow them to reach the place of hope you desire without losing heart, and that you will personally hold them so that they do not fall but reach the promised place.  
Father, are there groups today who are crying out for true life before you? Please extend your hand over them and protect them. How much do you long for the day when you can dwell among them and work with them? I earnestly hope and wish that when that day comes, you will allow them to serve you with all their heart and soul.  
Please overlook all our shortcomings today. Allow us to become your sons and daughters who can participate before you, prepared with traces of true longing for heaven, and grant us the time to offer our true hearts as living sacrifices along with our bodies.  
This place is where we serve you, where we discuss with you, and where we offer our sincerity before you, so please help us to separate everything and discern everything for ourselves. Let us realize whether we can be worthy before your heart, and allow us to separate ourselves so that we can offer ourselves before you.  
I earnestly hope and wish that you will prepare us so that we can offer our hearts, bodies, and entire lives before you without lacking anything, and allow us to establish a connection with you. Please personally oversee everything, Father. Father, guide us with that heart and lead us to a place where we can participate with your heart.  
May your glory be with all that has appeared. Father, please allow these people to fulfill your purpose of providence, and do not forget the promises you have made, but please continue to practice them with these people until the end. I earnestly ask all these things in your name. Amen.  
**Become a Responsible Person**  
<Summary of the Message> You have come representing your church and family in each region. From now on, you must be different from your past selves.  
You must fulfill the responsibilities and conditions that heaven requires, both internally and externally, according to the guidance of those who represent the purpose under one promise. Since the headquarters deals with many people, they may not be able to treat you as well as you hope. So please understand in advance and be patient. Even if there are shortcomings in how you are treated, please overcome them well.  
When a person takes responsibility for a nation, they become the leader of that nation; when they take responsibility for the world, they become the leader of the world; when they take responsibility for heaven and earth, they become the leader of heaven and earth. Our goal is to become the highest leaders. Therefore, the teacher aims to guide you to become eternal leaders, not temporary ones, before society, the nation, the world, heaven and earth, and the Absolute Being.  
From now on, you must take responsibility for yourselves and for everything. As a member of the people, you must take responsibility as one of the people, or as a member of a group, you must take responsibility as a member of that group. The same goes for ideology. If not, heaven cannot take responsibility for you. You must establish a four-dimensional aspect around yourself.  
April 7, 1961 (Friday), at the former headquarters church.  
* This message was organized as an encouragement speech at the opening ceremony of the 6th National Evangelist Training Conference, published in <Seonghwa> No. 9 (September 30, 1961).  
From now on, when you are sent to a region or any place on behalf of your purpose, you must be able to take responsibility for yourself. Those who cannot take responsibility for themselves cannot be entrusted with other missions. Only those who can take responsibility for themselves can be given other responsibilities. Only after taking responsibility for oneself can one establish this ideology. Those who cannot do this cannot establish an ideology.  
God has not yet found anyone in heaven and earth who can take responsibility for me. However, once you take responsibility for yourselves, that becomes the starting point. Nations and the trends of the world all move within the realm of responsibility. The rice we eat and the clothes we wear all question our responsibility. If you cannot take responsibility, you will have no face to meet all things. Therefore, I hope you will become those who can take responsibility for the whole. Only then can you call God the Creator, Father, and Master.  
Humans lost their position to take responsibility from the moment they fell. They could not become true children before true parents and could not become true possessions before the true owner.  
God is the Absolute Being for all things, the parent for humanity, and the true owner for heaven and earth. Where do you place your starting purpose? Can you become a being that can represent God? God is our true Father and true Owner, so we must advance to a position where we can represent this. Otherwise, it becomes a disregard for the Lord of life.  
We must offer life to the Absolute Being, love to the True Parents, and loyalty to the True Owner. Otherwise, we cannot establish a relationship with the true life of the Creator, the true love of the True Parents, and the true principles and relationships of the True Owner. If you cannot take responsibility for yourself, you cannot establish relationships with all your neighbors.  
Many of you may pride yourselves on being apostles of unification. However, you should be those who take responsibility for the value of the object concerning the subject. Such people are recognized as beings of eternal and unchanging value. When you go to each region, you must go on behalf of the Creator's position, the parent's position, and the owner's position that can take responsibility. All things do not groan because God is absent, but because there is no one who can take responsibility on behalf of God. You must take responsibility for yourselves. If there is a place where you must take responsibility, you must go regardless of whether it rains or snows.  
God takes responsibility as the Creator, the Absolute Being, the True Father, and the True Owner. That is why He has been carrying out the providence of restoration. If God does not take this responsibility, there can be no restoration or heaven. Even if God is betrayed and chased away, He does not abandon the position of the Absolute Being. God takes responsibility as the Absolute Being, as the Father, and as the True Owner. You must also take on the responsibilities of the Absolute Being, the Father, and the Owner.  
Do not refuse to take on the qualifications to be responsible, but rather take on the responsibilities of a Father and a Master and move forward. God takes responsibility for all three aspects, and you must take responsibility for at least one aspect. When you take responsibility and go to the region, all things in that region will know what kind of value you possess. The environment will testify to this. What will it testify? You will be testified as the one who can save our lives, the embodiment of the Father, and the owner of our region. There will be a desire to entrust and dedicate everything to you.  
If you take on the responsibilities of the Creator, the Father, and the True Owner, heaven and earth will help you wherever you go. You must take on the responsibilities of the Absolute Being, the Father, and the Owner. If you take on those responsibilities, you will not be rejected. Today, everyone is looking for someone who can take responsibility for their actions, their lives, and their hearts. This society is an ideal society. If you take responsibility and are prepared to risk your life, many comrades will appear.  
When you go to the region, you must take on the responsibilities of the Creator as the one who created life, the responsibilities of a parent, and the responsibilities of a master. If you cannot do this, you cannot be the representatives of the Absolute Being, the True Parents, or the True Owner. If you cannot even do this, you will inevitably be expelled from the world of existence. If you cannot take responsibility, you must serve with absolute obedience. Therefore, you must stand in a position where you can take responsibility for yourself. You must become victorious warriors who take responsibility on behalf of the Absolute Being, the True Parents, and the True Owner. Heaven is looking forward to such beings.  
**Jesus Came as the Center of Love**  
<Summary of the Message> Today is the day we commemorate Jesus, who returned after not being able to fulfill his purpose and resurrected. If humanity had not fallen, the term resurrection would not be necessary. Originally, God and humanity, the spiritual world and the physical world were meant to be inseparably connected, but due to humanity's fall, they became completely separated. God has been carrying out the providence of re-creation to restore this situation. Therefore, God has longed for the day when heaven and earth will be resurrected, and individuals, families, nations, the world, and the cosmos will be resurrected. However, since there is no individual to accomplish this, the paths for families, nations, and the world have all been blocked. Thus, humanity has lamented the mistakes of their ancestors.  
When God created humanity, His heart was for heaven, and He created their bodies to be grounded in the earth. Therefore, the universe was supposed to move centered around each individual, but due to humanity's fall, everything became divided. Thus, in order to unify the spiritual world and the physical world, my heart and body must first achieve unity. The divided must be brought back together and unified.  
God has led humanity in the direction of good through the responsive action of human conscience based on the standard of nature. In other words, God has been relating to humanity based on our conscience. In the family of Adam and in the family of Noah, God established the standard of conscience. In the course of history, individuals must completely resurrect to fulfill the purpose of creation.  
Through Jesus, the outpost of heaven on earth was finally established. Until then, God could not set foot in the human world. It was only after Noah, Abraham, and Moses that the outpost of heaven was established through Jesus.  
The central being that serves as God's foothold on this earth is none other than Jesus, the Son of God. He came as the center of love. Therefore, God's love can only be manifested through Jesus.  
However, due to the disbelief of the earth, Jesus lost his reality and could not establish God's foothold on earth before ascending to the spiritual world. Therefore, after creating Adam, God sent the Holy Spirit just as He created Eve. In other words, He sent the Holy Spirit as a spiritual counterpart. God does not bless only certain individuals. He has been working while centering on the conscience of humanity. When the standard of conscience aligns, the Holy Spirit comes; if not, the Holy Spirit cannot come. That is why the Holy Spirit only comes and works when we pray earnestly. The Holy Spirit brings the gift of resurrection.  
We must pray and give our utmost loyalty. We must offer a loyalty that exceeds the standard that the fallen archangel offered before the fall in order to approach heaven. We must serve in place of the fallen archangel and go before heaven. Although 2,000 years have passed since Jesus, the act of offering loyalty continues. The question is how much effort has been made to elevate one's faith to a certain standard. God has gone through the path of labor for 6,000 years.  
Just as Jesus labored as the embodiment of resurrection on this earth, we must also become the embodiment of resurrection on the final day and stand before heaven as loyal subjects. Fallen humans must serve in the position of the Holy Spirit, which is the position of the archangel, by offering loyalty in the position of the son of God, Jesus. We must all receive Jesus and the Holy Spirit as our reality.  
We must establish the way for the archangel to serve humanity on this earth. Due to the fall, this substantial standard could not be established. We must pray for our own resurrection before praying for the resurrection of all people.  
If Jesus comes to this earth as the True Father to establish each of us as a reality, we must certainly find and establish the True Mother, who is the substantial form of the True Parents. Jesus must come again to establish the path to fulfill his mission as a heart-centered parent, which is the Feast of the Lamb.  
We must establish the laws of heaven throughout our lives. The providential history leading up to Jesus has been a history to resurrect Adam and Eve. To accomplish this, countless humans had to be sacrificed according to the law of indemnity. God's purpose of creation is to create a world of creation that has the form and function of a perfect human being. Christianity is the bone, and all other religions are the flesh. That is why God has been working to move the entire spirit world centered on Christianity.  
God has not yet had the opportunity to exercise sovereignty on this earth by establishing a single reality. Until now, God has been working indirectly rather than directly. Due to the fall of human ancestors, the multitudes who had died have now reached the position of the Son of God. When the leaders of Israel fail to fulfill their responsibilities, countless humans remain in an intermediary position.  
Although Jesus established a spiritual standard, God's will has not been completely fulfilled. For this to happen, the time must be right, the environment must be prepared, and God must be with us. The vertical will of Jesus does not come to fruition just because there are many horizontal disciples. To fulfill that will, a vertical period must be traversed. In other words, the relationships from the past must be connected.  
The purpose of the Second Coming of Jesus is to carry out the mission of the Father beyond the mission of the Son. The True Parents must adopt those in the position of servants as adopted children and then establish those adopted children as direct sons and daughters. The day Jesus comes is known only to the Father. To God, the horizontal aspect of Christianity is not the issue. In principle, the Israelite people must never allow Jesus to be killed. However, both Jesus and the Israelite people died. Today, all Christians around the world must earnestly establish conditions of indemnity. The spirits of the Old Testament must pray just like Jesus did. All the leaders of the Old Testament are praying.  
Jesus works with the Holy Spirit in the middle. Jesus hopes that that day and that number will come. He is carrying out the providence of resurrection to find one being at the end along with hundreds of millions.  
Fallen humanity must walk the path of the spiritual Golgotha and the physical Golgotha. When multitudes approach God, they do so according to order and rank. In the resurrection of the heart and body, one must first go through the process of the servant's resurrection. This means that one must fulfill the responsibilities of a servant. A spirit cannot help someone who is of a higher rank than themselves.
Before the victorious being comes, the wall that separates heaven and earth does not come down. God created Adam to establish him as the substantial embodiment of victory. The Lord of the Second Advent must initiate the movement of resurrection and liberation from the lowest levels of the spirit world. He must pioneer the spiritual Golgotha of the spirit world, which is divided into many paths. He must pass through the stages of restoration and growth to reach completion. For the hope of all humanity to be realized, one center must come. The Lord of the Second Advent must break through the spiritual Golgotha and tear down the wall that separates heaven and earth. The path of righteousness must be opened. We must break through the lowest levels to establish a foundation for victory. After that, we must go through the expectations of reality.

To move from the growth stage to the completion stage, conditions must be established. This means overcoming the Golgotha of the two worlds. What kind of suffering has there been until the ideology of unification emerged? There was the Golgotha of heaven. To walk this path, we must follow the path of the highest cross. We must go with the will of heaven at the center. Parents and children must together welcome the day of victory.

Now is a time without a master. However, this period will not last long. During this time, we must awaken this nation. Our family must all become one. We must endure hardships in the countryside for three years. When we can mobilize and move even to the villages and towns of the countryside at once, the standard of victory will be established. We must go with life. We must head toward the day of resurrection. We must go with the hope of the promised day. If our will prevails, it will be God's victory and the victory of all humanity.

April 17th is the day Jesus resurrected. How wonderful a day it is! If we receive the blessing of Jesus, we will stand on the foundation of Jesus who has triumphed in the spirit world. You must appear as courageous individuals who can fight and win against the great adversary of the world.

If we can pass through this path smoothly, going to heaven will not be a problem. Since Jesus' resurrection is a spiritual resurrection, we must celebrate after achieving the resurrection of substance and fulfilling His purpose. Only after complete resurrection can we call Jesus our brother. God welcomed this day with tears and sighs. What is the complete resurrection? It is the resurrection of substance that has achieved the purpose of creation.

Humans with the bloodline of the fall cannot call God their Father. They must receive recognition from Jesus before they can call God their Father. God is not a cheap father who can be called carelessly. There is not a single person on this earth who can call God Father as Jesus did. Even in the spirit world, there is no one who can call Him Father. The reason is that humans cannot be trusted and are changeable. There are various kinds of fathers, including real fathers, false fathers, and stepfathers.

Humans must go through the history of restoration and resurrection on this earth. Jesus went forth to fight against enemies, risking death, but there was no one who followed that path. You must liberate God and Jesus from the place of suffering.

God does not give blessings indiscriminately. God is a God of order. We must be meek and humble. A person who was a laborer cannot become a minister immediately. We must cut off the roots of Satan.

To celebrate Jesus' resurrection, we must step on and pass through the cross. Therefore, we must meet the resurrected Jesus. We must welcome not the Lord of the cross but the Lord of resurrection. We must pass over the spiritual Golgotha and the physical Golgotha. 

In any case, all humans must cross over the hill of Golgotha. Thus, we must welcome the resurrected Jesus.

The year 1961 is a year of profound significance. We must go on behalf of Jesus and the heavenly land. You must stand as beings who can celebrate this day before the heavenly land as the substantial resurrection. Only then can we celebrate completely.

Live a life of offering.
<Summary of the Message> By creating a heartistic expectation that can connect 12 sons across 12 generations, the spirits that have come and gone through historical vertical paths can cooperate on earth. By establishing a vertical standard across 12 generations and then setting horizontal expectations again, the spirit world can also achieve horizontal history due to conditions on earth.

Many good children were sacrificed to find just one Adam, so we must endure hardships to restore them.

Until now, we have only sought blessed children and not wealth, but now we must pray to seek wealth.

Even if the food offered to parents is insufficient, we must strive to serve them well. If we have a heartfelt desire to serve them well every day, the development of our lives will come. This heart must be established as a tradition.

When offering a sacrifice, we must go to Abel and offer it. We must purify ourselves for three days before offering.

In the church, we must establish numbers based on 360 and offer them with a global character. Those who are elected as Abel in the church will receive blessings. Those in the position of Abel must offer sacrifices with even greater weight. Those elected as Abel will receive the grace of world evangelism.

If this happens, the church will grow the more we move. We must solve the issues of education and housing through this method. If we commit crimes, we cannot participate in this. We must establish the standard of not having slept. Therefore, we must keep watch. At the same time, we must be ready to obey God's commands.

Let us awaken.
<Summary of the Message> I feel sorry for having completed the training session in an inadequate environment. This sixth training session has a special significance compared to others. The number six has great significance in both creation and restoration.

Awaken to the responsibility of being a historical leader.
Those of you who have received training during this period must feel a special mission. The number six is important in settling the sins of heaven and earth, and it is significant in the fight against Satan. Even if you fight separately, you must not forget that you are the sixth training participants. The value standard that God intended when creating humans and blessing them was also the number six. This period is historically and universally significant.

Those of you who have spent this period must take on a central responsibility. You must feel that new activities will unfold centered around the sixth training participants. You are all young people who have fought on the front lines. Some of you may not fully understand this ideology, but you must not forget that those who fought on the front lines are at the center. The feelings, resolutions, and vows you felt during the training must not stop here; you must become those who will eternally bear responsibility for history and the times.

Also, you must be grateful to those who guided and cared for you, and to those who supported you from behind.

As we conclude this 40-day evangelist training session, what I want to ask of you is to awaken. You did not know yourselves. However, from the moment you understood the will, you have come knocking on this door with a heart of awakening. You must realize that you are a nation that will pass through history, transcend the times, and build the future.

It may seem that I am awakening myself, but in reality, God is making me aware. Countless prophets and sages shed their blood to create my present self, and even now, they hope that I will become self-aware. Here, what else must you feel? You must feel that you are a being that has ruined history, is ruining it, and has the potential to ruin it. You must realize that you carry the resentment of the original Adam and Eve on your shoulders and that you must take responsibility for both the present and the future.

Even if you awaken, do not center your awareness on your personal desires; rather, you must awaken for heaven and earth, for the nation and for all humanity. You must recognize that you are a debtor to history, a descendant of traitors, and a being that possesses all elements of unfilial piety and disloyalty. Because I am a descendant of Adam and Eve, their disloyalty and betrayal are my disloyalty and betrayal.

Let us fulfill the duty of loyalty and filial piety.
The phrases of loyalty and filial piety inspire us. We must remain as heavenly kin. We must never forget that we are unfaithful and unfilial. Every time we feel that we are unfaithful and unfilial, we must call ourselves loyal and filial and vow to be loyal, even if it means falling down. The reason you stand here is not because you are great, but because the Father has called you, despite your unfaithfulness and unfilial actions. How can we repay this debt?

If you feel this way, you cannot be a loser in any position. How can you be defeated when you are seen as a loyal subject despite being unfilial, and as a filial child despite being disloyal? If you awaken and vow to atone for the history of unfaithfulness, unfilial actions, and betrayal before heaven, even if it means mobilizing spirits or having the Father Himself step in, He will provide the foundation for victory. When I become self-aware, I can receive blessings from the Father, who has mourned, felt lonely, and sighed.

Thus, the self-aware me is the one who bears responsibility for the will. Therefore, from now on, do not forget the relationship between the world, heaven and earth, the Father, and yourself. Until now, God has not had sovereignty, territory, or people. I am the one who has ruined all of this. Nevertheless, the purpose of establishing me in this way is to restore what has been ruined through me.

We have nothing to boast about. We have only ruined the sovereignty, people, and territory of heaven. Now we must reflect on ourselves for having sold and violated the sovereignty, territory, and people of heaven through disloyalty and unfilial actions. We must reflect on our betrayals. Even amidst sorrow, we must have a clear conviction to restore the sovereignty, people, and territory of heaven. Everything we eat, live, and die for must be for this purpose.

When you leave this place and take your first step, tears, hope, and earnestness must overflow. Otherwise, you are still in a state of forgetfulness. Wherever you may be, you must have a common heart.

Each of you must start toward the three thousand li of this land. You must be loyal and fight for this land, this nation, and this sovereignty. Since the unfilial and disloyal actions are also part of myself, I must be the one to turn back. Everything we do—walking the path, eating, sleeping, fighting—must be for this purpose. We must be loyal until the end. We must repent. We must do this not for heaven, but for the land, the nation, and the sovereignty of hope. The time for repenting, being loyal, and being filial for heaven has passed.

So what should we do? We must be loyal and filial for the land, the nation, humanity, and sovereignty. If we awaken, it is a time when the Father can forget all disloyalty, unfilial actions, and betrayals, so repent on behalf of the nation, repent on behalf of the territory, and repent on behalf of the sovereignty. The time for repenting for the Father has passed.

We must repent for the land. Thousands and millions of saints are still waiting. We must repent to restore the sovereignty and territory of heaven. We have chosen you to restore the people of heaven, the territory of heaven, and the sovereignty of heaven. Therefore, if you do not do well, you will follow in the footsteps of Adam and Eve, but if you do well, you will meet the day of victory.

The hope of heaven rests on our shoulders. We must establish the sovereignty of heaven in the nation, humanity, and the universe. God is looking forward to you becoming self-aware and leaving behind achievements of victory. That is none other than restoring the lost people, territory, and sovereignty of heaven.

This nation is asleep and unaware. They do not know how they are, how the territory is, or how the sovereignty is. We must awaken them to the fact that we must establish the lost nation, lost territory, and lost sovereignty before the universe. We must make them recover it at the cost of our lives.

Let us repent and strive for the sovereignty of heaven.
We must awaken to the mission of repenting and striving to find the heavenly nation, territory, and sovereignty, and we must realize that we have this mission as heavenly warriors. From the moment the teacher became aware of his responsibility, he lived only for this purpose, whether asleep or awake. You must be able to say, "Who can take away my awakened vow?" Please leave with such a vow and conviction. Since we have the responsibility to awaken this nation that is unaware, I ask you to fight with pride and strength.

You must first abandon the notion of ownership of the self. You must thoroughly recognize that you are a collective possession that transcends your individual self. If heaven has called you, you must wish to be used regardless of time and place. With this awareness, please fight for the Father, humanity, and heaven and earth.

You must learn to fight against yourself. You must coldly question yourself, "Where will this eye, this foot, this hand be used?" There must be something to leave for your descendants. Otherwise, you must gather comrades. If you go out like this, you can accomplish anything.

The path you walk is only promised with victory. Now, I hope you will become those who awaken others, passing through the position of being self-aware. With this awareness, please leave this place.

Let the tears, sweat, and blood that will remain as tradition flow.
<Summary of the Message> Thoroughly recognize that you are one family centered on God. 

The heart represents heaven, and the body represents earth. Therefore, knowing that heaven and earth are centered on me, I must live a life that serves as an offering for the sake of heaven and earth, to save the greater self.

To establish our oneness, God has endured unjust circumstances. This is to establish the greater self. Know that the center of heaven and earth is yourself. Recognize that you are not for the individual but for heaven and earth.

Some may have come to this place without conviction. Just as the mistakes of Adam and Eve became the mistakes and sorrows of all humanity, our mistakes are the same.

We must transcend individual consciousness. We cannot eat, drink, and act for the individual. Everything must be done on behalf of heaven and earth.

Raising children must be done to create such people. You must understand that it is to create cosmic victors and valuable beings.

There are countless practitioners in the world wandering in suffering. Therefore, when you wake up in the morning… think of your kin. Is there anyone suffering from persecution?

We are public beings. Public beings must transcend the past, present, and future. We must be able to boast as public beings.

If one’s value is not determined, heaven and earth cannot be mobilized. We must be a model before all future generations. The ideology of unification will be determined by how we are. God has believed in us and established us. We have value.
It is not something that has been established. Therefore, the manner of our departure determines our fate.  
Our family members across South Korea are currently starving. Grit your teeth and push through adversity. The spirits of the ancestors in the spirit world are also watching this and feel indignant and resentful. We must harbor animosity while thinking of the day of revenge. When thinking of such things, one should become someone who weeps even while eating.  
We must become heavenly people. All of humanity is hanging on us. God intends to treat you based on the standards He has blessed and the responsibilities He has placed upon you. After receiving grace in a vertical sense, you must establish expectations in a horizontal sense.  
The Father is a pitiful figure. Because of the name "Father," He has walked a miserable path. That Father has come as a sacrifice for history.  
We are the embodiment of historical hope. However, we must lament that we have become unable to give thanks and praise.  
The Father has fought for us. We must abandon our notions about ourselves. Each person must strike their own body and discipline themselves before letting go.  
We must not forget that we must practice the heavenly tradition—holding the heart of the Father in our minds and being in the position of servants in our bodies. We must possess the heart of a true owner.  
We must not view the universe and nature indifferently. We must have a heart that can embrace and sing to nature. We must know how to hold nature with the heart of true parents and true owners and whisper to it. When we live with this heart, embracing all of heaven and earth, we become heavenly people.  
The heart must act with the heart of parents, and the body must act as a servant to become an owner. This is God's legacy. This can only be obtained by shedding tears, sweat, and boiling blood with the heart of the Father.  
To become a true leader, one must receive true guidance. Do not shed tears for your own sake. You must inherit the tears, sweat, and blood of the true parents who walk the path of heaven.  
There must be no disobedience to heaven's commands. If you are told to go to the North, you must go. Blessings must be taken from the enemy's land. Our blessings are received as a promise.  
The family of Adam was to unite around three sons, regardless of their strengths or weaknesses. It is not a matter of being knowledgeable or ignorant. The second family is always central. Centering on Hyo-won, the third family and the first family must move with the second family as the focus.  
Until now, the parents have given commands, but now we must move according to the commands of those who have inherited the parents' commands.  
From now on, we are substantial brothers. In the family of Adam, there were the eldest brother—Cain, the second—Abel, and the third—Seth. This is a brotherhood in both vertical and horizontal senses. Now, we must establish someone to command in place of the father among the brothers.  
Those who wish to be high will be brought low. This is the principle of the family. A person who governs ten must prepare a place for ten to lie down and jump. This means that the land must be prepared to establish the Israelite nation.  
Those who criticize their brothers must split their bellies. The elder must have the heart of the parents.  
To take on responsibility means to stand in the position of parents, and to serve means to stand in the position of children. The more the younger sibling obeys the elder, the blessings given to the elder become the younger sibling's. The one who says they will take on the responsibilities of the entire family will receive blessings.  
Hyo-won must weep several times a day. I hope to stand in a position where I do not have to ask for forgiveness again because of those who have been established.  
The teacher is a person who succeeded in one generation. You must leave many connections of tears you have shed throughout the mountains and rivers. The extent of your loyalty to the will determines how good of a child will come forth.  
We did not hold a horizontal oath ceremony. When commanding in the name of the Father, anyone must obey absolutely.  
When you treat others with more sincerity than your trusted teacher or your parents, public sentiment will turn around.  
**The Heart Regarding the Will**  
<Summary of the Words> People on earth have gone through their life journeys without knowing it. Yet, they have lived with their own centered hopes and purposes. My individual self is extremely small, but behind me is history, a realistic environment, and a future world. We must not forget this. Humanity has lived in lamentation until now and continues to live in lamentation. In the midst of this, we have fought while envisioning hope, happiness, and freedom. Humanity has struggled throughout history to solve this problem, but it has not yet been resolved. So can you confidently say that you have become the victor on behalf of heaven and earth?  
All people on earth value their parents, themselves, siblings, tribes, and humanity. However, in reality, the parents, oneself, siblings, tribes, and humanity that are considered precious are not truly precious beings. You do not have true parents, true selves, true siblings, true tribes, or true humanity. What could be more unfortunate than this? This is the position you are in. You are a pitiful and unfortunate group that cannot have eternal ideals. You must understand this fact to establish true and precious values.  
You must be able to assert that you can clear away this unfortunate environment and step forward as an infinitely happy person. God has infinitely hoped for the day when this will happen. We must find everything we have lost again. When the false parents, self, siblings, tribes, and humanity become true parents, self, siblings, tribes, and humanity, then a true world will emerge. Even Noah, Abraham, Moses, and Jesus, who have come and gone in the past, did not have true siblings. That is why they have been lamenting until now.  
From a value perspective, you are in a position to welcome true parents, who are the embodiment of God's 6,000 years of heart and hope, and to establish a connection as children of true parents. Therefore, every finger and hair on your body is historical, epochal, and future-oriented. In other words, you are in a solemn position to be the ancestors of a new era.  
Your eyes must look through the eyes of true parents and true brothers, the eyes of true champions. Also, you must stand in an unwavering position that does not change regardless of the past, present, or future. If you cannot do this, the past, present, and future will all be shaken. While people in the world have lived this way in the past and are living this way now, you must stand in an absolute position regardless of how the times move. You must firmly establish your position before God. If that position changes, you cannot stand in a straight line with God. No matter what suffering you endure, you must stand firm and unchanging. The more severe the persecution, the more difficult the environment, the more you must solidify your position and call upon the Father, the subject of your heart, with a sincere heart. Only then will God be with you, and your foundation will become even more solid.  
The circumstances of everyone gathered here today are different. You, who have come together from such different environments, must receive training in one place and then return to the battlefield. What will you use to establish an unchanging heart? It must be established with the heart of the Father. The condition to present before God in heaven is not having done well, but having the heart regarding the will.  
We must hate those who have created a history of resentment in the restoration history, but in terms of heart, we must surpass anyone in history. Even if our physical achievements are less than theirs, we must surpass them in the vertical heart. In the past, it was difficult to establish a vertical heart connection and the value of calling upon the Father was different. Even if you go out to evangelize in your local area, if you cannot establish a center and go back and forth, no one will follow you. Even in prayer and work, you must justify their position from an unchanging position and establish your own position. Only then can you understand the heart of Adam, Noah, Abraham, and Moses. This way, no advocate of any doctrine or leader can block the path of our unified warriors.  
We exist for a purpose, and if we do not fulfill our mission, eating and sleeping will become burdensome. Even when you encourage each other as brothers, it must be done with the heart of praying centered on future hope. If we are to stand in the position of heavenly warriors, we must silently subdue the enemy. To do so, we must go to the battlefield with God's heart at all times. If we do this, even if Satan appears before you, just as he appeared before Adam and Jesus, he will not appear in a three-dimensional way but in a two-dimensional way.  
Just like the three great tests of Jesus, Satan tests with heart, substance, and words. Therefore, to overcome that test, first, you must have the historical heart that God had toward fallen Adam and Eve, second, you must have the words of the Father that subdue Satan, and third, you must have the substance of Jesus. Whether the period of persecution before you is long or short will be determined by how firmly your heart and substance are established.  
The training you are receiving is to defeat the enemy before you and to judge the enemy. To do this, first, you must study the word. Where does this word come from? It comes from the heart at the time of creation and has gone through the path of restoration. You must not forget this fact. Without the word, you cannot establish substance, and without establishing substance, you cannot establish heart, so when you listen to the word, you must listen with your body, heart, and spirit.  
You will undergo a physically exhausting training that has never been seen throughout history. You must endure and overcome it with the word and heart. You must learn from Adam, learn from Moses, learn from Jesus, learn from the teacher, and stand in the position of Adam, Noah, Abraham, Moses, Jesus, and the teacher, and your word, body, and heart must become one to experience the heart of God. If you win in the internal struggle to unify the word and body, God cannot help but recognize you. We must always be able to say, "Please give me the hardest tasks."  
Any gathering or organization that can receive God's blessing must know the circumstances of hunger and starvation and must not change in the face of external threats of death (Satan's forces). They must be able to fight boldly for God and be willing to die. You are a blessed group, so you must have a living history of fighting and winning without yielding to any path of suffering to lead this nation on behalf of God.  
The training you will receive this time is the first phase. In the second phase, you must undergo training that does not yield even in the face of hunger and the fear of death before this nation, and in the third phase, you must undergo such training before the world, and in the fourth phase, before the spirit world. You must be able to say, "I am a child of God." You must not have a worldly character but must possess the heart of God and represent the heart of the Father. To do this, you must shed many tears. You must become the owner of all things with a heart that can truly caress nature around you. Do not let any worries linger for more than three hours or three days, and pray to avoid falling into Satan's tests. And when facing the injustices of good people, you must have a passionate sense of indignation.

When you say you have become the owner, each person must rearrange their own flowerbed centered on themselves. From now on, when you bless, it will be as it is. God intends to give you such authority. You must be able to call yourself a priest by going through the process of offering with the heart of parents and the body of a servant.

Restoration of Humanity Starts with Me
<Summary of the Message> God always starts the restoration of humanity from one person. In other words, it begins with a representative of one person. The success of any nation is affected by my individual issues, and the success of humanity is also affected by my individual issues. When my individual self stands as a substantial purpose before the whole, a new history begins. 
If there is a will of God that must be fulfilled, there must be a master to carry out this will. Achieving the divine purpose means achieving the purpose of all creation, humanity, and individuals. You have been called by the great master, so you must become a substantial being that can sing the same value from the past through the present to the future. When that happens, the will I hold will not only be my will but also the will of the Father. 
The will is one. The circumstances and environments of individuals may differ, but ultimately the flow of the whole is one. Until now, there has been no individual, nation, or country that has maintained an unchanging heart regarding the overall will, transcending individual environments and circumstances. The nation of Israel transcended its national issues, but it did not inherit God's will on a national level. It should have transcended the national scope but failed to do so. However, God will surely find one person who can fulfill the purpose and will seek nations, countries, and the world. 
On July 4, 1961, in Gyeonggi-do, Ju-an. 
* This message is organized from the publication of <Seonghwa> No. 17 (dated June 2, 1962).

Then what kind of person will God seek to bless and fulfill the purpose of creation? To which individual, family, nation, or country will this mission be entrusted? This is something that all humanity must pay the price for under a common goal. We must pay the personal price, the family price, and the national price. For the past 6,000 years, countless people have suffered, but no one has paid the price of suffering for victory. 
Now, for all humanity to receive blessings, we must pay a price and receive the price of overall victory. To do this, all humanity must unite and come together to confront this task. What must we do to obtain the happiness of all humanity, not just individuals? What kind of indemnity or price must individuals, families, nations, and any sovereign state pay to obtain this? If there is a nation that has paid the price and sought it, that nation will become the chosen people. 
The name Israel is a great blessing given by God. When we unite and say, "We offer this to you, so use it for global value," God will grant the name Israel. Our greatest hope is to receive blessings. The blessing of Israel will not come simply by sitting idly. To enter into the blessing of Israel, we must be those who are willing to overcome countless trials, both personally and as families. Thus, we must go through an era of shedding blood personally, shedding blood as families, and shedding blood nationally. And to become a heavenly people, we must kneel before God. We must be able to shed the same tears, the same blood, and the same sweat. Those who are to be sacrificed must not have the concept of ownership centered around themselves. 
Having gone through the path of individual restoration and the path of family restoration, we are no longer the past selves we were. 
If we have carried the burden of debt or worry, we must release it. Often, when releasing a heavy burden, we do not know how to start. If we do not know the method, we must learn the skills to release it. What skills must we learn? We must learn the skills to operate a crane. Whether we release it this way or that way, it is the same, but we must learn the method that can release the burden quickly. We must release this burden as quickly as possible, even if it means giving our lives. To release the burden in the time of the Second Coming, we must devise a method different from the past. 
All people at the end are the greatest debtors, the greatest wanderers, and the saddest. The only thing that can solve these is the heart. Only with a heart that can establish a relationship with the rich can it be resolved. The essence of truth cannot be separated from the heart. When the heart becomes one with the Father, one can become a true filial child. The Israelite people did not know this secret to releasing such a great burden. This is the heart that Jesus and the Holy Spirit could not express. To cross over the peak of this heart, we must create a road that can cross over that peak. 
The place where the will of hope remains is the foundation of the heart. 
Today, the world is divided into two camps. The ideology of communism cannot be an ideology where the hearts of the people of the world can rest. No matter how excellent an airplane is, it cannot land without an airport. However, God has already prepared that foundation. It is the duty of those who walk the path of virtue to develop the wellspring of the heart that can connect with God for humanity, who are weary and lonely without a master. 
You must take responsibility for all the mistakes of your historical ancestors. The one who comes with a receipt after paying the price before any Satan in heaven and earth is the Lord of the Second Coming. From now on, I can say that my tears are historical tears, my sweat is historical sweat, and my blood is historical blood. The one who comes to turn God's historical sighs into hope and joy is the Lord of the Second Coming, the Messiah. 
We must become victorious Israelites. We must fight until the historical enemy, Satan, opens his mouth and admits that he has become the defeated one. 
We must understand that obtaining the name Israel is not an easy task. 
If God loved humanity, on what basis did He love? God has been working throughout history to love humanity, but He has not yet fulfilled the purpose of creation and has not gained even one beloved son or daughter. 
If you wish to receive God's love, you must not be afraid to bear the burden of the cross that comes to you. We must be able to say, "Thank you, God, for living for Your purpose for thousands of years." Facing the destiny of having to repay the debts we owe, we must cut off the ties of wealth and brotherhood we have with Satan. You must fulfill the mission of a historical representative. If the priests at the time of Jesus had shouted to the people of Israel, "Look at the Lamb of God who carries the burdens of the world. You too must become the Lamb who carries the burdens of the world," the will would have already been fulfilled. 
From today onward, we must settle everything. Even when releasing burdens, we must do it in a way different from the past. All burdens must be released from the heart and from the family of Adam. Before us lie the historical deeds left by Adam, Abraham, Moses, and Jesus. The word can be known through the substance, and the substance can be known through the heart. And through the heavenly foundation, we can know the three-dimensional world. To receive the word, we must put forth the utmost sincerity. The body must become a sacrifice, and the heart must become one with God. If our nation has been chosen to receive such blessings, we must do our best to fulfill our responsibilities. Only then can we receive the cosmic blessings permitted by God. We must understand that we have the responsibility and mission to release the historical debts and burdens, and we must not be negligent in fulfilling such duties. 
Individuals must become the foundation of families, families must become the foundation of nations, nations must become the foundation of countries, countries must become the foundation of the world, and the world must become the foundation of heaven and earth. In this time when individuals, families, nations, and the world are being called, where do we stand and where are we headed? Now is the time to go for the nation. Since I possess cosmic value, I must have the heart to offer myself entirely before the Father. 
Do not forget that God is in a more miserable and pitiful position than you. Do not forget that you are in debt. Do not lose the standard of the heart and align yourself with the leader and your environment. I hope you will be serious as if you are negotiating prayers while placing individuals, families, nations, and the world on the table. 
3 times 7 is 21; let’s grit our teeth and move forward during the 21 days of wilderness. With this standard, suffer for 40 days, 1 year, or even 3 years. This is to create a foundation that can move God to tears and suppress Satan. Let’s take back the world of Satan as the price of suffering for these 3 years. If God were to ask, "What will you pay to receive blessings?" we must be able to respond, "With burning love."
