Become an Indispensable Group
<Summary of the Message> We are not a group trying to solve the problems of any individual or organization, but a group that aims to fulfill the responsibilities bestowed by the Creator by resolving the issues of heaven and earth through the history of the past, present, and future. To do this, we must subdue both visible and invisible beings. We must establish three or more supporters among our close associates on this earth. Even among ourselves, we must not proceed without having the backing of at least three. We must form vertical and horizontal expectations, feeling that while I am an individual, there is a historical backing behind me. In doing so, we must say, "What I cannot do, please take responsibility for it, God." 
The Israelite people only looked at the human aspect, the flat aspect, and did not realize that God had been working historically behind the scenes. While it would be a blessing to enter and prosper in Canaan, the greater purpose was to defeat the enemies in the land of Canaan. The Israelite people forgot that they should praise their ancestors and God. Even if they lay in the fields dressed in ragged clothes, the issue was to repay God's enemies. The greater hope was to repay the enemies on this earth rather than personal desires. 
The Israelite people should have been filled with animosity towards their enemies. They should have repaid the enemies and then returned to Egypt. 
Today, what Christians around the world must do is for denominations to gather and counterattack against the enemies. However, Christians do not understand this. They do not have animosity or resentment towards the enemies. God and I, the whole and the individual must unite. Fallen humans may temporarily unite, but they cannot unite eternally. God wishes to gather all humanity into one, even if it takes a thousand years or ten thousand years. Although humans may have fallen, anyone with a conscience admires God. 
The unification of the Israelite people is not only necessary under the leadership but also in the wilderness, in defeating the seven nations of Canaan, and beyond. You must become one. You must strive to unite day and night until the enemies are defeated. 
We must have a leader who can lead us for a thousand years and ten thousand years, entrusting all our circumstances and hopes to him. No matter how excellent the leaders in the world may be, they are not such leaders. A true leader is one who represents God and the heavenly principles to fulfill that will on earth. 
The Voice Crying in the Wilderness
You have come through tearful circumstances. God led the Israelite people into the wilderness not to let them fall and die but to unite them in loneliness. They should have been able to ask where Moses had gone if he was out of sight for even a moment. A person who has no one to share their heart with, no one to entrust their worries to, is a sad person. You must be able to say, "God! I will be with you even on the path of sin, suffering, and sorrow. Who can sever the bond between you and me?" 
The group God is seeking is an indispensable group. We must become indispensable individuals and indispensable families. Even if we appear as beggars, God is seeking an indispensable group. Therefore, now a new nation, a new Israel, and a new world are needed. God wants to connect you to restore the world. God demands indispensable individuals, families, and nations. Although the Israelite people established the 12 tribes and 70 elders, they could not remain as such a group, and only the courageous Joshua and Caleb remained. 
Even while holding onto the dead Jesus, we must be able to say, "Lord! We can do it," and even while starving to death, we must be able to maintain our integrity. It is human nature to forget the past when circumstances improve. It is easy to forget the grace received. The unified members must become an indispensable group before the 30 million people of our nation, before all humanity, and before heaven and earth. Without a center, all will deviate and conflict, but with God the Father as the center, there is unity. You must be a person who fears that the eternal bond with the center may be broken. 
In the Book of Life, those who can say that they will live forever with all humanity and remain unchanged are recorded. Even if the world changes and my body is covered in blood, we cannot change. Jesus, even in the face of death, only wanted to be with the Father, both in life and after death. Esau and Jacob were separated, and Jacob's two sons and ten sons were separated, leading to the division of the North and South, resulting in the global phenomenon we see today. 
We must become the Israelites who have come out of the wilderness. If we are the Israelites in Egypt, we cannot enter Canaan. Among you now are those who have come out into the wilderness.
there are still groups that remain directly under oppression. The group in the wilderness must attack the city of Amalek. We must fight both internally and externally. Only then can we hear the cries of historical mission bearers and communicate directly with God.

We must be with God, Jesus, and the Holy Spirit for eternity, but that place is not in glory. We must be together in a place of poverty, anger, and suffering. From the day we hold hands, we must have the hope of being together forever. In such a place, death is not a problem. Our ancestors forsook the Father in such places, but we, who have been entrusted with the mission at the end of history, must resolve the grief caused by our ancestors. We must become an indispensable group.

We are lacking. However, Heaven wants to recognize us with the standards of value like Adam, Noah, Abraham, and Jesus. No matter how hard we work and accumulate results, if it is not done in unity with the Father, Satan will take it away. Your hearts must always be with the Father. A loyal subject is one who is always with the king.

God has placed us today on the foundation of the sacrifices of the prophets of the past and is hoping for us. We want to be together, and we must be together, but we cannot do so without defeating the enemy. We must understand God's heart that tells us to go. That is because there is an enemy. If God could judge directly, He would have done so 6,000 years ago. Judgment is carried out through people. Until now, humanity has not understood this fact.

The path of the willing sacrifice
God commands based on His will, and to repay the enemy, He commands in a place where blood flows. This time, even young people are going out for evangelism. Young people, you must go out with the conviction to defeat the enemy that used to mock young people in the past. You must know and be grateful that the Father has also gone through such places. We must always remember that the Father is with us. When that heart moves within us, we can heal the sick and do anything. This year, there will be less persecution than last year. We must align with the external times and rhythms.

You are fighting on behalf of the historical ancestors until now. The enemy comes through sovereignty and power, then through material, and then through emotions. Therefore, you must go to places of hunger and loneliness. You must stand in a position that welcomes you, forgiving the position of the Israelite nation that betrayed in the past. We must understand that even if we want to be together, we cannot because we must repay the enemy. Our fight against the enemy is to allow all of humanity to be with the Father.

To be together, repaying the enemy is the issue. During this 40-day period, you must eat barley rice. You must become a sacrifice. A sacrifice must have no self-awareness or sense of ownership. We must go through the position of a servant, then the position of an adopted child, and then advance to the position of sons and daughters. Jesus went as a sacrifice. He wanted to become a priest, but due to the disbelief of the people, He became a sacrifice. The Lord of the Second Advent comes in the capacity of a priest, and then advances to the position of children.

On the morning of January 1, 1960, the teacher told you to stand in a position of serving for three years. During this summer's evangelism period, the number of mobilized circuit members is 102, including district leaders, regional leaders, general circuit members, and special circuit members. If these 102 members are on circuit for 40 days, it amounts to 4,080 times. With the heart of a parent and the body in the position of a servant, let us become sacrifices with blood, sweat, and tears, take on the responsibility of atonement in the position of priests, and advance to the position of sons and daughters to become representatives of the Father and judge Satan.

This is our motto, our practice.

As sons and daughters with the heart of the Father, you must shed blood, sweat, and tears. You must wet the path with blood, sweat, and tears, and connect towns with blood, sweat, and tears.

Become a person with attachment to the land
<Summary of the message> Now you are about to leave after completing the 40-day training. Please take a moment to think about how much you have changed from when you came to the training. The greater the difference between the character that Heaven desires and your actual self, the more you should feel your own shortcomings. However, even if you feel that your current self is lacking and you have no results, if your determination to walk this path is firm, there is no need to hesitate. Parents will listen more to the child who calls out with a sense of inadequacy than to the confident child.

We have nothing, but if we unite, there is nothing we cannot accomplish. I must have the conviction that I am a son or daughter of the Father. The good, the bad, and the disabled are all children of the Father. If you feel lacking when you go out to the local area, you must supplement it emotionally. If you aimed for 100 but only achieved 50, you must fill the remaining 50 with a heart of gratitude and remorse.

I hope you will fight with the heart that says, "Though I am lacking and insufficient, I have not lost in heart."

Heaven does not cooperate based on any results or qualifications. Heaven cooperates based on the heart. Therefore, you must go out with a prayerful heart, saying, "You have called and established the lacking ones, so please hold us."

You are pioneers before this nation, and you are those who bear responsibility before God, so you must have attachment. This nation, which has tarnished the name of Jesus, must correct its mistakes and take responsibility, especially the Christians. You must have attachment to serve Heaven and Earth beyond yourselves. Originally, the name Israel was obtained from serving Heaven rather than oneself.

Now, what should you have attachment to? Today, humanity has lost attachment to any existing ideology or thought. They have lost attachment to any religion or ideology, and even to any nation with sovereignty. They are even losing attachment to themselves. The ideology that can conquer and dominate the world in the future must be based on attachment and love, saying, "You and I cannot help but be connected."

In the Principle of Restoration, it is said that Heaven, Earth, and even God are filled with sorrow. I hope that the 7th training participants will become people with attachment. This land was our land from the beginning, but our ancestors lost the qualifications of sons and daughters, and thus we lost it for 6,000 years. Now, we must reclaim this land. We must hold on to this land and weep. Until now, humanity has lived by digging into the land, but how many truly had attachment to the land? We must have true attachment to the land, whether it is 3,000 ri or the globe. As citizens of a new era, should we trample on the land and things that God has painstakingly created for us? This land is a relic that the Father has created for me, and I must have a fervent attachment to inherit it. We must treat all things and the land with the love that the Father had when He created the land.

Today, the mountains and fields of Korea are bare. We must be deeply shocked by this. Someday, our plans must be put into action. The land cannot become fertile with just fertilizer. We must cultivate this land with love as if we were treating our own children. Have you not heard the story of the 60-year-old elder of the Yamok Church who cultivated the land with love, heartfelt prayers, and tears, and reaped a great harvest? We must cultivate with such tears and heart.

We have three sets of parents. God is a parent, the land is a parent, and the one who gave birth to our physical bodies is a parent. The center of all these parents is God. Therefore, God is the highest being. You must love the land now. After that, you must love the people. You must love the people more than any historical sovereign and embrace the land and humanity with attachment.

God has worked to establish material in place of the land and people in place of Heaven. Today, this land desires to become fertile under the love of its owner, so you must have more attachment to the land than anyone else and do what our ancestors could not do.

Now, we must strive with attachment to the land, sovereignty, and life. The rewards that come from there must be a source of pride to offer to God the Father. Wherever you go, whatever you do, you must become a person whom God can treat with attachment.

Let us become representatives of God
I traveled all over South Korea and returned after five days. I went through Daejeon, Jeonju, Gwangju, Masan, then through Daegu to Samcheok, and then passed through Jecheon to Chuncheon and returned.

What I felt during this tour
What I felt during this tour is that now is the time for us to fight. Seeing the great resolve of our young men and women in the local areas, I believe that the struggles of this period will bring victorious results. However, what saddened me this time was that our members walk hundreds of ri to the places where the teacher says he will go. While worldly people can travel by car because they have money, they do not want to come here, but our Unification Church youth walk hundreds of ri to come. When I went to Gwangju, I heard that they walked day and night for 2-3 days from Mokpo or Muan. Seeing this, I felt that the goals and intentions of our church will be realized.

They are people who, for the sake of the time and purpose that God desires, throw themselves into action without caring about their own difficulties and overcome any hardships. They are not people with social experience. They are also not people bound by personal circumstances or knowledge. When I see young people around 20 years old who are unknowingly prepared to dedicate their lives for the purpose, they look so admirable. There are many such members.

Generally, they have more spirit than the young people here at the headquarters. When comparing the members from Seoul and Gyeonggi Province, who are centered around the headquarters, with you who are present here, they have a spirit that you cannot match in terms of their earnest hearts towards God and their loyalty to follow His will. I felt that if you do not take responsibility, they will step over you and fulfill that responsibility.

After going through the tour, my throat is quite sore. I spoke for about three to four hours at each place and talked all night with the members I met for the first time.

Once, there was an incident. I was supposed to arrive in Samcheok at 9 PM, but the car broke down on the way, and I arrived the next day at 4:40 AM. Just imagine how long the Samcheok members must have waited! I was exhausted. We had a meeting in the early morning, but the security in Donghae was strict, so we couldn't talk for long. After about an hour, I went to Wonju and then to Chuncheon, and this morning I met you.

What do you think the teacher was thinking and what kind of prayer was he making during such times? This year, our young members are going out on evangelism under the teacher's command and are struggling to realize God's will as a shared mission. In fact, there were very difficult things. While worrying about such things, I prayed to understand your difficulties and to take them on myself. So, I even spent a night outside.

The local members and we are one family. We are one bloodline. We are all indispensable people. Even if it is the first time meeting a member, you will feel that you share the same heart. That is what Unification Church members desire. We are using a noun that is easily misunderstood in the world, which is "family."

In fact, we are family. Literally, we are family. Even if we say just one word to a member we meet for the first time, we understand each other. We are closer than worldly relatives, and we can share our feelings and talk openly. If we have a sincere wish, we can express that wish and ask for help. This is a natural connection that cannot be achieved through any means, method, or planned organization. This is a natural phenomenon. It is a connection formed around God without our knowledge. This connection is linked to God.

If there is a group that moves based on this connection, that group cannot be broken by anyone. Not even Satan can do it, and people cannot either. Only God can break it. So, when will God break this connection? It is when you go wrong. Remember that it is when you go wrong that the connection is broken.

Emotional local members
If there are any regional leaders attending here, please raise your hands. Regional leaders near Seoul, you know the situation at the headquarters well, and if I want to see you, I can go meet you by jeep. However, in going out centered on God, it does not matter if you know each other well. Being close and being able to meet is not what is important. The closer you are and the more responsible you are, the stricter and more significant your responsibilities must be. Regional leaders near the headquarters have more important responsibilities.

The members scattered in the local areas should be kept close to the headquarters, while those near the headquarters should be sent to the farthest ends of Jeju Island or Ulleungdo, or even to the southernmost tip of Africa, which is the teacher's heart.

If you have taken on responsibility, you must be able to bear it. You must also take pride in what you have taken responsibility for and know it as an honor. Is that right? Would you like that or not?

From now on, when difficult things happen in the Unification Church, you must not leave it to the local members. For the teacher's commands to be conveyed to the local members, they must go through several stages. How pitiful the local members are! If you look at those near Seoul, they are all slick and smooth. The female students probably all use at least cream. The male students over there probably do too. It seems likely.

If you go down to the southern part of Jeolla Province, there are also our members. They are also family like you and me. However, in terms of heart, they are more earnest and ahead of you. The teacher quietly observes that the members at the headquarters are said to be fighting because of the smooth girls, and I hope these slick members from Seoul get to experience hardship.

Among these slick members from Seoul, there are many who think, "What does it matter what the purpose is? When did I ever know the teacher? Does the Unification Church live or die because of me?" 

From the perspective of national destiny, global destiny, or heavenly fortune,
Of course, realistically, one might have more possessions, perhaps a few coins in their wallet, or someone behind them who can prove and protect them, but those things are not the problem. The person itself is the issue. A person who falls apart at the slightest difficulty may become successful in their desired field when they enter society. However, when it comes to designing and completing a grand, universal, and heavenly ambition without leaning or tilting towards one side, such a person cannot be used. Rather, a trustworthy rural person, even if their face is dark, is much better. They say, "If others want to see, let them see; if they want to speak, let them speak; if the sun sets, let it set." 

When it comes to working for a purpose, everyone raises their hands, but when it comes to the Seoul tightwads, no one raises their hand even when asked. If we look at the percentages, these Seoul tightwads are in the negative. Therefore, they should be treated as special cases and educated. The family members in the provinces are better than you who are in headquarters. You are these people, and the family members in the provinces are those people. I think so. Is this a good thought or a bad thought?

You all come here, which takes less than a day, with makeup on your faces and dressed in nice clothes, indulging in luxury, but they have feelings that explode from within themselves. The flood of feelings that flows from them is tremendous. You cannot withstand it. So, if you are not careful, you will be pushed out. 

Training begins in a place of hardship. If God exists, to whom do you think He would be more inclined: to those who eat well and live well or to those who do not? When someone asks, "Did you eat?" and they say, "Yes, I ate yesterday, I will eat today, and I will eat tomorrow," God’s heart would lean more towards someone who says, "I saw food yesterday..." Since they haven't even seen food, it is certain they haven't eaten. Even if I were God, I would feel more for those who cannot eat. God would feel sorry for those who cannot eat.

Anyone who wishes to live eternally enjoying the law of conscience and justice would want to be close to those living in such difficult circumstances and would try to protect such people. This is a principle of heaven. 

Therefore, if a true parent exists and has a plan to make their child a global figure, from what position should they send that child? First, they must be trained, but they should not be trained to eat well. Training should not start with eating well, playing well, or fighting well. They should be trained to overcome not eating, not playing, and doing what others dislike. 

Ah! I don't mind not eating. I can eat barley rice. I can eat dog food. They must be able to say that. From the beginning to the end, from the lowest to the highest, they must be able to digest anything well. Only then can they become someone who can guide both the high and the low emotionally.

Looking at the leaders of our country today, they say one must graduate from university. However, many of them are frivolous. There are many who would fall over with a single blow to the chest. Such people are nothing compared to those who are innocent, uneducated, love the land, and live according to natural laws with conscience as their wealth. 

If God exists, who would inherit the great blessing of heavenly principles? Is it someone who boasts that they know everything? Absolutely not. It is given to the innocent. Look at history. The world’s great figures were born from those who shed blood and sweat with nature, loved the scent of nature, sang with nature as their friend, worried about their country, and lived with a certain ideology. The children born from such parents became great. That is why most great figures are from rural backgrounds. They were born in natural environments.

You all try to boast about even the smallest things, and boasting is good. However, boast when you are alone. "Hey, eyes! You are really handsome." "Of course, I am handsome." "Hey, ears! You are really cool." "I am handsome." "Hey, your face is handsome too." "Of course, it is." This is what I mean by boasting alone. If you invite God into it, it would be even better. "God! Thank you for making my eyes so beautiful. Thank you for making my ears so nice. My body is strong, and my face is handsome. Thank you for making all of this without any flaws as your son or daughter." God, being the Creator, would be very pleased with that. This is not a lie.

However, those who do not have the content to boast that would please God boast about themselves. That should not be the case. Therefore, the youth of the Unification Church must have the heart to boast while putting the Father in front. If they cannot do that, they should not boast. Just as there is day and night in a day, there is a period in a person's life where they appear unattractive. This period is like the night. However, when the night passes and it becomes morning and day, at that time, they must not pass any responsibility onto others.

Today, the world is still in the night period. It has not reached the time of day. Therefore, all of humanity should not be proud or elevate themselves. Humans think they have reached the day, but it is still night. That is why it is said to be gentle, humble, and go to a low position. However, once they receive God's command and take on responsibility, they must act with the utmost authority. No one should blame that person. If necessary, they must do it even if it means hitting their own body.

Humans are not yet in a position to boast about themselves, so they must train themselves in a humble position. Only after that should they boast about themselves. However, there may be people whose faces are in such a poor state, like a pumpkin in the backyard, that they have nothing to boast about. Yet, that does not mean that person has nothing to boast about. A heart of love is noble, so if they have a heart that is wider, deeper, and gentler than others, they can positively influence everyone they encounter. If they have such a heart, the Father will be with them directly.

The reason I say this is that when you, who are in Seoul, go to the provinces this summer, you should not be the kind of people who avoid hard work and dust off with your fingertips. You must take the opposite path. That is why I am saying this. Do you understand?

Just because there is a difference between you and the provincial members, you should not look down on them even a little. Rather, you should emulate them. Even if you go to work in the countryside, do not stand in a position of boasting when you meet them. When you meet children, you should embrace them and say, "Hey, you are really great!" and hold them close. When you go to the provinces, you will find many people who are quite unsightly. There are many who only boast about themselves. You should not boast about yourself but rather say, "You all are doing great!" while holding them and boasting about them. If you make them feel good, everything will connect.

What kind of being is God? If we consider God's attributes, He loves to boast. There is no one in the world who loves to boast as much as God. God's boasting is endless. Since He is the Creator, it is only natural. God loves to boast the most.

If you want to boast to the people in your neighborhood, you must have the courage to impress them both inside and out and then boast. Even if you look like a pumpkin or a fool, the people in the neighborhood will recognize you as a blessing. God makes it that way. God takes the most unattractive person and makes them more outstanding than the most attractive person and boasts before the townspeople. Therefore, if you want to boast, you must put the Father forward. Then it is okay. To boast, you must first say, "I want to boast, Father," and then do it. You must not do it alone. You must boast in the name of the Father.

God, who wants to boast even a little when humans do well. 

When you go out this time, you must boast. However, you must do it in the name of the Father. Although you may not know what the Father looks like, if you boast using only the Father’s name, even if you make a mistake, the Father will be pleased.

What I have felt while walking this path until now is that God wants to boast. However, when you have a heart of love, you naturally want to boast. The more you have great, wide, high, and deep love, the more you want to boast; that is the inherent feeling. Isn't that so? Most parents are like that. Even the beggar in the slum, who others do not even look at, says he would die for his children. That is a heart that flows from love, and it is because of that heart that he wants to boast.

If God had a heart that was more malicious and more ugly, like that of a devil, He would not have carried out the providential history of restoration for 6,000 years for fallen humans. However, because God is a God of love, He wants to boast, saying, "Look at my children," whenever humans do even a little well. When a family does a little well, He says, "Look at my beloved family," even making Satan acknowledge it. However, after boasting like that, if humans fail to live up to it, it all comes crashing down. If you boast about an individual and they fail, crash; if you boast about a family and they fail, crash; if you boast about the nation of Israel and they fail, crash; if you boast about Jesus and they fail, crash; that is how it crumbled.

Wanting to boast even a little is God's heart. Just like a parent's heart, God's heart is the same. Therefore, if you make Him happy even a little and do well, you can receive all His love. Knowing this, you should go out to experience what the Father wants to boast about. Do you understand? What are you going out to experience? To experience what can be boasted about? Yes, you must go out to experience what can be boasted about. Just as you earn money through business, you must create many things to boast about. What will happen if you have many things to boast about? Will God only boast to the 30 million people? He will boast before all people in the world and in the heavenly world. How grateful is that? Knowing this, I ask you to bring back many things that God can boast about. Do you understand?

What time did I say to come today? (The members respond it was 9 o'clock.) Then what time did I arrive here? (They respond it was 10:10.) Then that means I was 70 minutes late. In fact, someone who cannot keep a promise does not have the right to speak here. They do not have the right to speak. In that sense, I apologize to you. Knowing that, you all must keep time well in the future. (Due to poor recording conditions, the message could not be continued.)

The Israelite nation that disbelieved Jesus. 

At the wedding feast in Cana, when Jesus' mother Mary said there was no wine, He replied, "Woman, what does that have to do with me?" From a human perspective, she is His mother, but from the perspective of heavenly public law, she was an enemy. That is why Jesus could say such words. You may think, "That can't be true. What nonsense!" but it is the truth. Those are words said without understanding Jesus' heart. Do you understand? I would have done the same.

Jesus wanted to say to His disciples what He wanted to say to His parents. He also wanted to say it to His brothers. However, He could not and left home. How did He die later? He was accused of being a traitor to the nation and a destroyer of social order and was killed. How much did they hate Him that they would ask to exchange Him for the murderous robber Barabbas? The Jewish people considered Jesus their enemy. How tragic is that? You believe in Jesus, who died so tragically. Yet, they overlook all these facts and are eager to hear about His return in glory on the clouds to save them. They do not know what they should know, nor do they do what they should do, yet they say they will go to heaven? Heaven is not a place for such people.

The Israelite nation has been a nation of traitors for 4,000 years. The entire nation, including the priests, held onto Jesus and said, "Take me away. Do with me as you will, whether to kill me or to save me. If you say to go east, I will go east; if you say to go west, I will go west; if you say to go south, I will go south; if you say to go north, I will go north. If you tell me to jump into a pit, I will jump in." If they had said that, Jesus would not have died. He would have lived and unified the world. Moses was driven by God to conquer the seven nations of Canaan; would Jesus not have unified the world? However, Jesus died. If Jesus had not died, He would have taken the Israelite nation as an offering and become the High Priest centered on the special sanctuary given to Him. Thus, He would have unified the divided heaven and earth. He would have torn down the walls of sin between nations and the deep-rooted walls of sin in the hearts of all people and offered a sin offering.

If Jesus had offered the sin offering as the High Priest and placed all the world under His dominion, God's providential work would not have been extended for 2,000 years. However, all of this returned to failure. He could not take the Israelite nation as an offering, nor could He work centered on the temple. Because He could not be in the defiled temple, Jesus walked the path of sacrifice, which was from the Garden of Gethsemane to the top of Golgotha.

That is why Golgotha is the universal temple. You must understand this. Where is the universal temple? (They respond Golgotha.) Yes, it is Golgotha. Where is the universal resurrection ground? Golgotha. Where is the universal ground of death? Golgotha. Where is the place that decides life and death? Golgotha. After Jesus passed through Golgotha, it became the Holy Place and the Most Holy Place. You must understand this clearly.

After Jesus walked the path of Golgotha, all the temples, priests, and the Israelite nation in Judea became Satan's. They all must go to hell. They must go to the upper hell among the hells.

What is regrettable is that Judaism still remains on this earth. It is unbelievable that the Judaism that killed the Messiah has survived to this day, 2,000 years later... We must organize that with our own hands. The organization must not be done with force or power but according to reason.

Those who killed Jesus must be punished. The 600,000 Israelites who followed Moses also became food for crows in the wilderness when they betrayed Moses and God. Similarly, the Israelite nation that betrayed the universal leader Jesus is becoming food for crows on a global scale.

Now is the time to create a new organization. That is why the restoration movement is currently taking place. What will happen? You must be curious. In the future, there will be movements of a global Israel. It will be exciting. You must start with a secret weapon in your heart.

What was the motive for Israel's downfall? They fell because they were trying to do well. They thought, "Oh, I don't want to suffer; the Messiah must come." They believed that happiness would come from the day the Messiah arrived. However, what happened from the day the Messiah came? The Bible clearly states that there would be a seven-year great tribulation, engulfed in the flames of extreme suffering, just like the darkness before dawn.
These days, there are many delusional people who claim they will welcome the Lord as their bridegroom. There are many who want to welcome the Lord as their bridegroom without doing what they should be doing. Where is such nonsense? Do they know how the Lord, who comes as a bridegroom, comes, where He comes from, and what He likes? Do they know? Generally, there are all kinds of bridegrooms, including beggar bridegrooms. But are they trying to make the Lord into such a beggar bridegroom? Do they think they can welcome the Lord with such a shabby appearance? Those who commit robbery and do all sorts of things claim they will welcome the Lord as their bridegroom?

The Lord is the Prince of God. Are they trying to take the Prince of God and make Him into a bridegroom like themselves? What will they do with such a bridegroom? The Lord is someone who is embraced by God because He is good, and He is someone before whom all nations must bow their heads. The Lord is the one who encompasses the world, possessing the glory and virtue to move the world with just a fingertip. To serve such a being as a bridegroom, one must become greater than that. One must endure even more suffering than that.

If I keep talking like this, it will never end. However, these words are truly precious. They are not the words of a teacher; they are the truth.

If there are those who are dozing off, I will not speak. For those who are dozing, I will take off my outer garment and lay it here for them to lie down on. It would be nice if the women lay down like that.

Hey, do not think that the Lord will come as my bridegroom. Do not have such frivolous thoughts.

Everyone, when you go out on the street, you see dirty porters with messy hair and blackened hands. Go and hug them and kiss them. They would be very surprised and not know what to do. No matter how much you fuss and fidget, God or the Lord will not look at you and say, "Ah! How beautiful."

Think about it. If you say you put in all your effort to make yourself beautiful, what if the Lord just pretends not to see? What if the Lord sees and says, "Ah, this is mine, and that is mine. Everything of yours is mine"? Only then can you become His bride. You must be able to say that everything of yours is His to become a worthy bridegroom. Everyone, is that not so?

When the Lord sees you, He will be disappointed. Oh dear, these things are called brides... They will be tainted with dirt. Do not even mention the Lord. You must have a heart like a butcher, saying, "Lord, please do as I wish." Can you play the role of the Lord like that? Because your hearts are so twisted, the Lord comes to correct that. The Lord absolutely does not grant the wishes of such people. Why? Because the wishes of such people are desires that come through the habits of corruption.

Therefore, all such desires must be denied. They must be completely crushed. If you do not do that and then meet the Lord, saying, "Lord, where are you going?" He will tell you to stop. You must think about what you have done and have a heart of repentance. Thus, you must evoke a heart of compassion towards the Lord. While shedding tears, even if you are beaten, you must be able to say, "Lord!" Only then can you finally make a new start as a bride. Of course, only such a person can become a bride. It cannot happen before that. That is why the teacher is pushing you. He is pushing you to create the image of beloved sons and daughters, the image of beloved brides.

Where does He push you? He pushes you into the slums where Satan is crawling, into the fields where Satan is lurking. He says, "Go and see." Will you retreat from there? The Lord is coming from behind, so if you want to live, you must risk your neck and move forward. Jesus went beyond Golgotha.

Everyone, where is the Holy Place and the Most Holy Place? (They answer Golgotha) That’s right. It is Golgotha. We also have the path of Golgotha left for us. Even if I leave behind a groan that shakes heaven and earth due to the pain of countless hardships, I must head towards the summit of Golgotha, determined to carry a cross of suffering that is three times greater than the one Jesus bore. Those who do not do so cannot even go to the backyard of Golgotha.

Because this path of suffering remains, for 2,000 years, the saints have labored and longed for the Lord, but the Lord has not come. However, if today there are more than the 12 disciples who followed Jesus, more than the 120 disciples, and more than the priests of Israel who can surpass Golgotha, the Lord cannot help but come. If He still does not come, we can write a petition before God, saying, "Please send Jesus." 

Why is that? Jesus came to the unfortunate places where there were only three disciples in the past, where there were only 12 disciples who were despised, and where the people of Israel were pushed out. But when a group that surpasses the priests representing ancient Israel goes beyond the summit of Golgotha, why would He not come? If such a group exists and says, "Lord, please come," He must come like lightning.

However, today, Christianity has become a truly global religion, but there are no true disciples who can boldly cross the summit of Golgotha, making Peter, John, and James pale in comparison, and even the 70 disciples and 120 disciples pale in comparison. That is why the Lord has not yet come.

Let us become representatives of God

When you enter such a place and suffer, you must not think of it as suffering. Just have the mindset that the bad is mine. Even when you are beaten, you should not think you are being beaten for that village, but rather that you are being beaten on behalf of 2.7 billion humanity.

You must show this sincerity to this nation and instill a sense of attachment to God. Only then will the path for this nation to revive open up; otherwise, it won't work. This is the same for today's revolutionary government. The question is how to bring about a consciousness revolution, or in other words, a mental revolution. We have already gone beyond several stages of that. We are the only ones moving forward. Do you understand? "Yes."  
As we walk this path, we must not blame them even if we are beaten. God thinks the same way. Shouldn't those satanic beings be mobilized so that we can quickly indemnify? That's right, isn't it? To reach a conclusion, we must fight. If we are to fight, we must do it with determination. The satanic beings must all retreat for us to win the battle. But can we just sit still and expect to be recognized?  
You must first fight against Satan and receive a certificate proving that you have won against Satan. Until you receive that certificate, you are not qualified to be God's sons and daughters. You must receive a certificate of victory over Satan from Jesus and from the teacher. Once that happens, we can drive out the communist parties on this earth in one fell swoop. Things like communism are not even a problem.  
You just need to go out with God's heart. You must offer your body as a sacrifice, and your tears, blood, and sweat as offerings. You must present yourself as a living sacrifice that has not died. You must also establish an heir who can become such a sacrifice, become a priest, and carry all the conditions of lamentation in the universe.  
Here I am, so please whip me. God, please indemnify through me. That is what it means.  
You have learned how Adam fell and how to indemnify that fall through the principle of restoration, right? You must add the sorrow of the teacher to God's sorrow. Only then can the teacher deal with you. God has promised to bless such sons and daughters, so I offer myself as your son and daughter, please accept me. Only then can you receive blessings, right? Only then can you finally go to the place of blessing. Do you understand?  
The path of the Unification Church is simple. It is the path of becoming God's representatives. God has worked so hard for us, so we must work hard in place of God to repay that effort. Only then will God be able to rest, won't He? I must first become a child of God and a citizen. We bear a historical responsibility. Therefore, each of us must become God's representatives.  
God came to this earth with the heart of a parent, using the body of a servant. When all people shed tears, God also shed tears, and when all people sweat, God also sweated. And when all people stood at the brink of death, God shed blood on behalf of all people. I don't know how many times God has become a sacrifice for me. I don't know how many times God has personally acted as a priest. Having done such work from the personal level to the family, national, and global levels, how much suffering must there have been? He wanted to send His son to fulfill this mission, but He had to take on the mission of the son Himself due to that failure.  
Originally, God wanted to establish a true son, a representative of heaven and earth, so that through him, all people could be reborn after overcoming the path of suffering. Only then did He want to bless them. The mission of Jesus was to make this possible. However, since Jesus could not fulfill his mission, we must take responsibility for that mission today. We must use the heart of a parent, using the body of a servant, shedding tears, blood, and sweat to become a sacrifice. Of course, we must become a victorious sacrifice. We must not die. We must not become a dead sacrifice. We must fulfill the responsibilities of a priest as a living sacrifice.  
To become a priest, there must be a temple, an altar, and a people. The altar exists because of the people, and the sacrifices and priests exist for heaven and earth. Therefore, you must now step into the position of a priest.  
Why are you going around the neighborhood? It is to build an altar. If you want to become a priest, there must be a temple. Therefore, when you go to the neighborhood, you must stack the pillars to build the temple. After that, you must build the altar. What is the altar? It is the sacred place of tears for that village. You must create the necessary altar until the purpose is fulfilled.  
To fulfill the mission of a priest, you must select a special person from that village and offer the three generations of sacrifices and twelve types of offerings. Why? Because the number three is the fundamental number of twelve, and twelve represents the whole. If you establish the twelve, you can win on behalf of the east, west, south, and north. That is why Jesus wanted to perform the priestly role with twelve disciples. However, since he failed, he had no choice but to establish three disciples. These three were sacrifices that could only look in one direction, towards the east where the sunlight rises. That is why he established three disciples and offered sacrifices.  
So how did the three disciples become sacrifices? Jesus himself took on the responsibilities of the first Adam and the second Adam, but when he could not fulfill his purpose due to the mistakes of the disciples, he set up the name of the third Adam, the Lord of the Second Advent, and established three disciples to perform the sacrifices. However, Peter, James, and John made mistakes. Therefore, Jesus has been working hard to restore their mistakes and has been preparing from the standpoint of a priest until the Lord of the Second Advent comes. Do you understand?  
Therefore, you must indemnify the sorrow of Jesus and the sorrow of God. Before the sorrow of Jesus can be indemnified, the sorrow of God cannot be resolved. Therefore, you must first resolve the sorrow of Jesus, and to do that, just as Jesus had a three-year public ministry, you must also walk a public path for three years. Can you not evangelize 120 people in three years? You just need to put in the effort. After that, you must build the temple, create the altar, and become a priest. Only after establishing the condition of victory can you finally receive blessings as sons and daughters of heaven. You are restoring the family structure from Noah's family to Jacob's family. Only then can you finally become the ancestors of an individual tribe like the tribes of Israel. It's simple, isn't it? This is our path. Do you understand?  
Therefore, you young people must start quickly from a young age. This path has no room for hesitation or delay. Once you learn the principle, you will realize that it is an undeniable fact, and you cannot avoid it or refuse to do it. Since it is the path you must take, do not become a loser along the way, but win. The teacher has fought alone until now, but since there is a standard of victory, you can also win. As long as the teacher is here, do not worry, and if you fight until the end, victory will be yours. The teacher is confident about that. Knowing this, let’s go forth with confidence and strength. Do you understand? Will you swear to do so? Raise your hand if you are swearing. Now, let's make that pledge with the teacher.  
Let’s be confident in victory and move forward.  
Until now, we have had all sorts of thoughts while facing Jesus and His purpose. We have also realized that the path to seek God is a difficult one. It must be difficult. Isn’t that right? The difficult path is the path to blessings. Taking responsibility for the difficult things is the shortcut to becoming God's sons and daughters. The teacher has experienced labor, has been in poverty, has been beaten, and has been scorned. He has lived in a poor house and has helped beggars. Yet, he is not a cheap teacher. Wherever he goes, he has not lost the integrity and dignity of being a son of God. Do you understand? Our Unification Church members must not protest before the teacher, no matter how harshly the world persecutes them. They are not allowed to protest.  
This time, as the teacher sends you to the pioneering areas, he feels the most heartbroken about not being able to go to the places where you are. I explained the reason for that the other day, didn’t I? How can the teacher go empty-handed to the places where you are mobilized? If 2,000 people are mobilized and two or three form a team, just giving each person 1,000 won would cost 2 million won. Also, if you are to travel for 40 days, you must inevitably use a car, and just for gas, it costs at least 15,000 won a day. To travel from early morning until late at night incurs additional costs. If you average 30,000 won a day, that amounts to 1.2 million won over 40 days. Last year, I gave money wherever I went, and at times, I gave as much as 15,000 won. Considering all these things, you would need at least 5 million won. Do you have that kind of money? No, so there is no choice but not to go.  
Knowing that, do not feel disappointed that the teacher cannot go. Instead, the teacher will pray for you. He will pray without even eating. He is doing his best for the many young people who need to go out and evangelize. He is trying to encourage you all before you go out to evangelize. You must participate in evangelism without deviating from the teacher's heart. Please become those who can boast before God.  
<Prayer> Thank you, Father. We truly did not know that the path of restoration you have come to walk is so full of wounds and so full of twists and turns. Countless people have lived and passed away, and countless people are living now, but no one knew the purpose we know. We know that we cannot repay the grace of being able to let many people know what we know, even if we die a million times.  
Through this word today, they have gained new confidence. Now, they are in the position to return and wish to return as sacrificial offerings, so please accept them. We earnestly hope and desire this.  
Please gather together the sweat, tears, and blood shed for the victory and glory of this nation. Just as you shed blood and cried out, let these also cry out with sweat, tears, and blood. We know that because of this, the second and third Israel will be restored, and the victorious authority of the Father’s restoration will be established on earth, so from the youngest to the oldest, please extend your loving hands and connect them to the heart of the Father. We earnestly ask this. We hope you will always protect us, and we pray in your name. Amen.

What the teacher wants to shout to thirty million people, he is holding you to do instead. The teacher started from the most humble position.

On Parents’ Day and Children’s Day among annual events, we must commemorate them with all our hearts. We must welcome those days as joyful (emotional) feast days, more joyful than any banquet held by any filial child in history.  
Since it is a restoration history, on Children’s Day, everything must be offered. We must prepare with sincerity for this day. On Parents’ Day, we must show sincerity, and on Children’s Day, we must show the fruits.  
To complete the internal temple, we must find and establish children of faith. God establishes representatives to manage the times. The worse the environment, the greater the struggle of God to establish representatives, and the greater the suffering of God’s heart due to that.  
Noah took 120 years to inherit God’s heart over 1,600 years. God’s heart was more anxious during those 120 years than during the 1,600 years.  
God is trying to establish the cosmic center with 6,000 years of heart. In that process, countless people have become sacrifices.  
The teacher wants to approach you from the perspective of Noah, who wanted to inherit God’s heart and pass it on again. Therefore, you must find and establish someone who can inherit God’s heart on your behalf. The reason God is trying to place you on the path of suffering is first to remove the conditions of accusation and second to create sympathizers by placing you in a pitiful position.
218   Let Us Inherit the Heart of the Father

220   Our Path  
In just three years, things unrelated to the teacher will arise. Even during Moses' time, 600,000 people fell in the wilderness, so there will be people falling in this era as well.  
The teacher's mental state is different this year than last year. In the past, the teacher tried to take responsibility for the family members, but now it is different. Since it is the time for each person to bear fruit, thinking of them would rather block their path.  
When I see family members dressed well, my heart feels uneasy.  
Since April, I have not preached from this platform. Each person must recognize that it is their final time. Until now, the teacher has not been able to live even for 10 minutes without worry.  
During the period of faith, one must have an environment recognized by heaven. Think about how many days there will be someone to hold and weep for you after you die. If there is someone who is saved and goes to the spirit world because of you before you die, that person will fight on your behalf as an angel.  
When I look at you, you seem like people with no flesh, only skeletons remaining. The skeletons in the valley of Ezekiel refer to living people. A believer must solve the issue of death in reality.  
The farther the path is, the more I must kick and go down that path. This is heaven's responsibility. One cannot go alone. We must stimulate each other.  
When I take responsibility and move, God also moves with me. When I hold onto the heart and rest, God also rests with me. There are laws and degrees that God provides. He only deals with those who represent heaven's work.  
The providence is to find one Adam. The heart is infinite. Only after subduing Satan, the servant, the brother, and the child can one stand in the position of a parent.  
Satan cannot be subdued in a comfortable position. It must be subdued with tears. The period to compensate for 6,000 years of historical indemnity is a period of three years.  
I must correct myself so that I can stand before God without dying.  
Excuses for oneself are not permitted. Jesus did not make excuses for himself. God does not make excuses for Himself either. One can make excuses for the servant, brother, or child. It is permitted to make excuses for the servant, brother, or child.  
When the teacher stands in the position of a servant, brother, or child with you, that time has already passed.  
You must become people who can stand as representatives of heaven.  
This path must be walked even if it means spitting blood, and it must be walked even if it means dying. Suffering is wealth. The path walked with regret has been walked, but it is a futile path.  
Two Princes of Two Worlds  
<Summary of the Message> When you came to the headquarters, you probably came with many expectations. However, as the word "training" implies, there will be many things that are different from what you expected. Those at the headquarters are all busy practitioners with their respective missions, and since they deal with so many people, there may naturally be times when they cannot treat you as warmly as the local evangelists did. Even so, I ask for your understanding and participation in the training.  
The Two Worlds of Joy and Sorrow  
If someone asks you, "Who are you?" you will answer from a personal standpoint, "I am this and that person." If someone asks, "What do you do?" or "Why did you come here?" the Creator God will surely ask such questions as well. The issue here is whether you can fully entrust your circumstances and heart to God. Although there are 3 billion people living in this world, there has been no one who can confidently stand before the Creator. There has never been an absolute person whom the Creator could recognize as such.  
So what is the purpose of your coming here? It is not to solve any environmental issues, but to clarify the fundamental problems of humanity and to receive recognition and confirmation from the Absolute Being so that you can stand before that Absolute Being.  
Everyone is unhappy if they are not happy. Even if one is happy externally, there is no one whose happiness extends to the spirit world. What kind of person does the Absolute Being seek? It is not a happy person, but a person who, even in the midst of unhappiness, overcomes that unhappiness and creates true happiness. Based on this content, if I were to give a title to today's message, it would be "Become the Prince of Two Worlds." It means to become the prince of joy and sorrow, these two worlds.  
God desires that any human being become a prince of two worlds. Today, the world desires, and the Creator desires, a person who can take responsibility for and conquer both worlds. Humans have a conscience, and they have a worldview and a life view based on that conscience, so it is a natural conclusion that there must be an existence that is the foundation and subject of that conscience. If that being is the Absolute, what kind of relationship do I have with that being? Furthermore, what kind of relationship does the family, society, nation, world, and the Absolute have with each other? This is the issue.  
Then, what kind of person can stand before the Absolute as a son or daughter? Until now, the Absolute has never rejoiced. Therefore, it is natural that humans have not experienced joy. Since the causal subject has never rejoiced, it is extremely natural that we, as the resultant objects, cannot be joyful. No great person has ever enjoyed true joy while pursuing goodness and fighting against evil. While humans wish for tomorrow to be better than today, and the day after tomorrow to be better than tomorrow, it has not happened as they wished. For humans to be joyful, they must eliminate sorrow. However, there can be no joy until God rejoices first.  
The ideology of religion is universal and eschatological. Religious people have fought for this for thousands of years, while ordinary people are just now talking about the UN and world government.  
Religious people have always walked a paradoxical path. To eliminate the tragedy of reality, one must go in the opposite direction of reality. One must not walk the same path as reality.  
A true person is one who advocates goodness and shares the sorrows of difficult people. Is there anyone among religious people who claims to have completely conquered joy and sorrow? There is not. God is looking for someone who has completely conquered joy and sorrow.  
First, you must conquer the world of sorrow.  
You must break through the two worlds of joy and sorrow. While religious people have pursued a higher world, no one has poured their efforts into eliminating the world of sorrow. A person who eliminates the sorrows and pains of their parents is a filial child. Just as parents love filial children, God will love those who regard the sorrows and pains of humanity as their own. You must become a practical warrior who pushes away pain rather than merely pursuing goodness. You must not be a follower. The person who is qualified to sing of joy is the one who has permanently eliminated sorrowful circumstances.  
You must not be lost in any idealistic delusions. True ideals emerge only after going through all sorrows. God uses those who pioneer the future rather than those who seek the truth, any prophet, sage, or historical figure. We must dissect the elements of unhappiness before knocking on the door of happiness. Only by surpassing this standard can one become a cosmic prince.  
You have come to learn the sorrows of humanity, the sorrows of history, the sorrows of nations, the sorrows of the world, and the sorrows of God. A person who sheds tears for history, for the era, and for the future can be called a patriot. Above all, you must first take responsibility for sorrow. History is not something God has wronged; it is something humanity has wronged. Therefore, you must settle this sorrow.  
The teacher does not pray to go to heaven; he prays to settle the sorrows. To stand in a good position in heaven, one must create a good position on earth.  
To build one world, you must conquer the two worlds of joy and sorrow. Many organizations have sought to possess good things, but none have sought to possess bad things. If such an organization exists, the world will be dominated by them, and God will also be owned by them. No matter what difficulties you may encounter, you must occupy that environment and find infinite value within it, singing and stepping on that environment to create a solid environment as strong as concrete. Only then can you become an unseen subject when the world of goodness comes.  
Heaven is not reached by avoiding hell; it must be penetrated through the depths of hell. To go to heaven, the issues of sin and suffering must be resolved. God desires those who fight for Him. To conquer the world, one must be able to descend to the most humble position. Today, powerful nations help the impoverished and sing along with them. Now is the time to move in this direction centered on God.  
You must shed tears, but not tears of self-pity, saying, "I was like this in the past, and I am like this now." You must shed tears of repentance. You must shed tears to the point where they gather in the valleys and you must cross them in a boat. Since history began with tears, it must be resolved with tears.  
To stand before the Father,  
You must shed tears. Looking at the history of revolutions, behind every revolution, there are always tears of blood. They were oppressed, persecuted, insulted, and beaten. The teacher mentioned here has also walked that path of struggle. You must recognize that God's sorrow is millions of times greater than my sorrow. The flat sorrow of humanity cannot be compared to the three-dimensional sorrow of God.  
How many times have you examined yourselves? You may have seen today's trial, but you are sinners beyond that. You must criticize yourselves. I am someone who cannot make any excuses.  
What have this mouth, these eyes, these hands, these feet, and this body done until now? You must judge.  
You cannot stand before the Father without passing through the valley of God's tears. The Father we call is by no means a lowly Father. He is a true and precious Father. This Father needs heavenly princes, which is why He gathers you for training. A scholar who goes straight is a filial child and a loyal subject. A person who knows the sorrow of their parents is a filial child, and a person who knows the sorrow of their nation is a loyal subject.  
In fact, Korea is last in many aspects. If it turns around, it will become first. God governs both the most advanced countries and the most backward countries. When you go out to evangelize, you must seek the most difficult places. Only in the process of returning can there be eternity. There can be no eternity on a flat straight line.  
You must become a prince of joy while also becoming a prince of sorrow. When you become a prince of sorrow, joy will naturally follow.  
Only by shedding tears can you become a historical figure and a cosmic figure. The history of restoration is a history of conditions. Therefore, to receive forgiveness, you must fill the valley of God's tears.

The Word Belongs to All People  
<Summary of the Message> Gangwon Province is a mountainous area. If there is something to be proud of in Korea, it would be the beautiful scenery it possesses. Here, the air is clearer and more beautiful than in other regions.
of the world. This is the path that you must take. You must plant, and the owner must plant. You must also plant from the perspective of the owner. You must personally plant, cultivate, and harvest without going through a servant. You cannot send someone else to sow the seeds of life.

Although the son has come to the ground that has been cultivated through history, he has not been able to bear complete fruit. That is why the Father has come to sow and harvest. It is not the time for servants or sons and daughters to work; it is the time for the Father to work. The Father must harvest.

I am an extremely insignificant existence, but since the Father has commanded, it is not mine, but the Father's. You must become the ancestors of the first, second, and third Israel. There is something you must not forget as those who will replace the Father: the Father has worked hard. The fact that the Father has established us as representatives for you means that there is hope for us. To keep this forever, the emotional standard must align with the Father.

The Father, who comes with the heart of hope, wishes to have eternal sons and daughters. To solve this problem, we learn the Principle. Until now, this land has not had the Word that can connect with the hope and heart of heaven, but you have it. This Word must not remain as mine but must become that of all people, eternal. It must be done until the unity of heaven and earth is completed and the overall purpose is achieved. This Word must be proclaimed to the ends of heaven and earth, and then it must be reported to the Father, and blessings must be received according to the results of the report.

The happy person is not one who possesses money, power, or fame, but one who can be entrusted with a precious legacy like a sovereign entrusting something valuable. 

Your tribe's rise and fall depend on you. You desire to be victors and do not wish to be defeated. You must feel this. You cannot die before you win. No matter what, you must not die and must fulfill your national responsibilities. This is the standard of heaven. This Word cannot be exchanged even for the world. You must have a feeling of gratitude a million times over for having received this Word. After all, you will die once anyway. How precious have you received this Word? You must take responsibility for more than seven nations alone. Furthermore, the whole must unite to take responsibility for the entire world. When the Word, the embodiment, and the heart become one, heaven and earth, the kingdom of heaven, and the Father will all belong to us.

You must suffer alongside the line where the Father is suffering. It must be a perfectly parallel line. If it deviates even slightly, the time of betrayal will come. If it is not 90 degrees but only 85 degrees, this minus five degrees will keep increasing and will collide and break. Fight for 90 degrees. A representative who fought that fight is Jesus.

You are not in a complete state yet. You must create a self that has a value millions of times greater than your current value. This is possible by working hard with the heart of the Father. Therefore, you must push me into the most intense battlefield that the Father has not experienced for 6,000 years.

With this, you can reverse and indemnify. The Father must have suffered this much. How did the Father endure this? What was in the Father's eyes? And what was the hope? You must find the Father's blood, sweat, and painful facts. You must find the Father and the brothers, family, nation, and heaven and earth.

The path of morality is the path to find the Father. It is a path to find the sorrowful Father, so you cannot walk a joyful path. Noah was the root for finding the individual, Abraham was the branch, and Jacob was the flower, but he could not bloom. And Jesus was a being that could bloom as a flower, but he fell. And now the second Israel, Christianity, has become bare branches in winter. Therefore, to graft this onto a new tree, one must feel the pain of being cut off from my Father, my mother, my brothers, and my spouse.

A nation that possesses God will dominate the world. Why? Because it is the lineage of God. Whether one likes it or not, Isaac is the representative of the world of death, and Jacob is the representative of the world of life. The grievances of God, Jesus, and the Teacher cannot be resolved by themselves. Sons and daughters must resolve them.

The face and body that the Father must like are mine. Everything of mine is the Father's. If one does well during the winter enlightenment period, they can indemnify and restore what was failed during the summer evangelism period. By becoming the embodiment of the Word (the person), that is, by being centered on the heart, one will surely win.

What I want to show, leave behind, and say is the three great wishes of the children, and what I want to see, receive, and hear is the three great wishes of the Father.

Be a person who has the vitality to sprout even when planted in a wasteland. Even when autumn comes, do not become a withering person.

God must not be at the forefront of the battle. If God stands at the forefront, then Satan and God must fight directly. Humans must fight on the foundation that God has cultivated. The final path is the path of fighting alone.

By dying on the cross, all the Israelites until the time of Jesus became like those buried in a grave. The massacre of six million was also due to the killing of Jesus.

The goal of the Israelites who came out of Egypt was not the wilderness but to enter Canaan. Even if 600,000 fell, they had to enter Canaan.

I worked in the prison in Hungnam, putting fertilizer into burlap sacks. Who will be the fertilizer of the heart of God?

The standard sworn to the Father cannot be taken away by anyone. Please do not let me become one who retreats after death. Let the blood and flesh that have received the lineage of Satan fall away. However, I thought that the bones would remain. Ammonia! I will think of ammonia as my mother. As the mother who saves life. I prayed like this.

From now on, a time of global struggle will come. What will a person who cannot take responsibility today use tomorrow! The entire path is precious. What will happen if we do not hold onto the Korean people and fulfill our purpose?

Now is the time to organize. All humanity is unhappy. There is no being as pitiful as humans. Without fighting and winning against evil, there can be no happiness. Even if happiness comes, one cannot feel it. To be a happy person, one must fight for justice and give on behalf of God.

The path of morality is the path of giving. One must give from the family to the world and to the ends of heaven. Those who walk the path of morality sometimes make their own children serve as the enemies' servants. One must give with heart to the entire creation and establish a connection with them.

Those who try to give a hundred while giving a ten will perish. Such a person cannot enter the world centered on the heart. The heavenly world is a world of giving. Material is not the issue. Good deeds are giving. When giving, one must add material to their heart. Giving with the heart of God cannot be taken away by anyone.

In the Old Testament, God gave from the position of a servant, and in the New Testament, from the position of a brother. Now is the time to give from the position of a parent. Since we have received from God in the position of a parent, we must also give from the position of a parent with the heart of a parent. When one becomes such a person, God cannot leave them.

When giving, one must remove the enemy, so there will inevitably be a battle. We must not be ignorant of the heart of God who wishes to give. We must understand the heart of God who has fought for 6,000 years to give.

A happy person is one who can give when they want to give and receive when they want to receive. An unhappy person is one who cannot give even if they want to and cannot receive even if they wish to. From this perspective, God is an unhappy being.

Judgment is centered on the heart. Humans have lost everything due to the fall. If there is only one thing left, it is the heart surrounded by the forces of Satan. Everything in the world has been occupied by Satan.

My greatest enemy is my body. This body is blocking the path of my heart. Our Father is not a foolish Father. He is a Father who can lead loyal subjects and filial sons and daughters.

Those who die with a purpose left behind cannot be filial sons before the Father. Therefore, Jesus must pray.

Have you not recognized the one who took away your parents and took away heaven and earth? The Israelite nation did not know they were perishing while perishing. Even if one is loyal, there must be a nation that can recognize it.

I am still fighting in the world of the heart. Even if I indemnify the Father's 6,000 years of effort with six years, the form must be the same. What were the Father's words that he wanted to say to Cain, Abel, Noah, Abraham, and Moses? It is regrettable that I could not be born as Noah, Abraham, or Moses.

Whether people know it or not, I have placed my life on the line and fought to find the Word. It is regrettable that I was born as a Korean and have fought for 40 years.

When crossing the tidal path to go to Yongmaedo, I thought that if I could not go this way, heaven would perish. I thought, if I fall here, where will the Father go? Where can I not go!

I will go anyway. Even if you are exhausted, I will go. What has been lost to Satan must be found by going before Satan. It is said to be a seven-year great tribulation, so at least I must wander for seven years. I must establish at least three people who can be blessed because of me. When overcoming such a hurdle, I must find the point of alignment with the Father's heart.

You may understand the heart of restoration, but you do not understand the heart of the times. You must think about what you will do in front of the heart of the times.

Before heaven, earth, humanity, the universe, and True Parents, I pledge to fulfill my responsibilities and establish the value of victory. Amen.
