<Summary of the Message> I am grateful as a teacher that we have had no accidents in an uncomfortable place for 40 days and that we are having a graduation ceremony today. I believe you have thought about the path you must take and the responsibilities you must fulfill.

Three Types of Humans Centered on Goodness

Humans are roughly walking three types of paths. One is to go against goodness and walk in the opposite direction of goodness, another is to walk a path like a buffer zone that is neither this nor that, and the other is to aim for the purpose of goodness while taking on that responsibility. In other words, there are people who walk the path opposite to goodness, those who walk a harmless and unproductive path, and those who walk the path of sacrificing their lives for the purpose of goodness.

So, what path are we walking now? What was the past, what is the present, and what path should we take from now on? We must walk the path of sacrificing our lives for the purpose of goodness. And at some point, we must sing a dirge to expel the elements of evil in this human world.

You have entered a very difficult path. Once you enter, you will realize that it is a path you cannot avoid. This path is neither a middle state nor a path opposite to goodness. You must realize that it is a path to establish a connection with the Absolute Being.

From a religious perspective, there is the path of rebellion that aims for evil, a path that merely advocates a conscientious way, and a path that aims for the highest goodness. Living conscientiously, based on human morality, is different from living for God. Looking through past history, there have been paths of evil and paths based on conscientious human morality. This historical background prevents us from having an absolute path, keeping us from breaking free from past habits. You must decisively cut off these habits and not look back.

After all, humans must go somewhere, but where and how should we go? Without a doubt, we must go the path for God and the Absolute Being. This cannot change even if heaven and earth change. However, you have not yet escaped from even your own problems. The body is close to evil, and the heart is close to conscience. Still, many people are in a position of doubt about whether God exists. However, God is not an illusory being but a real and active being.

There are three paths, but where should the first step go? Of course, people must go the path for God and the Absolute Being. So how should we go the path for God? Just as there are various fields for serving the country, there are also various paths for walking the heavenly path. There is the path of a servant, the path of a child, and the path of a parent. So which path should we take? If we want to go more nobly and more valuably, what position should we take? We may take the position of a servant. However, when going forward with all sacrifices in mind, we would not want to go from the position of a servant. God would not advise us to go that way either. The position of a brother? That is not it either. The position of a child? God and you do not want that either.

So what position does God want us to take? At the very least, He would want us to take the position of sons and daughters. This is also what any normal person would desire. You, who are leaving today, must have the conviction that you will go from the position of sons and daughters. Being a servant is fine, but if possible, you should go from the position of sons and daughters. You might worry that God might say it is presumptuous, but that is not the case. Rather, God will say, "My son, my daughter! Fight well."

So what is the position of sons and daughters who walk that path? Of course, it is more difficult than the position of a servant or a brother. God wants us to go from the position of sons and daughters not just as children but as filial sons and daughters. Because God wants to love humanity immensely, it is natural for Him to call humans as sons and daughters. If God wishes for humans to stand in a position to exercise His full authority, He will encourage us to come as His representatives. He is not calling us as sons and daughters who can sing songs of peace, but as a God who is still in a position where He must fight against Satan, desiring filial sons and daughters who can take responsibility on His behalf. Heaven desires those who want to take responsibility for God more than those who want to receive love.

God desires representatives who can subdue Satan by any means necessary. For 6,000 years, Satan has mocked and ravaged God's world, and we must fight and win to reign over it.
God is longing for a substitute who can judge. 
Now, I want to ask all of you, the departing trainees, to go at least from the position of sons and daughters, passing through the positions of servant and adopted child. Only by becoming sons and daughters can you participate in the glory of the Father. 
We, the Unification Church members, have walked a difficult path until now, but we have not disappeared. The one who remains until the end is the representative of the Father. 
God is crying out painfully for you to go as sons and daughters, and as His substitute, for the 30 million people of this nation. He wants to send His beloved sons and daughters, who will become the Father’s representatives. God wants you to be His substitute and His sons and daughters, those who can repel Satan and receive true love from Heaven. 
The path you are taking is not a luxurious one; it is a path where you must die in place of God. Since you are in a position to walk the path of death on behalf of the Heavenly Father, you must fight while being sons and daughters. This world is a battlefield of good and evil. For at least 6,000 years, Satan has been making a fool of God. Therefore, you must take responsibility and walk the path of battle on behalf of God. You are not servants, so you must not be self-centered. 
You must fight to break down the stronghold of Satan and the enemy. So, you must be firmly armed. 
How wonderful it would be if you were the sons and daughters of the Father who can take responsibility for Heaven and Earth! However, until now, there have been no such sons and daughters. God is a pitiful God. If you understand the sorrowful situation of God, you must now put your life on the line and do God’s work. 
Everyone! Today we stand on the battlefield fighting against Satan. When it is time to starve, starve; when it is time to be naked, be naked; when it is time to be chased and cornered, be chased and cornered, but still be the sons and daughters of God. Even now, God cannot sing a song of peace and say, “My son! My daughter!” So, you must fight until you can be in such a position. If the beautiful land of this nation is filled with the sons and daughters of God, then God could command with ease, but that is not the case. There is no one to receive God’s command as His sons and daughters or as His substitute. Therefore, God is still hoping for such sons and daughters, for God’s substitute to emerge. 
So, we must become the substitutes of God the Father. If you cannot be His substitute, at least be His sons and daughters; if you cannot be His sons and daughters, then be His brothers; if you cannot even be His brothers, then at least be His servants. If you cannot do that, then it is better to die. Because of the mistakes of our ancestors, the people of Israel are still wandering. They are still in a situation where it is uncertain whether they can be salvaged or not. 
We are not trying to expand the Unification Church or any denomination. There must be more sons and daughters that God desires than there are church signs. What good is it to have many signs if there are many worthless people? 
We must quickly break away from the position of being like a buffer zone or an intermediate stage. You cannot do this with just conscience; you must do it with heart. You must become the sons and daughters of God and His substitutes. Even if you face difficulties while fighting out there, do not fall. And when you cry, do not cry alone. Even when you cry, you must cry as the sons and daughters of God, saying, “Father! I am sorry for causing You concern because I am lacking. I am ashamed to be called Your son or daughter.” You must never cry in a cowardly manner. If you shed tears as the son or daughter of God, then God the Father will also shed tears, and you must shed precious tears. You must have the spirit that says, “Father! Do not worry. This is nothing.” 
Is it a problem to have nothing to eat, to starve for a while, to sleep outside because you have no place to rest, or to get beaten up once in a while? What is wrong must be hit without mercy. If it cannot be done by strength, then you must throw your body to make them surrender. For 6,000 years, Heaven has been opening the way of providence as Heaven comes down when Satan rises. We have put our ideals before Satan and said, “Swallow this!” If he cannot swallow it and gets caught, it will be resolved. 
When you go out as the sons and daughters of God, Satan cannot withstand it. The ideals of our Unification Church cannot be swallowed by anyone. Not even communism can swallow it. No ideology can swallow it. If it cannot be swallowed, then so be it. Who can swallow God? In fact, throughout history, God seems to be a very unfortunate God. He has been trampled on all the time. However, in the end, He will make Satan surrender. 
We Unification Church members must grow even if we are beaten. We must grow correctly and uprightly. A good pine tree grows straight in both its branches and trunk. Likewise, we must not spread sideways but grow straight up. When a tree is trimmed for useful timber, the branches are cut off. Knowing this, fight beautifully. Are you confident? 
What I want is for Satan to come rushing at you when you go out for evangelism this time and hit you on the jaw. You must not scream “Oh!” and fall down there. You must never retreat. Have you made up your mind? When you go as the sons and daughters of God, Satan cannot withstand it. There will only be victory for you. If you do not take this victorious path, you cannot become the substitute of the Father. What matters is how much you fought as the sons and daughters of the Father or as His substitute, or how much you fought as brothers or servants. 
As descendants of fallen ancestors, we humans have personal Golgothas, familial Golgothas, social and national Golgothas, and global Golgothas. There are also spiritual Golgothas and physical Golgothas. Only by overcoming all these Golgothas can you finally hear the words, “You are the sons and daughters of God. Therefore, receive glory.” 
Until now, the established churches have only sought holiness, saying, “Holy, holy! Oh, God! Receive glory.” But until now, God has not been able to receive glory. Throughout the long history, all the prophets and saints sent by God have died, and the Holy Spirit is suffering to wash away human sins, and Jesus is praying, yet what glory is there? The greatest king of suffering throughout history is God, and the one who is most indignant and most wronged is God. Do you also find yourself in such a position as God? How many are there who call upon the Father from such a position? 
Fallen Adam and Eve! If I had been there at that time, I would not have stayed silent. There have been no heavenly sons and daughters who have called out the betraying ancestors to settle accounts and judge them. There must be children who, even if they fall a thousand or ten thousand times while fighting, rise again and fight. God has not had such sons and daughters. God is truly pitiful. Even now, He is filled with resentment. If there were sons and daughters who, knowing this, would fight to resolve this resentment, the world under Satan’s dominion would break apart. Everyone, let us live magnificently, fight magnificently, and die magnificently. 
We belong to the Father, so let us do according to the Father’s will. If it is the Father’s will, I will even go to the depths of hell. We must do this. And we must make it so that God can say, “Oh, I cannot do anything to you.” The secret to this is only loyalty. If there is anyone who is more loyal to Heaven than Jesus, he can become a brother of Jesus. You know that in the Bible, Jesus said, “From now on, I will not call you servants but brothers.” 
In the three paths I mentioned earlier, do not go to the buffer zone where intermediate people go, nor to the opposing path of God. A conscientious farmer recognizes the master. But what good is it to just recognize? If you know, you must repay… 
Once a concept takes root in your mind, it is hard to remove. That is why religion is necessary. A place without religion will perish. We have the absolute God as our Father. We are the sons and daughters of God. Satan is the adulterer who tramples on God’s love. 
The path we take depends on our determination. Our true Father is God, but Satan is acting as the Father. That is why, in John 8:44, Jesus rebuked, “You are trying to carry out your father’s desires.” If you know the fact that you have the blood of Satan, your indignant heart should rise up, and you should have the righteous desire to stab your body with a knife to expel the filthy false blood. Have you ever thought about that? A person who is indignant, saying, “You piece of flesh!” while hitting their body is a loyal subject of Heaven. 
That is why Jesus also fasted. That is why the saints strike their bodies. Satan, the enemy of God, is defiling Heaven and Earth and trying to take away true people, true families, true nations, and the true world, including me. 
If there is a Savior who is responsible for such Satan, I must be able to give everything to Him. The monster of sin is Satan. We must catch this Satan. I must carry out a revenge campaign against Satan. Now is the time for guerrilla warfare. Unification Church members must become splendid warriors. We must become the sons and daughters of the Heavenly Father and His substitutes. 
Among the three paths mentioned earlier, which path you take depends on your determination. You must be able to walk your own path well. 
Father, come to me. Many children must come forth. He is a Father who cannot come because He has no children, even if He wants to come. Oh, Father, who could not come because of Satan until now! Please come quickly. How much have You suffered? Come and receive glory. 
You must become the prince of victory. Only those who can worship God as such a prince can enter the Kingdom of Heaven. To pave the way for God to come and prepare a place of blessing, you must go forth and say, “Father, please discuss with us and guide us.” 
God wanted to infinitely come to this beautiful land, but He could not come because of Satan. Now you must create Heaven and say, “Please come quickly.” Do you want to do that? “Yes.” Then let us do it. 
Everyone, do not forget this: there are three paths, and we must walk the path that takes responsibility for the world of goodness centered on God’s will. The teacher has been doing this work until now because he knows this. I will never die just like that. Even if I die, branches will spread and new shoots will sprout, and the will shall be fulfilled. So, let us not hesitate to stand at the forefront of this path of will. 
Do not incur a debt of heart.

When meeting workers, you must treat them with the heart of humanity’s laborers. 
Do not incur a debt of heart. If you cannot repay loyalty with loyalty, you are incurring a debt. 
Those who teach must also have the heart of those who learn. Stand in a position where you take responsibility for what you have said. 
We must honor three parents. The parent of the heart is God, the parent of the body is the Earth, and the parent of kin is our biological parents. Since the Earth is a parent, it also has the heart of a parent. 
However, even though the Earth has given birth to us, it receives infinite contempt yet does not complain. It does not know how to be grateful but accepts everything, and even if it is trampled on or spat upon, it rather returns something to us. 
The Earth returns hundreds of grains when given one grain. It produces beautiful flowers. The heart of the Earth never changes and is without deceit.

Let us become victors.
<Summary of the Message> Once you participate in the training session, from this time onward, you are no longer free as before. You must become victors through thorough training of body and mind.

You may have entered here from a personal standpoint. You must not forget that you have a historical background woven over a long time behind you. The path laid before you is one you must take. You must remember that you are destined to walk this path.

There has never been a complete victor in human history.
So what methods and means should we take to walk this path? This is the issue. To walk a hopeful and valuable path, a firm determination is necessary.

One must understand that the existence of oneself is more problematic tomorrow than today or yesterday. While one individual may seem insignificant in a flat view, from a historical and three-dimensional perspective, surrounded by those before and after, left and right, one must recognize that one is an extremely important existence.

The title of what I want to say to you today is "Let Us Become Victors." Everyone undergoing training, and everything else in life, is a struggle. Those of you who are training are in a critical trial of whether you will become victors or losers. The question is whether you will become individual victors, national victors, or global victors. In any workplace or school, there is always a process of struggle involved. All humanity living in the fallen world is fighting.

So how can we win this fight? Preparation is necessary. The fight does not end quickly as one might think.

Then, in what fields should we become victors? A ruler of any nation may have been a victor at that time, but the victorious value established until today has not been achieved. Today, the two opposing camps of democracy and communism are fighting, and even if one side wins, the fight does not end. There are still paths of struggle ahead. Is there anyone who can confidently claim to be a historical, epochal, and future victor?

Can any sect or sovereignty that has won become a future victor? All that passes. If countless victors in history were true victors, would the world today be in such a state?

Can we truly say that Jesus achieved eternal victory? Can the prophets of the past boast of their authority until now? No. There have been no such victors in the past, nor are there any in the present, so there must be an eternal victor in the future, right? Until God can say that your victory is my victory, humanity must continue to struggle forever. If one only looks at the flat phenomena, one can only fall into despair and hopelessness, but humans cannot determine that on their own. Historical victories have been achieved when the time and circumstances were right, not by humans alone. Even if we claim to have won under historical conditions today, there is a greater purpose than my individual purpose.

If there is a Creator who made heaven and earth, what kind of being would He be? If He were to regret what He created in this historical end time and collapse, He would not be a true Creator. A Creator must bear the fruits of victory, not failure.

Has that absolute being ever boasted of victory? No. Therefore, no matter how much ability and talent humans have, they cannot win. As long as God does not win, humans cannot win either. Everyone has received the judgment of history, and what has passed was only a temporary victory; it was not a complete victory.

God who desires the final victory.
God has been providentially working through individuals, families, and nations, establishing the Lord and the ideology toward one purpose. Now, He is dividing into two opposing camps and moving toward a day of victory. Before establishing a relationship with the absolute being and the heart, one cannot achieve complete victory. Happiness can only be obtained by winning with the heart.

God has established religions to save humanity. There are national religions, global religions, historical religions, epochal religions, and future religions. Religions must be historical, epochal, and future-oriented. Without that, complete victory cannot be achieved. While current Christianity may have fulfilled its mission from the past to the present, can it fulfill its future mission? In this view, a religious ideology that can connect the past, present, and future is necessary. One must establish a victorious standard that no one can criticize in the past and present to win in the future. Because that is who God is.

Materialism must inevitably perish. But does democracy have the conditions for historical and epochal victory? No, it does not. Without the conditions for victory, there can be no future victory. So what should a religion that lacks such conditions do? Christians around the world must unite. Now, the future must emerge. Some religions are claiming to return to the past, but today's situation is different from the past. Can we handle today's circumstances with past methods? We must not go back to the past. There must be historical and epochal achievements to establish a future foundation. Therefore, an ideology that can encompass the past, present, and future must emerge.

Your life is both epochal and global. Therefore, salvation must not only be individual but must pass through individuals, families, nations, and the world to achieve cosmic salvation.

Has there ever been such a time in history? After establishing the individual expectation centered on Abraham, the family expectation centered on Jacob, and the national expectation centered on Moses, during Jesus' time, there was an attempt to establish a global expectation centered on Jesus. However, Israel could not lay such a global expectation. This is where the problem lies.

Those walking the path of virtue must carry out the Second Israel reorganization movement. Christianity was established to reorganize the national Second Israel, but it has not fulfilled that mission. Therefore, the one who comes to complete that mission is the Lord of the Second Advent.

Today, each organization is forming alliances within themselves, but they must engage in a global movement. They must develop into a movement that is historical, epochal, and future-oriented. If God is providentially working in this way, what should religious people do? They must not only become historical victors. They must not only become current victors. They must become future victors that transcend the past and present. Otherwise, they cannot become the final victors. In the future, religions that do not have global content and form will break apart. Christianity, Buddhism, and Islam are no exception. If they cannot do that, they must at least serve as materials for the world. It is not the time to quarrel over "mine" and "yours."

God desires the final victory. We must win centered on His will. That will is superior to any ideology present on earth today. The root of this will has existed since the past. The time has passed for simply believing and going to heaven. The key issue is which side one stands on. Even if one cannot be saved right now, one must stand on the side that can be saved.

If a leader makes a mistake, it will influence everyone beneath them. Even if an individual does not do well, if the whole wins, they can also win together. In the future, it will pass when individuals are blessed, and it will pass when nations are blessed. Now is the time for the world to be blessed. If Jesus had won in that era and environment, even the wicked could have been saved. There must be a global organization to save the world; otherwise, it is unnecessary.

First, we must fulfill God's will. To achieve that will, we must be pushed and condemned by the epochal ideology. If one knows the will, then one must know God. God is the master of the heart. Anyone who knows this heart and moves cannot be judged.

The first issue is to know God's will.
In any case, numerous ideologies and claims are bound to collide. They will collide and become one. While they may fight in the head, they must become one in the tail. The heart facing the will must not change, and one must become one with the one who established the will. What kind of will should it be? Even if the races are different and the environments and ideologies differ, it must be right and achievable. Establishing this will is the mission of religion.
All traditional religions have fulfilled their historical and temporal missions, but they have not aligned with God's future providence. It must be God's will, Jesus' will, and the saints' will. God's will is not merely for individuals to believe and go to heaven. It is to save the whole. In the face of this will, the enemy is Satan. He is the one who opposes the will. However, we must fight for the will. We must fight to find historical value. We must be able to do so.

So what is God's will? It is for heaven and earth, humanity and myself, will and heart to become one. When that happens, God's will will be fulfilled. In the air, Satan holds power. Heaven and earth, humanity and myself, will and heart must unite. And then, if we align with God's heart, everything will be complete. It is simple. How great a victory it is to become one with God's heart! To fulfill the will, we must unite with the heart of the Absolute.

Let us become victors. If God has a dream, what would it be? It is not to create servants. It is to create beloved sons and daughters. In the future, emotional leadership and emotional thought will conquer the world. Tribal and national issues must pass. The First World War was an economic war, a physical fight, and the Second World War was an ideological war, a fight of the heart. In the future, an era of emotional struggle will come. This war must be fought by religious people.

In the time of Jesus, people prayed for blessings. But now, the time has passed for praying for blessings for one's family or nation. Now we must ask, "Please resolve my resentment and unite my heart with humanity and all things." Only then can we be recognized by God as His beloved sons and daughters. Those who know the will must be able to encompass heaven and earth, humanity, and their own bodies in their hearts.

If democracy and communism fight, communism will perish. Even if it perishes, it will be divided and destroyed. What will happen if democracy wins? This ideology must be able to dissolve all ideologies of the world. If establishing such an ideology is the task, is it not worth doing even if this body turns to dust? Moreover, how incredible is it that such an ideology has emerged from Korea? To establish this ideology, we have fought until now while being scorned.

Our eyes must look to heaven and earth, and our lives must be for the will. God is such a being, but because He is incorporeal, He cannot act as He wishes. However, we can act freely. 

For you, the primary issue is to know God's will. To know the will, you must understand how history has flowed, how this era is flowing, and what the future will be. You must also know what kind of being God is. What kind of God has been historical, and what kind of history of struggle has He woven? What kind of struggle is He engaged in during this era, and how will His will be connected to the future? You must know the content of that will.

In repentance, you must repent of historical sins. You must repent of the historical sins that began with Adam and Eve and have not been resolved through Noah, Abraham, Moses, and Jesus. Those who cannot repent of historical sins cannot inherit God's will for the era, and without repenting of the era, they cannot inherit God's will for the future. You must repent across three generations. This is because the three generations centered on God have not been connected through Adam and Eve to Cain and Abel.

Repentance and victory. We must become princes of historical victory and princes of future victory. Is it enough for you to go to heaven alone? As long as this world is unresolved, even if you go to heaven, you must return.

If we summarize the letters of the Bible we believe in, the center of the Bible is Jesus, the center of Jesus is the bride and groom, and the center of the bride and groom is love. The important thing is emotional unity. When we dance, the world dances, and when we laugh, the world can laugh. This is the wonderful world that God envisioned.

You must say, "I will take responsibility."

If there are those who wish to resolve their resentment and become truly faithful archangels, Adam, Moses, and Jesus will weep, asking, "Where have you been until now?" Would not God, Jesus, and the Holy Spirit long for such a scene? Only when such a scene unfolds will historical fruits be borne. What kind of struggle is the Father engaged in now? What is the most painful thing? You must be able to say, "I will take responsibility for that," and resolve God's resentment.

When God created each creature with a hope for the future, how serious was He? As He poured His heart into creating sons and daughters of heart, how much did He long to see them grow up and rejoice in the reality of His creation? Yet those sons and daughters fell. There is not a single creature or blade of grass that does not contain God's energy. God created all of that to give to His sons and daughters. While people cherish and handle historical cultural assets and antiques with care, what could be more precious and valuable than all things that God Himself painstakingly created? How wonderful it would be if the heart of God at the time of creation connected with us!

If we were to gather all the historical figures who lived on this earth and ask them if they have gone through the conditions of repentance before God, they would have nothing to say. You, who are here, may have wasted the past, but from now on, it must not be so. Those who know this ideology can follow this path, but if not, they cannot even follow the communists. It is to completely eliminate Satan from heaven and earth. You! If the person standing here is not half crazy or out of their mind, then the problem is great. **Children's Day Address**
<Summary of the Message> We have lived many years, but we have not had a year we can boast about. We have not been able to claim and boast, "I am this before heaven and earth." It is our own body, yet there is no part of it we can boast about. Among many days, there is not a single day we can boast about, and it is a sad thing that there is not a single part of our body we can boast about. How can I feel that I am precious? How can I make my body valuable? How can I spend my time valuably? This is the problem.

In our Republic of Korea, there are various commemorative days. Labor Day, Memorial Day, Mother's Day, and many other commemorative days exist. However, there is no commemorative day that can bring joy in heaven. Your birthday is also a day that is connected to fallen parents, so it is a day of lamentation.

Therefore, heaven must inevitably carry out the great judgment. The great judgment is a great sorting, a great clearing, and a great accounting. As long as the noun "fall" exists, judgment is unavoidable. It is a sad thing that Jesus was born in the pit of sin, and it is extremely sad that He died on the cross. It is something that must be judged.

Many loyalists, dutiful children, and virtuous women have come and gone in history, but there has not been a loyalist, dutiful child, or virtuous woman that heaven can recognize. In the end times, there must be loyalists, dutiful children, and virtuous women that heaven can recognize. To distinguish between truth and falsehood, principles must emerge. The names of countless people who could be called loyalists, dutiful children, and virtuous women in history are written in Satan's notebook. They all thank heaven but cannot be in a position to do so. Therefore, Satan has accused God, saying, "Do I not have such loyalists, dutiful children, and virtuous women?"

The loyalists, dutiful children, and virtuous women that heaven can boast about must be much higher than those in Satan's world. That is why Jesus was sent to this earth. Throughout history, Satan has accused. While there are many days on earth that can be boasted about, heaven still does not have a single day that can be boasted about. Now is the time for religious loyalists, dutiful children, and virtuous women to emerge. Therefore, we must be at least a little better than Satan.

Instead of boasting about the history of Israel, we must boast about the figures who led that history. A global and historical loyalist must emerge before God's presence. God exists for the whole, Jesus exists for heaven, and the Holy Spirit exists for the earth.

When we celebrate a day of events, we must say, "Father, you have not had such a day until now. We apologize for celebrating it first." 

Without a holy land, holy people cannot emerge. That is why heaven carries offerings. The Bible says, "There is no righteous person, not even one..." (Romans 3:10), does it not? There cannot be a temple without a holy land and holy people. However, God has been working in reverse.

Next, there must be a holy heaven. Jesus came as the representative of the holy heaven. Now we must become holy people who possess both the holy heaven and the holy land. My body represents the holy land, my heart represents heaven, and my character represents God. One must not comfort and believe in oneself. One must look forward to a time.

Today, two types of people are needed. First, there must be those who can be called by the leader for discussion, and second, there must be those who can be commanded by the leader. If you cannot be the former, you must at least be the latter.

To celebrate this day (Children's Day), you must devote yourself from 40 days prior. You must purify yourself three days before and fast for three days before and after.

God has not yet had His day, His Parents' Day, or His Children's Day. The ideal of creation that God aims for is emotional oneness. The purpose of creation is to form an emotional straight line connecting God, Adam, and children. He created in accordance with the principles of harmony. Therefore, God works according to the method of re-creation and that design, adhering to these principles.

The fact that Jesus lost the 70 disciples is akin to Moses in the land of Canaan, and the loss of the 12 disciples is a return to the state of Noah, while the loss of even the three disciples is a return to the position of Adam. Therefore, He had no choice but to die.

God's restoration providence must first find the three sons of Noah's family, then establish nine people to complete the number nine, and finally establish a total of twelve. Only then can the upper and lower be united.
Connecting is essential. We must find and establish the 12 numbers of Jacob's family and the 3 numbers of Adam's family. Thus, all laws of creation must establish the positions of the three subjects. God, Adam, and Eve (children) are the three subjects, and when we connect the circuit of the exchange centered on each side, we derive the total position of 12 numbers. God must establish a day for children, a day for parents, and a day for God, so that all people can celebrate, completing all commemorative days.

Let us become those who remain.
<Summary of the message> Where should we go? In response to this question, most people will think of some external place. However, you must enter the deep place of the heart. Rather than going for external nations, hometowns, or relatives, always think of your own insufficiency and walk the one path centered on infinite heart. 

A person with whom God can be together.
Now is the time that surpasses the second year of the three-year evangelism period, and this 9th training session will be the last training session of this year. Additionally, the number 9 carries the meaning of settling all things. What I want to convey to you, the participants of the 9th training session tonight, is to become those who remain forever. 

If God is present, what kind of being would God be? God is the one who will exist forever, even if history is cut off in the future. Therefore, the person God seeks cannot be a temporary person. He must be someone who can be together with eternal heaven. His will, ideology, lifestyle, actions, words, and heart must all be historical, timely, and future-oriented. Only then can he remain forever.

* This message is a summary of the closing remarks from the 9th National Evangelist Training Session, published in <Seonghwa> No. 14 (March 1, 1962).

Everyone desires the eternal. They wish for everything they feel and conceive to be eternal. For us today, to firmly establish our self-awareness, we must find a position that can resonate with the vast universe. In other words, we must find a position where when I move, heaven can also move. 

Great figures and saints lived lives that moved like heaven. However, no matter how great a figure may be, they could not possess the path that remains forever. This is an undeniable fact. Then, what kind of person can be the true person with whom heaven can be together forever, and where will they be? The masters of the way that people believe in were necessary until now, but they cannot be said to be eternally necessary. There has not yet been anyone who can be said to be eternally needed. 

So, who is the person that heaven wants to speak to and engage with forever? He is the person without whom the providence of restoration cannot be carried out. He is the one whom past saints, today's humanity, and future descendants all want to speak with and connect with. Such an existence must emerge in this world to encounter and see God. He is the one who wants to live together with all people from the past, present, and future. He is the one who desires to share not only life but also every action, and to love eternally with a heart that is connected. If such a master or sage had come to this earth, we would not be in the position we are in today.

A happy person, a valuable person, is someone who feels happiness in their life. A person who cannot let go of God can be called a valuable human being and a happy person. Heaven is seeking such a happy and valuable existence. You must seek a position where you can relate to such an existence. 

The valuable existence that heaven desires is someone with whom it wants to speak, live, and act together forever. If you cannot become such an existence, you should at least pray to be led toward such an existence. No matter how great a person was in the past, no matter how great a person may be in this era, and no matter how great a person may become in the future, they must welcome such a being. If such a being were to appear before us, we would be the happiest. That is a precious value that cannot be exchanged for anything in the world.

And if that being's ideology unfolds in this world of our time, this world cannot help but become one. The place where we speak with him, act with him, and live is a place that aligns with heaven. Therefore, any doctrine, ideology, or thought that can be permitted between heaven and earth must be like this. 

If you have found such a thing, you are infinitely happy. If there is such a person, the words they speak for the world and humanity will be words that everyone should enjoy, and no matter how difficult their life may be, everyone will want to live with them. If God is eternal, then God's words, ideology, and life must also be eternal.

The key to unification.
There are individuals, families, societies, nations, the world, heaven, and earth. How can we connect these into one? If you have listened to the words, to what extent do you accept these words as valuable, and how many percent do you accept them? Do you have the desire to be forever with these words? If not, you must part ways. If you listen to these words and then wish to re-establish the same relationship as before, you must have a heart that has a deeper emotional connection than these words. Otherwise, you cannot move to a higher position. Therefore, you must think about what these words are. And you must feel the desire to live forever with the one responsible for these words. Furthermore, you must be able to go together even to the place of death.

This universe must be unified. Words, actions, lives, and hearts must be unified. This cannot come from humans, as humans are resultant beings, not causal beings. We are now establishing unity. What are we trying to unify? We are trying to unify truth, actions, lives, ideologies, and hearts. The heart unites families, societies, nations, the world, and heaven. Only in the world of the heart can we feel three-dimensional emotions, and the noun "eternity" can exist. Therefore, above all, the heart is the issue.

If I exist, above me are my parents, and if I trace back further, there are the human ancestors, Adam and Eve. Then, what exists above that? There must be the source of the heart above that. And that source will appeal to us to seek itself. We must feel that. If we cannot feel that, we are sinners who cannot speak.

Christianity emphasizes love. Whom does that love pertain to? The ultimate destination of love is God. There is something deeper than this love, which is the heart. Therefore, centered on this heart, words, actions, and ideologies are established. Nothing can be done alone. There must always be a vertical heart that comes from God. We must have God's historical heart, timely heart, and future heart.

When the subject and object give and take, reproduction occurs. Deceit is what has departed from the heart of heaven and earth, and evil is what departs from the heart of heaven and earth to give and take. We must know God's heart before the fall and the heart of restoration after the fall. A person who can stand confidently before God's historical, timely, and future heart will become a victor before heaven and earth.

When you go out to the local areas to spread the words, you must speak to all people with God's heart, not with personal feelings. Even if you have to repeat the same words, actions, and lives thousands of times, you must not feel displeased. Even when speaking to one person, you must speak with the heart as if God is directly addressing that person. And you should not give the words all at once but rather step by step, providing words that the person can appreciate at each stage.

Until today, God has not been able to say all the words He wants to say to humanity. He has only spoken the words that humans like. While doing so, He has been looking forward to the time when He can speak the words He wants to say. Therefore, we must find a being who can convey God's heart. All actions must be done together with the Father. Even in speaking and sending a gaze, it must be done together with the Father. If you go out with only God's heart, you will not be a loser. Those who rebel against these words will be judged, and those who mock those actions will also be judged.

When you go out to fight in the local areas, you must live with the heart that considers how much the Father wanted to live with reality. You must lead a holy life and act together with the Father even in unjust situations. However, in difficult situations, do not put the Father forward but rather bring Him behind you and become someone who can stand at the forefront.

To lead truly,
Now, you who have been trained must become leaders. You must be leaders of words, leaders of actions, leaders of ideologies, leaders of lives, and leaders of hearts. You must recognize that taking on such a mission is an indescribable honor and a valuable task.

In the past, the teacher spoke a lot without paying much attention, and there were times when his tongue did not turn well. When you go out to the local areas, you must speak with a heart of caution and concern. When you see someone who is loyal for the sake of that village, you should feel grateful, thinking, "That person is taking my place." Even when giving principle lectures, you must speak as if you are the historical figures like Cain, Moses, and Jesus. In this way, you must instill the heart of the Father into the thirty million people. Even if you appear insufficient, your words, actions, ideologies, and lives must be said to belong to the Father.

This year is a time when we must meet firmly before the nation. Therefore, we must make a solid resolution and oath. We must be prepared to be the tip of the shell at the final battle. We must convey the words centered on the heart, live centered on the heart, act centered on the words, and spread the ideology centered on the words. We must share with a pure heart. We must not have even a little desire to utilize it for ourselves.

We must give with the heart of parents. We must not give with our own desires and ambitions. Because the Father did so, you must do the same. This word has come forth through tears, so you must also give through tears. We must plant the truth in this land where there is no truth. Speaking is to testify to oneself and to show oneself. Acting and living also show oneself. When giving words, it must be done emotionally. Words that flow from the heart will allow the inner person to grow, even if they are heard and then forgotten. As you move, the object will stand.

You must become a person who testifies to yourself. Testifying must be done from an eternal position. Eternity comes only through the heart. When you go out to fight, if you are rejected once, you will reap the harvest of the ship. Everything will be determined by whether you can give what is unchanging on behalf of heaven. You must clearly understand this.

You must become the driving force that calls forth the many families and individuals who have historically borne public responsibilities, such as Noah, Abraham, and Moses.

To become a valuable person.
If God were to drag you to a historical public auction and put you up for sale, you must think about how much your value would be. When God asks, "How much will this person sell for?" you must not become someone whom no one cares about, not even a beggar. You must become a person whom God can say no to even before He finishes speaking. You must be a person who can make Satan anxious, saying, "I will give you half of all things on this earth." 

Jesus was a valuable being who could save all humanity centered on the Israelite nation, which is why Satan invaded. Reflecting on the three great temptations of Satan against Jesus, you must consider how much you are worth.

Today, I do not exist merely as an individual but as a being clothed in connections. This clothing is soaked with the sighs, sorrows, tears, and grievances of all historical figures like Adam, Abel, Noah, and Abraham, and it is stained with the sins of humanity's disbelief. Therefore, we must shed this clothing. Only by shedding it all at once can we qualify to approach the tree of life. 

O God, I will inherit and bear the sweat, tears, grievances, blood, and heart of historical figures on behalf of others.
"Please stand me up!" we must negotiate with that in mind. The teacher knows this, and wants to place you in a public position, but do you want to become cheap? Will you be sold for a bowl of rice, retreat in front of a club, and easily surrender before an enemy?

If a specific value is greater than an individual's value, then the individual's value is subjugated. Therefore, if one realizes that their individual value is less than a specific value, they must submit. If the value of an entire nation is less than a specific value, then the entire nation must submit. To live and die with that specific value, one must stand in a position of public value. That specific value is eternal, absolute, and unchanging, so to participate in that value, one must stand in an absolute public position and become a representative of that value.

That value cannot be established by heaven and earth. Only a true person can establish it. The term "true" contains historical and public significance. To inherit the value of this true person, one must place their perspective and heart in a position that represents heaven. Therefore, when you go out to enlighten in the local area, even if you write a character on the blackboard while lecturing, do not lecture only to the few people sitting in front of you, but lecture to the entire universe. Even if you sweat, you must sweat with the heart of returning to heaven. Then, as you have a historical connection with your descendants, you will move the ancestors and bear fruit in connection with the conscience of the ancestors.

God has been carrying out the providence of restoration through the age of servants, the age of children, and the age of parents. We think that a prophet has appeared on this earth and pioneered the position and environment of a servant, but that is not the case. First, heaven came to this earth and worked hard to pave the way for a global age of servants from the position of a servant, and then we must understand that the prophet was sent as the reality of a servant on that foundation. To lay the foundation to send the only begotten son Jesus, God personally worked from the position of a child. Moreover, to pave the way to send the True Parents, God has traveled back and forth to this earth thousands of times, laboring with a thread of hope for the Korean people. Even though He is God, He shed tears in the form of a servant, and even though He is God, He shed tears in the form of a child, and in the form of a parent, He sowed tears.

The attitude that a believer in the last days must have
We cannot walk the historical path that God has walked with such effort. We are limited to a finite time on this earth, so we must connect with God's heart through that historical process. Only then can we become historical figures.

Oh God! How sorrowful You must have been without a servant to inherit Your heart and take responsibility during the Old Testament age! I will become one who emotionally represents the servant of that time in this age. Oh God! How lamentable You must have been when You worked from the position of a child and could not find the child You were seeking! I may not have what it takes, but I will emotionally become the child of that time to comfort You.

We must comfort God's heart. 
If one claims to walk the path of true faith in these last days, they must either take the position of a servant seeking God or become the reality of God seeking a servant, and take one of these two positions.

Today, all humanity is in the position of God's servant, so to meet God, one must meet the daughter of God among daughters and the son of God among sons. God paves the way for global filial sons and daughters, creates global filial sons and daughters, and then judges. That person is the standard of a true person. He says, "Become like that." This true person is the Lord who is coming.

When the day of emotion and the day of the Second Coming comes, those who are alive to meet that day must weep from the position of a rebellious servant, weep from the position of a cast-out child, and weep from the position of one who has returned. They must shed tears and wail, washing the clothes stained with the blood of sin. Being in such a position is the public existence of a unification warrior based on a value relationship. The teacher is worried that this tremendous relationship may be violated due to your mistakes.

The wild olive tree must be grafted onto the true olive tree, but when grafting, it must not be received from the branch side, which is the result. It must be grafted from the root side to settle historical issues. One must remember that at the moment of grafting, they must eliminate the sap they had and receive new sap. One must eliminate the self of the past and become absolutely gentle, humble, and obedient to harmonize.

The importance of the three-year period
When you go out to the area you are responsible for during this period, you must work with the resolve to say, "People of the district, come all! People from this district, gather! Let's hold a loyalty meeting." If any opposition arises, treat that person with the great love that a parent would show, a love that they cannot even show to their own children. The element of life for creatures is God's love, and the pinnacle of love can subdue such a person. Also, stand in the position of a child who can serve that opponent with more service than a parent would for their own child. Then you will be able to subdue that opponent.

Since Adam was defeated by the enemy Satan, men must be taught how to fight and win against the enemy as servants. And since the sun caused Adam, who was to be a filial son, to fall, women must become filial daughters and help men become filial sons, so women must be taught how to be filial daughters. Men must fulfill the mission of a servant, women must fulfill the mission of a child, and Jesus must fulfill the mission of a parent. Therefore, a man cannot say he loves someone before he has fought and won against the enemy to make the enemy a child. Also, a woman must become the reality of a filial daughter before the Father, so she cannot have any other thoughts.

The designated three years is the minimum period of historical indemnity and is the period of individual indemnity. Therefore, in the future, all members of the Unification Church must go through this three-year period. Since it is said to be one heart and one body, you must all understand the teacher's heart. During this night, think about what the teacher will do, whether he will spend the night with his eyes wide open, and stand in the position of the teacher to feel even a semblance of it, which is what this three-year special period is about. During the three years, holding two enlightenment campaigns a year, combined, it does not even amount to one year. If you cannot do even this much, it is unacceptable. Originally, this period should be passed while fasting.

Everyone, there is only one time for such a relationship. Please find your place and establish your purpose during this period. If you miss the time, you will lose both your position and your purpose. If that happens, you will become unrelated to the teacher.

Bring something to boast about before the Father
<Summary of the words> This three years is a historical turning point. You may not know it, but internally it is so. Participating in this period is a great honor. 

In this year of 1961, we are moving into the second year of the three-year course. During this three-year period, you must achieve victorious results. On the third day (January 3), I will give you the slogan for the new year.

Until now, the blessings have been consumed due to things that need to be indemnified, but from now on, that will not be the case. From now on, blessings will be realized as they are blessed.

Now, we must establish blessed families. If there are blessed sons and daughters among your children, you must treat them with three times the sincerity compared to those who married in the world. From now on, those who come in must live for three years without the help of others. During this period, we will not allow them to live above the standard of life we have lived.

Before establishing believing children, one cannot have their own children. One must first establish Cain and pass on the blessing before having children. Those who have married until now belong to the teacher, and this is an exception.

From now on, we must organize tribes. The blessing is a conditional blessing. Externally, God is harsh towards the teacher. At that time, I had my heart in heaven and my body placed in the opposing position, and then I retrieve it.

December 31, 1961, at the former headquarters church.
* This message was given at the New Year's Eve gathering and was recorded by former association president Yoo Hyo-won in his notebook. The title was added by the editor.

We must teach from the position of being in the world of Satan and fill in what is lacking. Jesus also died while trying to establish believing sons and daughters. Until now, even babies have walked the entire path of restoration. Now is the time to save one's own family.

From this year, the spirit world will be mobilized. If the hearts are united, we can invoke the work of Jesus and the Holy Spirit. We can also engage in spiritual work while placing the reality on the ground. Because the connections of parents, couples, and children are sprouting, everyone's hearts are converging.

Humans have a desire to boast and show off their own. Therefore, one must have something to boast about or show. One must have something to boast about before the Father.

What will you show and boast about before the Father this year? Only the heart. If there is something to boast about in the Unification Church, it is individuals and families that communicate through the heart. Therefore, one must not become a person who evaluates this. Also, one must not become a person who hinders what heaven wants to boast about. The reason one cannot evaluate is that those things belong to the teacher.

The teacher has many enemies. However, he cannot hate them. Good must be good even in front of enemies. Until now, he has been met from the position of Abel. From now on, legal measures can be taken.

The first generation is being pushed back, and it is time for the second generation to rise. Even if pastors and elders cannot enter, their children will enter.

When the teacher sees someone who claims to be great, he wants to ask what they have done until now. The teacher does not want the members to remain as they were in the past.

He feels pity for the babies.

Live a life that can show
<Summary of the words> Live a life where you can see and do everything without hesitation, whether you are sleeping or waking, coming or going, or meeting. If you cannot do it externally, you must live a life that shows internally.

Since humans are beings made of the Word, reality, and spirit, you must first establish the Word, establish character, and engage in spiritual work. Only then is it normal. If one places the spiritual aspect first, it becomes a leap over the stages, resulting in great indemnity.

Sermons must first touch oneself. One's prayer must move oneself. Sermons should be done from the position of being sympathetic. One must stand in a position of pleading with God for the pity of those who must establish a connection of life through oneself.

To stand in such a position of receiving sympathy, one must return to the position of having sought the heavenly path while suffering. To do so, there must be no enemies. They may want to kill me, but I must become a person who can walk through dark alleys without worry.

January 1, 1962, at the former headquarters church.
* This message was given during the New Year's worship service, and was organized from the notes of former association president Yoo Hyo-won. The title was added by the editor.

Let us become those who can show and boast
<Summary of the words> 1962 is a year that will not come again historically. So how should we welcome this year? We must welcome the new year with the goal of fulfilling what God desires, even if only a few Unification members can do so.

God who has come to find humans
This year, you must avoid becoming the object of God's concern by escaping Satan's accusations and become a being that is not lacking in any direction—front, back, left, right, up, down, inside, or outside. 

You must become the reality of the wish that God has wanted to boast about while carrying out His providence until now. You must also become a being that can be recognized before heaven and earth, all creation, and furthermore, a being that can show and boast even to this earth and the world of Satan. This year, you must be the one who practices and bears that.

What does God desire? It goes without saying that it is the ideal world of creation that humans should have achieved without falling. However, after humans fell, God has been searching for a being that can give and receive His heart and can show and boast before all creation. He has been working with that wish until now. However, God has not yet fulfilled that wish. 

Creatures created by God have form but lack value. This is because the master of all things, humans, have not been completed. 

Until now, God's wish has been for humans to connect with all things and with God. Therefore, God has been working to elevate fallen humans from the position of servants to the position of adopted children, then to the position of children, and finally to the position of parents. This is to cut off the sorrowful connection of the fall and to establish a connection of oneness between all things, humans, and God, so that God's joy is human joy, and human joy is the joy of all things. God wanted to boast about and show off His sons and daughters to the world of all creation and the angelic world.

None of us humans are as we were at the time of creation. Humans have a static nature, so they can feel emotions such as sadness or joy. They can feel joy or sadness through others. When the joy of the other becomes my joy, there is a desire to boast and show it off, and that is the human heart. God is the same. God rejoices in seeing humans rejoice, and humans rejoice in seeing God rejoice because that is the joy of giving and receiving.

It is impossible to return to the original world with human strength alone. Therefore, God carries out the work of elevation. This is the providence of restoration. If humans cooperate in this, the providence of restoration would be easier, but until now, humans have not cooperated with God's providence. God has been tirelessly searching for those who will place their hearts and hold onto God's hand, but there has not been a single person. There have been those who have rebelled, but there has not been anyone who welcomed and supported God. In the midst of this, God has expanded His will to families, nations, and the world. The internal and external hardships He has endured in this process are beyond words.

Any nation or people can claim to have suffered on a flat level, but before God, they cannot say they have suffered. Individuals are even more so. Not only on the ground but even when considering all humans who have come and gone, there is no one who can say they have worked hard and cooperated for the will. This is an undeniable fact. To draw such humans, God is personally working hard and fighting with responsibility.

Originally, God is a being that appears in glory. The joy of humans is God's joy, and God's joy is the joy of humans, which is the ideal of creation, but that ideal has vanished, and God has become a pitiful figure. The appearance of God before humans is not a glorious one. God is in a position that is far more pitiful than any pitiful individual or nation. Originally, God was in a glorious form, but since the day humans fell, He has been in the opposite form. God was supposed to entrust everything to His children, and humans were supposed to entrust everything to Father God, which was the mutual position between God and humans, but that could not happen. How painful must it be for a parent to appear before their children in such a pitiful state? God also...
It is the same. However, God does not want to inform us of His pain and circumstances, nor does He want to show the sad appearance of endlessly struggling.  
The pitiful God  
Many believers on this earth are waiting for the glorious day when the Lord will come for their wishes, but God is enduring unspeakable suffering until He sends Him. The believers do not know this fact.  
The prophets sent by God are not beings for themselves, but existences that must raise their hands when God commands them to, beings that cannot help but cling to God. Any leader who is not like that cannot hold onto God and thus falls away. However, before sympathizing with their suffering, we must understand that God's suffering was greater until He sent them.  
Behind the glory we will see, there has already been God's suffering, and behind the fulfillment of our wishes, there has already been God's suffering. Until we achieve victory, God has endured the bitter pain of defeat tens of millions of times. If we have done something wrong, God has become a being who can offer a sacrifice for it and can relate to us. Therefore, God appears not in a glorious form but in a tragic form tangled with blood, sweat, and tears. Until we are called and receive God's blessings, until He places us in that one position of victory, God has come forth as a sacrifice.  
So, what must God do to enjoy glory? Since God has walked the path of suffering, we must also walk the path of suffering. Otherwise, God cannot enjoy glory. Until now, we have not known such labor of God, and God has not wanted to show it. As a parent, He would not want to show His struggling appearance to His beloved children. That is why He has covered it up until today. What kind of appearance has God had until now? It has been an infinitely sad appearance.  
God's pain is manifested in the world of creation. However, humans do not know. God has not been able to boast. The heart of God, who wants to boast, has been ruthlessly violated.  
Has there been anyone who has held onto God's hand? Has there been a nation? There has not. There have been those who oppose and belittle, but there has been no one who has fulfilled their responsibilities. Moreover, there has been no one who has pushed others to fulfill their responsibilities. Every time someone tried to fulfill their responsibility and fell, God wanted to judge them immediately out of frustration but endured each time. He has endured until Abraham, for 2,000 years, for 400 years of national restoration, and for 2,000 years of national restoration. When Moses was worried about his purpose, was there anyone who cared whether he was naked or clothed, hungry or fed? Everyone robbed him; there was no one who provided a resting place. If he were to pay the price for that sin, nothing would remain. When God judges an individual before Satan, He had to make excuses saying, "I cannot judge because I am not a God for individuals." How sad and miserable is that?  
If He goes out for individuals, everything is crushed. Therefore, God goes out for humanity. However, Satan stumbles over individuals. God says, "Even if individuals fall, I, who sent that individual, will not fall. You deal with individuals, but I deal with the universe." That is why Satan cannot contend with Him. From that standpoint, God is coming to find humanity. The pain we endure in fighting against Satan is indescribable. Of course, God will listen if we inform Him of our circumstances, but we cannot inform God of our circumstances.  
God holds individuals to deal with families, holds families to deal with nations, and holds nations to deal with the world. Thus, a psychological foothold that surpasses one stage is needed. We must understand that God has continued to work, dealing with families, and when that family falls, He raises individuals again.  
No matter how great the pain of an individual, they cannot speak of that pain before God. No matter how great the pain of a family, they cannot speak of that pain. We must pray not for ourselves but for the glory of the Father. We must pray with the heart to hold onto God's ideals and fight against this world. We must not be bound by individuals but be bound by heaven and earth. Since the Father is like that, we must be like that as well.  
We must subdue Satan.  
As the time approaches, God shows not a glorious appearance but an infinitely sad appearance. Therefore, we must shed blood, sweat, and tears. If there are those who oppose, we must make them surrender and defend God. Otherwise, the restoration history will not be fulfilled. In the past, we were cornered and chased, but now we must not be cornered or chased in front of difficulties. We must not die. The forms of environment and connection are the same as in the past, but we must not die, nor must we be pushed out. Why? Because there is the hand of God who is laboring. We must feel that hand. We must hold onto individuals and families.  
Before we show anything to God, what must we do? We must see the Father's appearance and communicate our circumstances, releasing all our frustrations. Only then can we show something of humanity. We ourselves cannot be beings to show anything before God. As fallen beings within the realm of fall, we cannot show anything. Since the historical Father is in such a miserable state, we must repay the Father's enemies and fulfill His wishes.  
That must not be done in glory. Even if Satan guides us to the most perilous places, we must be able to follow without hesitation. Rather, we must go to places where Satan cannot even set foot. We must follow Satan, fight, and win. Only when humanity breaks through the final crisis can God finally say, "My son! My daughter!"  
If we establish conditions to drive out Satan, the Satan who melted thirty million will not be able to take anyone. Then God will come back with hope. God desires to judge. But who has prevented Him from judging for 6,000 years? It is because of people. If He judges unconditionally, Satan will say, "Kill them." The problem is that there are no people, so He cannot judge. God has judged humanity through Noah, Abraham, Moses, and Jesus. God did not directly raise His hand to strike. He judges only through humanity.  
It is not the father who repays the son’s enemies. The son must repay the father's enemies. The enemy must be repaid by oneself or by one's son. If Jesus could not do it, his son must do it. But is there a son of Jesus? Therefore, we must comfort God, who has appeared in a sad form without being able to establish Jesus in the end. He is a sorrowful Father.  
The words "pitiful" and "unjust" must be said in relation to God. The only one who can say "sad," "angry," and "unjust" is the Father alone.  
We must be able to seize Satan, who accuses before the miserable Father, and drive him out. Then where will Satan go? He will go to the bottom of hell. If we drive him out from there, he will flee to the abyss. After that, we must prepare good steeds for the Father, who has fought through a long history, the Father we must serve, the Father who has suffered, and say, "Father, are you coming now?"  
The Father prefers a son who follows Him, even if he is poorly dressed, over a son who is well-dressed but does not follow Him. The one who comforts the Father before He gets angry and curses is the Messiah. We must share in God's sadness, injustice, and anger; otherwise, it becomes a blasphemy against God.  
What kind of appearance has God shown before humanity? Not a glorious appearance but the opposite. People do not know that, but all creation knows. That is why all things groan.  
You must be prepared to endure more pain than those who have suffered historical pain. Even if your arm breaks, you must go. You must go to a place where you can settle the pain, sorrow, and anger.  
Do not be sad. Let us have hope. When we go out, the nation will be able to avoid disaster. This year is an important year in terms of significance; every day is important. It is time to overcome a crisis that Jesus has surpassed.  
Jesus fought at the forefront. We need believers who can inherit Jesus' ideology and fight for God, believers who can fight against Satan until the end. God will make the final decision centered on a certain nation. If God works centered on our Unification Church, what should we do? We must take revenge on our ancestors, who have caused God to be angry, and furthermore, on Satan. You must show in place of God. You must show the most pitiful things. You must show the heart of restoration and the heart of hope. Just as you must not lose God's heart of hope, you must not lose your heart of hope either. You cannot possess God's heart of hope until you drive out Satan.  
Let us show the appearance of fighting for God.  
This struggle is the greatest struggle in the 6,000 years of human history. Right now is a desperate time when even if your father is dying, there is no time to hold onto him. In this process of struggle, God must be able to say, "You are doing evil in my place. You are being persecuted in my place. You are shedding blood and sweat in my place." Only then can restoration and indemnity be achieved. We must fight more bravely than Israel, so that God can say, "Oh, indeed, you are my son." Only after fighting like this can we say that everything is accomplished. Jesus said it is all accomplished, right? He said it was spiritually accomplished, but we must say it is accomplished in the physical realm.  
Now we must show and boast. The Father has shown a sorrowful appearance, but people have not even thought of such a Father. You must be indignant about the sorrowful historical background of the Father and be able to fight in place of the Father. Thus, you must make the Father able to believe. What must you show? You must show the heart of restoration, the heart of hope, and the appearance of fighting against Satan in place of God.  
God wants to see true sons and daughters, true parents, true families, true nations, and a true world that have not fallen. God wanted to rejoice in seeing His beloved sons and daughters governing heaven and earth. From this standpoint, not being able to serve God is a grievance. This grievance is my grievance and at the same time God's grievance.  
God has taken 6,000 years, but we, who are on that foundation, can accomplish it in a period of 6 years, 6 months, or even 6 days. To do this, we must move voluntarily. God is not just for one nation but for the entire world, so we must not stop at one nation but go toward the world.  
What kind of group are you gathered for, and what kind of workers are you? Are you a group gathered to eat well and live well? No. You are a group gathered to fight against Satan. If we fight with strong power, Satan will flee. No one can withstand us. We are a group responsible for all difficulties and pains. We must indemnify the historical sorrow and pain of humanity horizontally.  
These three years are a short period, but it is a time to walk an important path symbolically and figuratively, so we must overcome any difficulties well. We must lead the way in going down the path that this nation does not want to go, and we must be at the forefront of doing what the democratic world does not want to do. If we fall while carrying the heart of restoration and the heart of hope, the body may be dragged away by Satan, but the spirit (soul) cannot be dragged away. This is because it is not spiritually occupied.  
After that, we must enter the era of glory. We must continue to fight, but in the midst of that, we must be able to sing of happiness. Also, we must organize internally in that midst. We must engage in this dual struggle. We must suffer the greatest pain and cause the frontline of Satan to collapse so that they bow their heads before us. On one side, we must engage in a terrifying battle, and on the other side, we must boast of the victorious glory.  
Let us walk the path where we can boast of the appearance of victory.  
What must we do first? After the personal struggle ends, we must engage in family struggles. After the family struggle ends, we must engage in tribal struggles. When tribal struggles arise, the problem is different. Internally, after personal and family struggles end, we must not only fight externally anymore. There are individuals and families found before God, so we must be able to boast of this environment. While going out to fight, we must have something to boast about internally. We must have something we can show. When the frontline becomes the rear and the occupied area expands, and internal development is achieved, only then will God move.  
God has raised Jacob, raised Moses, and raised Jesus, and has been guiding providentially through them. Now, in the end, He will find and establish sons and daughters who can boast personally, a family that can boast as a family, and a tribe that can boast as a tribe. When this reaches a certain level, the world will move. In that case, Satan will be expelled from among thirty million nations.  
We must fight to repay God's enemies and die while witnessing for God.  
I die as Your son. I die for the sons and daughters You are seeking. We must be able to do this. Only then will God boast of us as sons and daughters and bless us.  
Let us return to ourselves and think. Do we have anything to boast about? No. Boasting can only be done after fighting and winning. If we boast without fighting, Satan will accuse us. We must fight in place of the intangible Father, inherit the legacy, and inherit the legacy in place of the coming substantial True Parents. And we must say, "Father, receive glory."  
The slogan for this year is to become those who can show and boast. We must chase the fleeing Satan to the ends. God wants to reveal and boast about individuals and families, so we must fight and win for this. Only then can we become sons and daughters who can connect the spiritual and physical worlds. We must win in the fight to be able to boast. You must fight for the restoration of the heavenly family.  
The year 1962 must be a year to establish a standard that can be shown and boasted about. When fighting, we must fight centered on God or centered on the heavenly family. Thus, we must achieve victory. Even when fighting, we must fight in the most laborious positions. We must start from the most difficult and hard labor, or as beggars, and press down to subdue. We must carry out joint operations with our parents. It is time for parents and children to work together in evangelism. Parents and children, as one family, must fight side by side to restore the heavenly family, tribe, and nation to restore the whole world. From now on, we must fight centered on the family.  
If you become discouraged, that wound will affect the family. If you are pushed out from here, it will be the end. The only thing that the Unification Church must have is the heart of God. That heart goes back and forth between heaven and earth. To the world, we may seem foolish. Even if we spend money, if we can use it in a way that benefits heaven emotionally, there will be no problem.
To show, we must set the highest standard of hardship. Hardship should not be faced alone but should be shared between couples and families. Now is the time to endure hardships not just individually but as families and as a nation. This year, we must walk a path that can be shown to the world on a national level. It is the time to transition to a global stage. *
