The True Birth of Jesus and True Celebration
Luke 2:1-
<Summary of the Word> When God created the heavens and the earth, He desired to establish a true human ancestor to rejoice forever. With the hope of a world where such joy could continue, He created Adam and Eve. 
However, when Adam and Eve rejoiced, gave thanks, and were happy, it would have pleased and glorified God, but due to the Fall, they became the vanguard of hell, and thus God could not be pleased. They should have been able to boast of what God had created for them, but they could not, and so Adam and Eve became the ancestors of shame. 
As they blamed Adam and Eve and everything else, the more they blamed, the more sorrow returned to God. We must restore everything that Adam and Eve committed. Then, when will the sorrow of heaven, humanity, and all creation be resolved? This was to be resolved through the latter Adam, that is, Jesus. The birth of Jesus becomes the starting point of the rebirth of Adam and Eve. 
Through the birth of Jesus alone, the Kingdom of God is re-presented, and all creation is reborn. The birth of the Messiah is the starting point of God's desire for the world to be fulfilled. To meet that moment, hardships have been endured, but the nation of Israel did not respond to God's will. Rather, it was because of the nation of Israel that there was failure. 
If there had been no rebellion from the nation of Israel, Jesus could have established the personal, familial, and national standards. However, due to the disbelief of the nation of Israel, He could not bear the overall responsibility of providence. 
Jesus walked the path of a double cross. One was for the nation of Israel, and the other was to fulfill His own mission. After His resurrection, He returned to His twelve disciples to work. 
Since the nation of Israel did not uphold Him, until the age of 30, He had to establish personal, familial, and tribal standards in order to move toward national standards. 
If Joseph and Mary had become one, familial expectations would have been fulfilled, but in their inability to do so, they bore the double cross of having to establish tribal standards. Unable to unite with the internally chosen nation of Israel, He sought externally to fulfill His purpose by finding the sons and daughters of God, which was the three years of His public ministry. 
While constructing the Kingdom of God, He also aimed to establish the nation of God's sons and daughters and to remove the forces of Satan in the universe, which is God's purpose. Thus, during the three years of public ministry, He fought against Satan while trying to fulfill that purpose. Jesus is the representation of God, the representation of the Kingdom of God, the representation of the Garden of Eden, and the representation of God's love. 
The nation of Israel was meant to be a nation that would not be a sorrowful nation but one that would govern all of heaven and earth, yet it could not be. The God of Israel is the God of Jesus alone, and the name of Israel remains the name of Jesus alone. The nation of Israel should have been able to become a heavenly nation, a heavenly people, and the desire of heaven, but both God's nation and God's people became limited to Jesus alone. 
It should have been a familial and bloodline foundation that could be achieved with Jesus, but it could not be. The witnesses were the same. Joseph and Mary were the same. Jesus was meant to enjoy glory from birth, but that did not happen. This remains until now. The gospel of Jesus became the property of Jesus due to the mistakes of the nation of Israel. Furthermore, because the Messiah could not remain for all people, He remained as God's alone. 
Since Jesus was born only as God's, God who looks upon this must have sighed and regretted it. Mary and Joseph did not know that Jesus was the Christ. 
The first Israel established over 4,000 years has collapsed, and a second Israel has formed with those who believe in Jesus. Since then, God has been working with that group. Jesus walked to fulfill His hopes and dreams for humanity and the hopes of heaven and earth. 
To offer true celebration, we must understand the true appearance of Jesus as He showed before the nation of Israel. God's love is the love of Jesus, and the love of Jesus can be said to be my love. 
Before the heavenly hosts of angels sing praises, we humans must first repent for not having praised. Regardless of emotional differences, today's celebration is the first. If we cannot offer true celebration, we cannot welcome the true one. If He dies, we should be willing to die in His place. 
You must become individuals who can resolve the grievances of the returning Messiah. You should rejoice and love in the position of liberation upon welcoming the Messiah. The Messiah was the center of love, life, joy, and ideals as the prince of the heavenly kingdom. 
Become a qualified person who can appear before the returning Messiah without shame. When comparing your state of heart or life with Jesus, do you truly have confidence? Are you prepared to welcome Him? If not, that is a problem. You must appear as God's family, God's nation, and God's world. You must feel the responsibility to celebrate on behalf of the nation, heaven, and earth to qualify as those who will carry on the lineage of Israel. And you will become the reality of the past representation of Israel. 
Therefore, now you must have the conviction that there should not be a path like the one the nation of Israel took in your end-time journey. You must have such faith. Now, you must prepare and lay the foundation for a global appearance. You must be able to welcome the Lord who comes with the conviction to break away from what has been left as grievances and inherit everything. If you cannot do that, you will not be able to welcome the Lord again. 
You should understand that all past mistakes were due to ignorance and now must receive the new love of the Lord. Today, heaven desires those who celebrated during the time of Jesus more than those who celebrate His birth today. We must become the reality of God and celebrate the birth of Jesus, and after doing so, we must be able to resolve the grievances of the dead Jesus and welcome Him. If we celebrate the Lord's birth with such qualifications, even though 2,000 years have passed, that celebration will hold the greatest significance. 
I hope you realize that the Lord who comes with the heart to forgive all your past mistakes is not an individual but the embodiment of God and the embodiment of the ideals of the entire universe. Become a qualified person for true celebration. 
                  ─ ─    Middle   ─ ─ 
The 6,000-year history is a history in which God has struck individuals, taken individuals away, struck families, taken families away, struck nations, taken nations away, struck the world, and taken the world away. Jesus is the returning embodiment of the central figures who have come and gone throughout history, and the nation is the returning embodiment of Israel. 
Communism symbolizes Cain, democracy symbolizes Abel, and the ideal world symbolizes Seth. The faction that seeks to restore Eden legally keeps the Old and New Testaments. The faction that seeks to restore Eden through truth is a faction that resolves everything through truth. However, now a faction that seeks to restore Eden through love must emerge. Now is the time to gather the highest words in the Bible and fulfill them. 
You are now connected vertically with heaven, but after the center is established, you will connect horizontally. There is nothing that exists beyond emotional connections. If there are true sons and daughters of unity, God will have many expectations of them. He will want to give Himself to them. This has been true in the past, present, and will be true in the future. 
No matter what pain and sorrow there may be, if you succumb to Satan, there will be no way to resolve grievances. So what should you do now? You must establish an emotional standard that no pain, sorrow, or difficulty can block your path. And you must ask the Father to place upon your shoulders and body what He wishes to place upon you. You must be able to express yourself. 
The branches of a tree grow at a 90-degree angle toward the sky. Humans are the lords of all creation, and the lord is a central being. Therefore, humans should not fall no matter what tries to pull them down. Those who are in a 45-degree position have all been bent. 
The teacher did not want to walk this path; he walked it because he had to. Until now, it has been a path of indemnity. God's desire is to fulfill the ideals of creation. We must fulfill that purpose. It is good to have high ideals and aspirations when approaching God, but God's heart is beyond your ideals and aspirations, so you must practice self-restraint. 
If you are God's sons and daughters, you must represent God's heart. To resolve grievances, it must be centered on the heart. Even if the countless spirits of heaven and earth, or the countless spirits of the spirit world, try to trip you up, you must overcome them smoothly. God delights in you resolving the grievances of your closer family members. The teacher is very sensitive to such things. 
God's 6,000-year grievance must be resolved on this earth. When did this grievance begin? It has existed since before the Fall. It is a grievance centered on the ideals of creation. The grievance of the Fall has been added to it. 
Therefore, we must resolve all of God's grievances. Where? It must be done on earth. It must be done by each of you. It cannot be done by anyone other than you as sons and daughters who believe in God. The providence to restore what has fallen due to the Fall and to achieve the work of creation is the history of 6,000 years. We are in a position to resolve all the mistakes we have made until now. 
What will God seek to establish with you? You must be in a position to call God your Father, having been liberated from sin and having your heart and body in harmony. You must devote your heart, mind, and sincerity. To what extent? There is nothing in creation without a purpose. Until the day the purpose is fulfilled... 
This is a time like the autumn harvest season. Everything visible before your eyes, or all that exists in heaven, must come through the heart of the Father. You must advance to the position where you can call anything on earth your Father. 
Your feelings must move your heart and even your emotions. Furthermore, you must move your environment and touch all of creation. 
Critique yourself! What will you show before the love of the Father? You must show something substantial. This is the mutual exchange between man and woman, and between man and woman, and among family members as parents and children, husband and wife, and siblings. You must resolve grievances among family members to resolve the grievances of the Father. *

Become the Substance that Remains as Good Grain
<Summary of the Word> For the nation of Israel heading toward Canaan, would they have entered Canaan with their individual possessions? For us, who are in a historically significant three-year period, having money is rather futile and causes many obstacles on the way. 
When the nation left Egypt to return to Canaan, if there were those who did not receive notice and could not leave together, then those who were responsible for the notice must take responsibility until the end. Similarly, if there are those among us at the end who say they could not follow because they did not receive this news, they will not be able to escape responsibility. Therefore, during these three years, we must ensure that there are no compatriots who say they could not follow because they did not hear the news of our Unification Church, and we must spread this news to every corner. 
Now, anyone who possesses the heart of those who have come and gone throughout history can connect emotionally even from a flat position. Furthermore, the ancestors of history are supporting our believers. They are cooperating with those who live on the ground through spiritual exchanges. We are in such a position of privilege. 
If we were to offer a salary to you who are suffering outside, who would give that salary? It would be given by God. In that case, your labor has already been compensated, and that labor becomes God's work. As a result, you are merely hired hands. Therefore, you must endure hardships. 
When you first accepted this purpose sincerely, you must convey it to others sincerely as well. 
We are no different from century-old refugees. In fact, we must become refugees. Those who take responsibility for something must be deeply affected by it. I worry that you may leave conditions of regret, thinking, "If I had done it this way when I die, or if I had not done it that way..." A baby that has grown only on nutrients from its mother does its first bowel movement immediately after birth. How can there be feces when it has not eaten anything? Yet, there is definitely feces. Likewise, there are such beings among those who work for good history. There will be people like that excrement, so please do not become a being that is discarded like waste but become the substance that remains as good grain. 
Leaders must not overestimate themselves. Do not incur debts of heart. Even if you are in a position of responsibility, always be a learner. *

53)
God and Our Property is Heart
Romans 8:12-
<Summary of the Word> There are many people on earth who are suffering with grievances. We have relatives and friends with whom we can express these grievances. However, God has no such objects. 
We have lived thinking that pain or sorrow has nothing to do with God. In reality, even if humans have great grievances, no matter how resentful an enemy may be, these are all within certain limits. However, the anger and grievances of heaven are historical. 
Humans think and pursue various things to resolve grievances. However, no matter how sad things may be, God could not express that sadness. This is because this world is one governed by enemies. 
While there are various words to express human unhappiness, God's unhappiness cannot even be articulated. How can God's unhappiness be compared to human unhappiness! 
Humans are unhappy. We must go to find unhappy humans. Since it is humans who have caused pain to God, humans must resolve God's unhappiness. 
God's grievances are century-old and global. God is leading history and is heading toward the day of judgment. Those who take the lead in this must understand God's heart. 
Why must the loving God receive offerings? It is because He is in suffering. Therefore, no path can avoid the process of offerings. Humans cannot prevent themselves from entering a miserable position. Why is that? It is because heaven seeks to establish human misery as God's. 
God sacrifices individuals to establish families, societies, and nations. That is why the seven-year great tribulation must occur. The ones who can receive the final call at the judgment seat will be the miserable people. 
Those who seek the Messiah cannot be granted happiness and peace. Heaven, humanity, strike me! Even if everything throughout history is mobilized to strike me, only those who can overcome that will become the final victors. 
No matter how much pressure there may be from the world of Satan, when you fall, do not fall alone but hold onto God and fall, just like Jesus. The nation of Israel fell...
I could not hold onto God while I was failing.
If America fails in its mission moving forward, the tower built until now will collapse. Even if it falls, it must fall while holding onto God.
We must be able to say, "Father, please resolve Your resentment through me." No, we must be able to say, "From now on, let us start a new history."
In such a position, we must lay the foundation of our hearts with God for a new history to begin. Only such people can become the vanguards of a new era.
Now is the age of ideologicalism. It is also the age of globalism. We must understand the relationship between the world to come and ourselves. The greater the difference in that relationship, the more it manifests as suffering. Now is an unhappy time. The greater this unhappiness, the sooner a blessed world will come.
The heart has drawn a straight line from the individual to the cosmos and has expanded its external form. Therefore, what humans must understand is ① the heart of the fall ② the heart of restoration ③ the heart of resurrection. This has been passed down historically, but you must be able to feel the entirety of this era in a flat manner today.
When Jacob suffered, everyone had to suffer in response.
I must understand that I am the embodiment of the past individuals, families, nations, and the nation itself in a heartfelt way.
When asked, "Who are you?" I must be able to say, "I am the restored Adam, the restored Noah." Only then can I judge Adam and Noah. In short, the heart must be centered for judgment to be established.
We must become the substance that can resolve resentment by uniting spirit and flesh. Such a person is historical, epochal, and futuristic.
We must have the heart of God before and after creation and throughout the process to be able to govern. The final judgment is to determine whether one has become such a victorious being. Such a person must overcome the temptations or trials faced by Adam, the trials of Noah, the trials of Abraham, and any terrible trials faced by Moses. They must stand in a position where the hardships of 40 years in the Midian wilderness or the death on the cross are not an issue. They must stand in a position where it is okay even if God strikes them. Only then can they indemnify and restore what has been betrayed to God.
Can a world that one does not even think or hope for become theirs? We must have the ability to judge the dead and the living. How wonderful it would be if we could transcend the peaks of historical figures and move toward God!
Have you ever prayed to bear the burdens of any historical figure? Have you ever felt that the God who has harbored resentment throughout history is shining upon a hopeful day while looking at the morning sunlight and the evening starlight?
The God who created us is saddened by seeing us, and thus all creation groans. No one is without the burden of food. If they say otherwise, they will be resentful. If they form an alliance, humanity will collapse within ten days. So, all of humanity will say they live because of themselves. We, who live under the burden of food, might even say we are less than food.
When we think this way, all creation becomes universal. The ability to govern these things as one's own is solely because one has the heart of God. This is only possible when the condition of being one with God's heart is established.
God and our property is the heart.
Among all elements of the Word, the center is the heart. The Word existed from the beginning. God is saddened because this has been severed. The providence of restoration is to reconnect this. Those who reconnect this are the substance of historical representation.
Jesus comes looking forward to a day of heartfelt representation. God can conquer and then rest. Until now, no matter how much we have sighed, we have not sighed centered on this heart.
We must be able to digest everything with the heart that substitutes for God. Conquer your enemies with your heart! God and our property is the heart.
Be a historical filial son.
Genesis 1:27
<Summary of the Word> Seeking ideology cannot be anything but blessed. Humanity has sought blessings, but no one has lived a blessed life. What is the limit of blessing? Power or fame are fleeting. True blessing coexists eternally.
True blessing cannot be exchanged for the fallen humanity or the entire earth, nor for any created being.
The driver of blessing is love.
The command to govern means to govern not only all things but also God.
One cannot receive blessings without being a blessed person. God has promised to give blessings. However, we must become people who can receive God's blessings. Blessing resides where the heart eternally dwells. Where blessings go becomes the focal point of God's heart.
Therefore, we must be able to hear the words, "You are a blessed person; I am yours." One cannot be a blessed person alone.
We must ride over the peaks of historical figures. We must even ride over Jesus. Jesus hopes for this too. This is the heart of a parent.
Do not be a person living in the era; be a person living in history.
February 25, 1962 (Sunday) night, former headquarters church.
* This message was given while rearranging the leaders of the Seoul district, and what former Association President Yoo Ho-won recorded in his notebook has been organized. The title was added by the editor.
Be a historical filial son.
If we do not live this way and someone emerges who practices a heart-centered life beyond us, we will fall behind. Therefore, we must walk the blessed path.
What remains is only suffering. If you enjoy receiving this, the only gift I can give you is this. You must meet the Father in a place of suffering to become an eternal being.
Do not be a person of the era; be a historical filial son.
The path to becoming a direct descendant.
<Summary of the Word> When God strikes a nation and people who cannot fulfill their mission from the position of a servant, it is after God Himself has suffered much more pain. Therefore, God is a pitiful God.
There is a complicated procedure to move from the position of a servant to that of a son. Christianity is a religion that has the authority of a son.
Now is the time to move from the position of a son to that of a direct descendant. A son is different from the start. Body, mind, heart, and lineage are different from the parents. However, a direct descendant shares the same lineage as the parents.
The pain of the parents is in that bloodline, and all the good and evil of the parents are in that bloodline. A child is born as a little one, but that child has a connection to the source where the parents grew. Everything of an 80-year-old's life is connected to even a 10-year-old child.
When grafting, a standard must be established where sap can come out from both sides to harmonize. To graft, one must cut cleanly. You cannot graft onto an old tree. No matter how big the tree is, everything must be cut away to graft. Telling the end-time saints to give up everything is to prepare for grafting.
It is the work of history. Therefore, when viewed from a servant's perspective, Jesus is a parent, and when viewed laterally, He is a bridegroom. Of course, He also referred to men as brides. Thus, men must long for Jesus. They must stand in a position where their bodies are not their own.
One must become a person who can judge oneself to be able to judge the world. All historical figures started from the position of "Am I the only one left?"
Loving parents must be even slightly better than loving children. The scale of the way of virtue is the children.
Creation was due to God's heart, so one can say that there was heart before everything existed. Therefore, although we live in modern times, our hearts have participated in all of history from the time God created.
We must move from the position of a servant to that of a son, to that of a couple, to that of a parent, and ultimately to the position of oneness with God, so we cannot avoid a difficult path.
Let us be those who meet a joyful day.
<Summary of the Word> Until you came here, your living environments and methods of living were all different. However, now that you are attending this training session, you must abandon all past habits and ideas and start a new life. The first 6 days to a week will be a testing period for you. Here, you must adopt the position of closing your eyes tightly and saying that you do not exist. Of course, there will be many inconveniences compared to the free life you lived in the past in your own way. However, all the seniors from the past nine sessions completed them gallantly and joyfully, so I hope you will also send it off with a joyful heart. You may have expected to be treated well when you come to the headquarters, but do not have any such expectations at all; just keep your eyes focused ahead and listen diligently to the instructor's words.
Today, the title of the message I particularly want to share with you is:
Let us be those who meet a joyful day.
A world of existence that wishes to be joyful even in sadness.
Regardless of whether a person is talented or not, or knowledgeable or ignorant, all humans live in days of sadness. There has not been a single person from the past until today who has not experienced this. It is not just people; all creation is also in a state of sadness.
However, all created beings, including humans, desire to be joyful. They wish to meet joyful times and joyful days. The Creator also undoubtedly wishes to meet a joyful day.
I cannot escape this principle (the principle of wanting to be joyful).
All of you are here to meet a joyful day in every direction—front, back, left, right, up, and down. Each of you may think, "I am good enough." However, what you present cannot be accepted as joyful before the entire universe. Perfect joy can only exist after distinguishing between good and evil. Since you are all still in an undifferentiated environment, you cannot boast. Because humanity is in a fallen state, there is nothing to show or boast about before all creation.
Even if I can be in a position where I can be joyful when viewed from the north, south, east, and west, I do not want to be satisfied. People are never satisfied with that. Thus, it is unfortunate. We must fight against this element of unwanted dissatisfaction. We must fight whether we win or fall.
We are like soldiers on the front line.
What position is God, who created humans, in now? Is He enjoying joy? The omniscient and omnipotent God has not yet met a joyful day. This is because the world He created has not manifested as an object of joy. Therefore, God and the created world are undergoing a tragic operation.
Since the fall of humanity, what kind of days has God been in? He has been in days of sadness. Therefore, we humans have also lived in days of sadness, and all creation has passed through days of sadness. All things must meet a joyful day. God is joyful, but humans are sad, and humans are joyful, but all things are sad; this cannot be.
God's laughter must be met with laughter from humans and all creation, but it has not yet been so.
The reason we walk a more meaningful and valuable path is to find a day when God and the entire universe can rejoice together. You are merely saying that you will meet a joyful day with words. Was there any condition in your past life that could bring joy to God? Those without such conditions are dealt with in hell. It is like isolating incurable patients today, like lepers.
The history that has passed has all been days of sadness. Humanity is stepping up this path of sadness step by step. This is the phenomenon of historical development. Who are those who have been called sages throughout history?
They are those who said, "I now die; O God, please hold onto me."
"Love the Lord your God with all your heart, with all your soul, and with all your strength," but in fact, it should also include "with all your life." God does not leave those who are falling; He intends to save them. We must hold onto those whom God is trying to hold onto. To hold onto them, we must do so with all our heart, all our will, all our character, and all our life.
The joint task of God and humanity.
Thus, a leader is needed here. Then, where is our universal leader, our conscientious leader? The most central figure is not any human but the One who created heaven and earth. Therefore, that God is telling us to believe in Him rather than the world. Trusting in humans will lead to ruin. Those who wish not to perish must seek God. God is the Absolute Being. Religion has emerged to seek the Absolute Being by pioneering the heart before all humanity.
God is also working hard to meet a joyful day. However, God cannot meet that day alone. It must be done jointly with humanity. Regardless of the era, it is common sense for humans to call upon heaven. If there is someone who has not lost hope, unlike the dead, the direct call of conscience cannot be official. God knows everything.
"God, please save us" is the final declaration and will. Those who know this cannot fall. There may be progress, but there cannot be regression. Heaven knows. That is the destination of humanity.
Even if a parent calls their children and teaches them to become certain types of people and to do certain types of work, teaching them to know God is far superior. To become a person who knows God is the highest teaching. Saying "God!" before dying is the legacy that countless people must leave behind. Even amidst continuous sadness, the final words should be "I know God."
When one’s child is sentenced to death as a murderer, there is not a single parent who would say, "Thank you, God, for my child dying." Regardless of the law, they would say, "God, please save our child."
The same goes for wicked people. Even Satan has such a heart, which is why the providence of restoration is unfolding.
It is more valuable to suppress one's anger and say "God!" than to appear with a knife in hand. Many people walking the path of virtue are unknowingly walking such a path. When they realize that there is a hidden hand of heaven in that, they should all be able to say, "Thank you." When there is anger that must be released immediately, saying "God, you know" is more valuable than anything else. Those who can do that will be able to appear in this world with joy.
The more difficult and complicated life is, the more those who shout "Father!" in that situation are the ones who will win in the way of virtue. Ordinary people live their own lives, but those on the path of virtue must have the heart that all the wrongs of my family, my nation, or the world are my sins and my mistakes. Only then can they be said to be people who hold onto God. They must be able to communicate with God and be those who can declare "God." If not, God will have to seek another person.
A will from one generation aligns with God's will, saying, "What is yours is mine." The one who comes to establish a position where this can be said is the Messiah. This person must come and find a joyful day on behalf of humanity on this earth. Is there an individual, family, nation, or world that can make a historic will? If not, we will perish.

You, the trainees gathered here, must welcome a joyful day with heaven. You must not become a pitiful being that collapses into the cauldron of destruction, holding onto a troubled past. When comparing the past me to the present me, the present must be improved. Those who cannot do this are obstacles to welcoming a joyful day. Have you improved compared to the past? Raise your hands if you have. (All hands raised) That's how it should be.

Is it bad or good to think that you have been lacking not only in knowledge and health but in every aspect? It is good. That is a good thought. However, in the midst of such worries, you must be able to think about what the Creator would be like with your eyes raised high.

This place is incredibly solemn and sacred. It is not about having ten million or a hundred million won. The issue is how much you have improved. 

Why is God sad? In the past, it was acceptable to only have graduated from elementary school in the countryside. But now, one may feel inadequate. Now, even at the dining table, we must say, "God!" and even in the place of hunger, we must say, "God!" The sources of our suffering have increased. The greater our suffering, the lower the threshold of suffering in this world becomes. When we roll around due to that suffering, the suffering of the world is pushed away. Now, the prince of despair in heaven and earth must take his leave.

If there is someone who calls upon God with a greater grievance than the sorrow for this thirty million nation, will God not say, "My beloved son, my beloved daughter!"? The more such people there are, the more God's sorrow will disappear. Both humans and God have not been able to escape the environment of sorrow until now, so to break free from this, we must resolve God's sorrow as soon as possible. When we say that God's sorrow and grievance are all ours and take responsibility for each other, God's grievance, the nation's grievance, the world's grievance, and my grievance will be resolved.

God is not trying to make humans suffer. Because humans have committed acts of corruption, they must fight within the realm of indemnity that God has prepared. This fight must be done by humans. Many must emerge who carry a cosmic grievance and fight. Unless such people appear, God's wishes will not be fulfilled. If there are such responsible individuals, a group that walks that path must appear. This is where the Unification Church has emerged.

I am a historical being. I am the one from the time of Noah and Abraham. Many historical figures must appear who can leave behind a will like this. After the period of national struggle and the period of global struggle, when liberation comes, God's wishes will be fulfilled, and the world that will be realized then is the ideal world. In the past, I focused on my family and my village, but after training, I must embrace this world and move forward, holding onto the desires of heaven and earth. In the end, God will gather such people. Even today, He needs such people. Creating such people is the mission of the Unification Church.

We have hope to welcome a joyful day. Here lies the secret to welcoming that day. First, if I exist, there is front and back, left and right, up and down. And there is past, present, and future. I must become the one who turns around and seeks history, and the one who seeks my ancestors. Am I that person?

Why has God not become the God of joy? Because God has turned back on the path He has walked, He is a pitiful God and a sorrowful God. Because He cannot go the way of the future and must turn back to the past, He cannot be the God of joy. Turning back means losing everything, which is why He is a sorrowful God. If God does not turn back, humanity cannot have a day of hope. Therefore, we must follow the path where God walks backward.

"O God! Where are You going?" We must become humans who weep while holding onto God as He returns to Eden.

The path God walks is not a smooth one. It is the valley of sorrow. We should shout loudly upon seeing that path, but we do not even know the direction. There, we say, "Oh, how frustrating! It is blocked. I will suffocate." But now, we are in a situation where we cannot even call upon God or hold onto Him. Even if we are left with only bones, humanity must follow God, yet we do not know the direction. If we collapse here, God must leave us and return. We are those who only call upon God when we are torn apart and dying.

We have felt the powers of darkness encroaching since ancient times. Why have we become orphans? If we cut off our wrists, there is no one to protest. We are a pitiful people without sovereignty. We are a pitiful sight without sovereignty. If we want to find sovereignty, we must call upon God with all our hearts and intentions. However, God cannot come down again. Satan prevents God from coming. Therefore, we must go to the place where Satan cannot follow, no matter how treacherous the mountains and roads are. This path is the way of indemnity. We must create a safe zone where God can dwell, a place where Satan cannot follow.

God has governed history through good people, good families, and good nations. The saints of the past walked paths where Satan could not go. They walked the paths that everyone despised. They went through the way of suffering to understand what heart is, what love is, and what truth is. This is the path that humanity must walk.

What kind of church is the Unification Church? It is a church that tunnels through mountains and builds bridges over valleys. It is the frontline church that confronts the ironclad Satan. Here, an attitude of taking responsibility for Satan alone is necessary. When you cannot do it with all your might, you must ask God for cooperation. Then God will cooperate.

How joyful was this nation and this people at the liberation of August 15? Now we must liberate God. There is only one such group in heaven and earth. The goal is to liberate God. Only when God can relax and smile will a day of joy and liberation come to the world. Therefore, there must be a responsible group to take that on. How blessed it is that such a thought can be realized in this half of the world!

So what is the secret to finding this good day? How will we seek that one day? The secret is that there is past, present, and future... We have walked a long and sorrowful historical path until now. Tomorrow must be better than today, and the day after tomorrow must be better than tomorrow. I must establish today’s self to be better than yesterday’s self, and next year must be better than this year by at least a fist's worth. Knowledge is important, but we must also live in a way that improves our character in heart and body; otherwise, we will become dropouts.

Do not become a dropout in the future. Do not be discouraged by today’s desolate reality. Do not lose hope because there is a future. If the path is blocked and no other nation or person can go, even if we are the weakest group, we must break through that path. Then we will become a blessed group. In a good environment, we can dance to the music. But if we are told to carry a heavy burden and cross the hill, can we do that?

All of this must be dedicated to God, and if there are those who say they will do so, everyone will have no choice but to offer everything before them. Koreans have inevitably experienced sorrow, despair, and failure. But we must be able to magnificently overcome such despair. And we must step forward, saying we will work for God. Wouldn’t God be pleased with that?

Until now, I have only sighed, but from now on, let the American people and the communists compare themselves to me. I will walk the path that you cannot and will not collapse on. This is the confidence we must have. When they collapse fighting among themselves, let us raise the flag of victory. This is the position of a saint. The Unification Church teaches such things.

Tomorrow must be better than today, and the day after tomorrow must be better than tomorrow. We must keep improving. To do this, we must endure much hardship. We must suffer to the point of breaking our bones. Whether studying or farming, we cannot achieve good results in comfort. The cross must accompany us.

A great leader is someone who discovers the path that life must take. Even if you are burdened with the suffering of six thousand years, you must be willing to do so. You must become a leader who can say, "I will risk my life," and even if you collapse while going, you can say, "Thank you." Then the world will belong to you. Even if you fall, if you fall in such a position, the fortune of heaven and earth will move, and you can conquer heaven and earth. Jesus died but conquered the world.

Our mission is to gather the young men and women scattered across this three thousand li of territory, train them, and create loyal subjects, filial children, and virtuous women who can completely resolve the historical grievances.

Become a person who makes God happy. 

Unification Church members may be pushed into places of sorrow and suffering. If you fall while exerting all your strength there, will you perish? If that path is the way, you will not perish. The teacher has the disposition to push you into such a path. What kind of place are you in now? It is a historical place that transitions from today to tomorrow. You, the young people, must step forward, saying, "All historical people, come! I will take the beating for you. I will die in your place." If I, who used to run away from difficulties, now declare that I will become the watchman of a new history, is that a bad thing or a good thing?

God is bound to become the possession of those who strive, so the new era must surely say, "Please entrust me with Your labor." Those who fight cannot help but become God's possession. Therefore, take responsibility and fight. The ideal of the Unification Church is to create people who can bring anything to God. Let today be better than yesterday, and tomorrow be better than today. Then you can become the prince of joy.

The teacher is at the headquarters but wishes to travel around the nation several times a day. Moreover, I want to see the entire world and even heaven. Today, I must become a more valuable person than I was yesterday. Our God! The voice calling out to God must be louder than the cries of countless religious people and saints. And the Father will surely listen to our words. We must pray with confidence that we can do so.

I must become the kind of person who can make God happy. I must pave an unchanging expectation that heaven, earth, and all things can eternally envy, so that the whole can rejoice. When that happens, the day of joy that we hope for will begin.

Only the heart can accompany heaven. 

<Summary of the Words> When humans face a sorrowful event, they can express their feelings to their siblings, children, or comrades. However, until now, God has not been able to speak of His grievances even to His beloved children. Thus, God is in infinite pain, sorrow, and lamentation, yet He has not been able to reveal Himself to humanity. The suffering of humans is nothing compared to God's suffering.

God, who could not speak of His own misfortune. 

Even if humans have grievances, they are grievances of one generation, and humans spare no effort to resolve them. However, the grievance of heaven is a historical grievance, and the enemy of heaven is a historical enemy. Therefore, no matter how great a grievance humans may hold, they cannot present it before heaven. Humans can express their grievances to those who are blood relatives, tribes, or nations, but God cannot do so. Why? Because this world is a world of enemies, and humans are children of enemies. Even if there is historical pain, misfortune, or injustice, God cannot say to humans, "I have this injustice." 

Even if He has the anguish and pain of being torn apart by enemies, He cannot appeal to humans. God has circumstances that cannot be compared at all to human circumstances.

Humans must be thoroughly unhappy. All of humanity must be thoroughly unhappy. Since humans have made God, who should not be unhappy or in pain, unhappy and in pain, humanity on this earth must enter the place of suffering. God has historical misfortune. To resolve this misfortune, God is still leading history and striving toward the day of judgment. Who should take the lead in that? Those who know God must take the lead. The one who understands the will must become the offering.

Why must God, who should sing of ideal peace, receive offerings of sheep and cattle? If it is true, one must go through the process of offering.

We cannot prevent humans from going toward miserable places. This is the result of the sins committed by humans. God intends to connect humanity's misery to His own. Thus, God has expanded from individuals to families, tribes, nations, and the global era as a result of His own collapse. Jesus collapsed with a global purpose. God accompanied Him in that. Although humans do not know, God takes responsibility and comes forth.

In Christianity, it is said that there will be seven years of great tribulation at the end. Those who can be called during that time will not be those who sing of happiness or receive envy. The seven years of great tribulation are not familial but global, so we must overcome it with a global heart. The one who comes to take responsibility for all of this is the Messiah who will come at the end.

Those who walk the path of heaven cannot eat properly or dress as they wish. Moreover, nouns like happiness and peace are not permitted. So what must we do?

Heaven, all humanity, strike! Walk the heart that connects the past history to the present and future. Strike against the enemies of the past, the enemies of the present, and the enemies that will appear in the future, as well as the satanic forces of the spirit world. To indemnify historical misfortune, even if the surrounding environment mobilizes to strike me down, I must be able to overcome it. Only then will I become a victor. 

How can there be no unhappiness when there are satans?

Even if you fall, you must hold onto God and fall. This is the life of a believer. When we look back at history, Abel, Moses, and Jesus all fell as loyal children. However, the families of Adam, Noah, and Abraham, as well as the nation of Israel, could not hold onto God and fell. Even if you become the prince of misfortune, you must not fall under the noun of misfortune. Rather, you must fall while holding onto heaven, and only then will the heavenly purpose be fulfilled.

"Please resolve all my misfortunes." Only then will a national beginning be established from there.
Falling down while holding onto God is how the foundation of the heart is left behind, leading to development. Even if you fall, if you hold onto God with the thought of hope, saying "God!", you can become an heir of the new era. This is the principle.

Heart and Restoration through Indemnity
Now is the age of ideology and the age of globalism. It is not the time for families centered around children to serve tribes or nations, but rather the world. In such a time, what will I become, and what will the world become? What is the relationship between the world and today’s me? The greater the difference, the greater the suffering and unhappiness, which we must overcome. Only then can historical unhappiness be indemnified. It cannot be done otherwise.

Looking at the past and the present, we will face elements of unhappiness in the future as well. This is the time when we feel the persistent unhappiness and pain. The greater the unhappiness, especially if it is global or cosmic, the sooner the blessed time will return. All the complexities of reality must pass away for the ideal world to be realized. Countless people are suffering in pain and are either starving or living unjustly. Did not Jesus pray in the Garden of Gethsemane? 

The world He desired was like this, yet today’s world is like this. He prayed with a lament.

Only the Heart Can Accompany Heaven
We must go beyond the peak of offerings. The marrow of the heart has expanded outward in a straight line. As we expand our environment globally, centered on the individual, family, tribe, and nation, God’s heart has been passed down through those who have taken on that mission. To achieve restoration through indemnity, we must understand the content of the heart. First is the heart of the fall, second is the heart of restoration, and third is the heart of resurrection. We must understand these three stages of the heart.

God's magnificent ideal has been shattered. Therefore, from a value perspective, all people in history are in a position like that of an unborn child in the womb. The Second Coming refers to the birth of a world-historical prince. The child in the womb is influenced by everything the mother experiences. All people scattered across today’s world are dead. No matter how much I claim to be someone, we are all dead. Without knowing the heart of the fall and going through the path of restoration, we cannot resurrect. The historical heart must become the foundation of our present and future lives. Whether one is talented or not, this heart must be known.

If there is a grievance in heaven since the fall of humanity, it is that there is no heartistic being. We need owners of the heart who can represent the individual, family, tribe, nation, world, and heaven and earth.

Who are you? You must be able to say, "I am the historical Adam, Eve, Noah, Abraham, and so on." We must hold onto God with the heart of our fall, the heart of restoration, and the heart of resurrection, shedding tears. We must be able to say this.

How will the loving God judge? He will judge with the heart. When He asks, "Are you like my son or daughter?" and brings forth heart issues, who can receive praise before the Father? We must be able to say, "I am the entity that can resolve grievances." We must have the conviction that "I am the entity that can resolve grievances." Such a person is not just an individual but a historical, epochal, and future being. They are the embodiment of God's hope.

To govern all things is not something anyone can do. It is said in reference to a heartistic being. All creation seeks the governance of one who possesses the heart of God before creation and the heart of hope after creation. All things in the universe are within my heart realm and, moreover, they belong to me. We must be able to say this. Through the heart, we must establish connections with the entire cosmos and claim it as our own. Then, the paths of Adam, Noah, Abraham, and Jacob will not be problematic. The path of Moses will also not be an issue. The death of Jesus on the cross will not be a problem either.

Even if this human world is filled with vermin and God forsakes it, I cannot change. I swear by God's heart that I will not change. I will not change. Only then can there be heartistic indemnity.

We must think sorrowfully about the fact that we cannot bear the pain of the cross that Jesus endured. Can we feel God's heart through non-principled pain? No. Who will bring us what we do not think or hope for? We must shed tears. You must know this and shed tears to become a historical being.

In the Book of Revelation, it says that the dead and the living will be judged, but how will the dead and the living be judged? By the heart. Even when walking, we must walk with the heart of Adam, Noah, Moses, Jesus, and God.

Creation in Lamentation
How pitiful is God, who entrusts His will to us, who are so insignificant? Yet, have you ever prayed, "Please hold me responsible for even a part of Adam, Noah, Abraham, Moses, or Jesus?" Have you done so? God, who knows the hearts of Abraham, Moses, and Jesus, longs for someone who possesses even greater heart. But have you ever prayed seriously about the historical circumstances of that twist and turn? Have you looked at the rising dawn that brightly illuminates the heavens and the earth, or felt the historical grievance and hope while observing the twinkling starlight in the dark night sky? God feels sorry even for seeing sunlight or moonlight. Since the blessing of establishing a son to govern all things has been reversed, how can God have any face?

It is indeed true that all creation laments. It does not lament because it is in pain, but because the God who created it laments. There is not a single thing that does not harbor grievances among those that are flailing their arms and colliding with each other. Therefore, humans should at least know how to feel sad, but where is such a person? Who will resolve this realm of lamentation? God cannot do it alone. Creation cannot do it either. Satan cannot do it even more. Satan only brings destruction. Only humans can do it. Therefore, at the very least, we must be comrades in sorrow. Otherwise, we are rebels.

Why have you come to a path that others do not take? This path is a serious one that our descendants must walk if we do not. If we do not do this work, who will? The same goes for the teacher. We must walk this path.

Are you not ashamed before all creation? Is there anyone from the past, present, or future who has not depended on others for food? When asked, "Do you feel good about serving three meals a day?" the answer would be, "Ah! It’s unfair," and what about your comrades? They are all the same. What would happen if all those meals went on strike at once? This noisy world would become quiet all at once.

Food will speak to humanity. It will say, "You worthless humans who only depend on me! You have only depended on me since the time of Adam and Eve." No matter how much the words of Jesus are called the words of life, if food goes on a union strike, everything becomes impossible. So, is it only food? It is not even as good as food. If it were human-like, it would say, "You humans!" And then it would ask the air, "What about our connection?" It would say, "I occupy the entirety of humanity inside and out." If the air were to go on a union strike, all of humanity would die within seven minutes. Even the muddy ground at the end of the rainy season would boast loudly.

My tail stretches across the world, and two-thirds of the earth belongs to me. If the land protests and seeks its original value, nothing will remain in this world. The same goes for the sun. If you eat without singing praises or even greeting, it is theft.

What must there be for us to treat all creation as our own? What are the conditions under which humans can live with the special value of being the lords of creation? It is to possess the heart of God, who existed before all things and will exist forever. Having the heart of God allows us to surpass everything. Only when we establish connections with the center, that is, the root, can human value be determined. That is the heart. This heart has been with God since the beginning. When we command with this heart, all creation will respond, "Yes, that is right. Thank you." It is set to be so.

But why do God and all creation lament? It is because the connection of this heart has been severed. The history of restoration and resurrection is to reconnect this severed heart. There is no logic to deny that you are my Father, and I am your son or daughter regarding God. No one can deny it. The heartistic connection between a father and child cannot be denied by anything.

Possess the Heart of the Father
Even though the world is divided, when we see believers eagerly awaiting the day of hope, we can know that God is alive.
