Humans are originally the princes of the universe. We can say, "God is my Father, and the heavens and the earth that belong to my Father are mine." We must conquer God to finally find rest. When we conquer God's heart, we conquer God. We must embrace all things centered on God's heart; only then can no one else conquer, and from there, the heavenly fortune will move, and the blessings of the world will dwell, opening the Garden of Eden. The place where God, humans, and all creation, as well as heaven, humanity, and earth, unite heartistically is the paradise on earth. It cannot be without the heart. In a place where historical circumstances and the heart are connected, there is no one who will say it is painful, unfair, or frustrating.

You must live with three hearts. Do not take any pain as a grievance but digest it with your heart. Just as God did, you must become someone who can digest it with your heart. You must conquer your enemies, not with swords or fists, but with your heart. God does not conquer with weapons. Since God has not yet established His dignity, we too must live humbly and meekly, like fools, bowing our heads. God's suffering has become the foundation of victory, and Jesus' sacrifice has become a blessed place for future generations. We must conquer this world even if we become naked. This is God's wish.

What should your wealth be? What is worth possessing is not wealth or honor but the heart. You must become a companion of God's historical heart. With a naked body, you must become a counterpart to God's heart and navigate through the harsh winds of the enemy's world, which is like a wasteland. Even when you sleep, do not sleep for yourself, and even when you eat, do not eat for yourself. You must sleep and eat for your family, for your Father, and on behalf of the 3 billion people of the world.

Do not be crushed by the two characters of unhappiness; you must win the global battlefield with hope, which is what Unification Church members must do.

If humans shed tears with the historical heart that says, "My Father is my Father," the value of those tears will be more precious than anyone or any loyal subject in history. Let us seek the lost Father, the Father who sheds tears. We do not want to welcome a God who sings of happiness, but a God who comes bearing the cross. This is the duty of a loyal subject. Those who eat a spoonful of rice and fall may become representatives of the times, but those who shed tears while thinking of heaven, even if they cannot eat a spoonful of rice, will stand on historical value.

As we know through the work of Saint Francis, how happy it is when all creation, that is, all beings, support us! Of course, you have likely faced much persecution during this time. I am sorry. But it cannot be helped, for the Father has done so. Instead, possess the Father and possess the heart of the Father. This year is a significant period. Please keep this in mind and work diligently.

What We Must Do
<Summary of the Message> You, who have different circumstances, have gathered to achieve a common goal, leading complex lives. There have been many lonely times and many hardships. On the other hand, I believe you have also had many realizations. Now, as the 10th training participants, we have reached the last day of the training that we can no longer have. We are spending a day that will become a memory in the future. I thank those who guided us, the training leaders, family members, and all the participants.

The title of the message I want to give you today is "What We Must Do." There are still things to be done in heaven, things to be done on earth, and things to be done for humanity. From the very large to the very small, there are certainly things that must be done. Both good and evil appear in this process. There is a cosmic proposition here, so we must recognize that both joy and sorrow are before our eyes.

When We Must Feel That God's Work Is Our Work
Every task has a purpose, a mission to be shared, and a time to carry it out. The Creator, who created the heavens and the earth, is in the same position. Any being in heaven and earth has a responsibility to fulfill. God does not desire bad things. So what does God desire? It is for the protagonists of heaven and earth and all creation to unite and fulfill the purpose of creation. Due to the fall of humanity, God, humans, and all creation could not unite and have become divided. The work of God and the work of humans have become different. God's hopes and human hopes have diverged, and God's happiness and human happiness have become different. This aspect has manifested as despair through life and history.

Until now, humanity has engaged in personal, familial, and at most, national matters. However, God has worked not just on the level of individuals, families, or nations but has dealt with the issues of the cosmos. God has worked towards a standard where all creation can rejoice at the same time as He rejoices. Regardless of the hardships faced, there has been no change. Humans did not know, but God has labored and fought for this purpose. However, humans did not know what work God was doing and what kind of relationship God had with us.

So what must we do now? It is to align our work with God's purpose rather than work for the individual. Only then can God's position and our position become the same. The time has come when we must thoroughly feel that what God does is what I do, and my work is God's work. God's work is cosmic, and historically, countless ancestors have cooperated in it. From Adam to Noah, Abraham, Moses, Jesus, and up to today, God has involved ancestors in this work, but no one has clearly understood this work. No one has known God's will and acted accordingly, so God's work remains as it is. We must understand this. God has never forgotten or been careless about this purpose for even a single moment.
Since the fall of humanity, humans have forgotten God, but God has never forgotten us and has tirelessly worked for our sake. 

You each need to reflect on the questions: Who do I live for? Who have I lived for? You will realize that you have lived only for yourself, your parents, or your siblings. So, what should we do now? God's will is such and such, but we have not lived according to that will; therefore, we must feel regret, reflect, and think of our grievances. Thus, we must make a resolution to act from now on. We must repent for what we have failed to do, even though we should have been faithful.

Now, we must take on the work of God. Without this determination, even if heaven blesses us, we will not be able to bear it. We must resolve to inherit our Father's work as our own. I must feel the sorrow of God that He felt towards fallen Adam and Eve. We must establish the standards that we failed to establish in the past today. We must take responsibility for making Cain submit to Abel. Furthermore, God looked at Noah, who worked for 120 years, not with temporary joy but with the heart of eternal hope. This was because there was a standard He hoped Noah would become a universal mission bearer without any shortcomings. Knowing this, you must work with the same heart as Noah. 

Additionally, God had great expectations for Ham. However, the greater the expectation, the greater the impact of disappointment. Therefore, you must be able to look at God with universal sorrow. Only then can you inherit God's work and represent Him.

Now, through Abraham, Moses, and Jesus, we are approaching the time when the purpose of creation will be fulfilled, passing through the Old and New Testaments. If there is someone who calls God's work their own at this time, even though they are an individual, God will not see them merely as an individual but as a universal and cosmic being responsible for God's work.

What we must take responsibility for
If you understand that there is a great will and providence of the Father here, you can move with the firm belief that no one else can do it but you. This is the time when we must move in such a way. If the Father's work is a historical one, you must feel that you have a greater mission than anyone who has come and gone in history as one who has inherited the Father's work. In the past, one only had to fulfill the mission of that time, but today we must fulfill the mission of 6,000 years. You must thoroughly feel that God's work is my work. Additionally, my very being must take responsibility for Adam, Noah, Abraham, Moses, Jesus' indemnity, and even God's indemnity. Therefore, I must understand that I am the embodiment of historical purpose and hope.

So how should we act on behalf of God? Until now, the Father has been the Father of sorrow, pain, and unhappiness, and He has experienced the greatest misfortunes that humanity has never encountered. Thus, we must experience the path of unhappiness and lamentation, not the path of happiness. Only then can we resolve the historical unhappiness, lamentation, and grievances.

God has never had a day filled with joy and hope. In the midst of that, He has been working. God has walked the path of indemnity to restore individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world, working alone while maintaining that difficult position. We must never forget that He is such a Father. Where must I, who have inherited the Father's work, go? I must walk the path of lamentation, not the path of singing happiness. Until now, I have wished to live joyfully with God, but that cannot be. Since I have inherited the Father's work, I must take responsibility for everything. I must take responsibility for individuals, families, nations, the world, and even the heavenly world. I must bear the responsibility of lamentation, not joy. As one who has inherited the Father's work, I must take responsibility for the Father's sorrow and unhappiness. I have the responsibility to subdue Satan and confine him to hell.

Until now, God has only been able to block Satan but has not judged him. This is because there has been no one to fight on behalf of God. The responsibility to judge Satan and confine him to hell lies with us. If we cannot complete this responsibility, there will never be a day of joy for God, nor will there be a day of original joy and joyful work for us.

Now, where should you go? If you realize that you have not felt God's sorrow, you must go to a place where you can feel that sorrow. You cannot inherit the Father's work without passing through the place where you feel God's pain, sorrow, and adversity. Therefore, from now on, we must seek out the sad and unjust places. The world is the Father's workplace. No matter how much the world changes, it is undoubtedly the Father's workplace. If working in Korea is easy, we should feel ashamed for not being able to work in more difficult places. We must participate in difficult places to also participate in the places of benefit. We must strive to work in the most difficult places. Those of you who are going out after training must do so even more. We must carefully distribute and convey the Father's heart before this nation. 

If we know but do not act, the lamentation will only grow greater. 

Now that we understand the will, we must not leave the Father's work as merely the Father's work. Our ancestors have left it to us, so we, as their descendants, must take responsibility. Our ancestors did not know on earth, but they are now in the spirit world, lamenting. The lamentation of not knowing is great, but the lamentation of knowing and not acting is even greater.

I hope that you will inherit and bear the great work of the Father. So that through you, heaven can forget its sorrow for even a moment and enjoy joy. Until now, He has not been able to be a God of joy, but you must prepare a time of joy on His behalf. Only then will you have the face to meet the Father in the spirit world. How can you approach the Father with so many sad matters left undone? If that happens, you cannot face or serve the Father. Even if you do not have the capacity to take responsibility, your heart must have the standard to face not just thirty million but the whole world.

All the loyalty we offer will make it so that when the will is fulfilled on this earth, we will not be ashamed to be placed there. In terms of heart, there is no difference between those who do great things and those who do small things. In terms of loyalty, God sees them as having the same value. When the small person offers loyalty in their own way and shares joy, it can manifest as a condition of joy no matter where it is placed.

You must take responsibility for the area you are entrusted with. So that from the perspective of joy, you can say that there is no shame, and since it is my joy and your joy, please accept it. Only then can it become a holy place and a sacred place. You must go before the Father with such conditions. In other words, you must become someone who can leave behind and show the historical God, the God of the times, and the God of the future in your work.

You already know everything but have not acted. This is because you have not established a foundation that can be offered to God, a foundation that will not bring shame. 

I have understood what I must do. It is the Father's work and my work, and my work is the Father's work. I must create a victorious foundation that can make the Father rejoice and expand this to create God's garden. This is the new garden. Now, I must do what I must do before I die on this earth. My individual happiness must not be the goal. I must offer my individual self to fulfill God's work.

Jesus said, "The Son of Man has no place to lay His head." Thus, the disciples of Jesus are in the same position. Therefore, we must create a place where we can lay our heads. It is good to bring joy to the Father, but we must also establish the minimum standard of family, which is eternally belonging to God.

The purpose of restoration is to complete the hope of the son-in-law. After presenting the conditions of victory, you must prepare a foundation where I can rest, that is, a family. This must be done even if it means dying. Before fulfilling this mission, one should not even think of satisfaction or happiness. We started from suffering. It is more difficult than climbing Baekdu Mountain. Many prophets and sages have come and gone in history, but in terms of the division of providential mission, there have been many failures. However, I must be able to say that I am different. The path of 6,000 years of providence has traces of the blood and tears shed by God. These traces of blood and tears remain in both heaven and earth. The path you walk connects the past, present, and future. The suffering and trials must be able to represent the historical past, the contemporary present, and the hopeful future.

The substantial mission bearer of responsibility sharing
God has been carrying out the history of restoration through the First Israel, Second Israel, and Third Israel. In terms of purpose, the First Israel corresponds to the spirit world, the Second Israel corresponds to the saints on earth today, and the Third Israel represents the hopeful sons and daughters. The Second Israel comes through the First Israel, and the Third Israel comes through the Second Israel. To inherit the First Israel, one must receive Moses' blessing, and to inherit the Second Israel, one must receive Jesus' blessing. Originally, this is the case. If Moses did not receive the blessing on Mount Sinai conditioned on a 40-day fast, he could not be Moses, and if Jesus did not curse them on the cross at Golgotha and could not receive the blessing, he could not be Jesus. In this logic, the returning Lord must also lay the foundation of blessing without reaching the decisive final position. God cannot bless unless He is in a miserable position where He turned His face away from Jesus. 

Have you ever participated in a position where you could be blessed like Noah, Abraham, Moses, Jesus, and the Teacher? No, you have not. Moses came down from Mount Sinai with the tablets, and Jesus, who bore the cross, gave His blood. Therefore, we must keep the Ten Commandments and eat the flesh of the slain. The entire history, that is, the providential journey, has consistently set the conditions for indemnity. The tablets of Moses and the cross of Jesus are also for giving the resurrected body to humanity.

For a family or tribe to stand before heaven, they must always set the conditions for blessing. You must become a proactive being capable of receiving blessings.

You have established me in the position of a messenger. I will fulfill my responsibilities, so do not worry. You must set even a condition that can receive blessings. Otherwise, misfortune will come upon you. To inherit even one aspect of the blessing of succession, you must sweat and cry while fulfilling your responsibilities. Thus, you must stand as a victorious being that your ancestors can acknowledge. That is the responsibility that remains for us.

Until now, it has been conditional service, but in the end, it must be substantial service. In the future, the saints must perform substantial service. Conditional service cannot make one a faithful servant, nor can it be said that one has fulfilled their responsibilities. You must become a substantial mission bearer who repents of historical sins, harbors enmity towards the enemy, and vows to fulfill future responsibilities.

Dear ones, there can be no words like "slow down a little" in front of the steps we Unification Church members take. We must hurry. We must go with a noble appearance. How glorious is that? From such a position, we must receive heaven's sending and establish a foundation of victory that God cannot forget forever, whether it be a region or the world. We must create a world that not only includes my individual self but also extends to my descendants, so that the Father may receive glory forever. 

As I go to do such work, my hands are not just my hands, but hands that represent thirty million people and the entire human race. You must feel this. These hands are the Father's hands, and they must be hands that ancestors can boast of and descendants can commemorate.

You must embody the figures of Abraham, Moses, Jesus, and God. You must establish an unchangeable foundation that says what is within my jurisdiction cannot be taken away by Satan. These hands are the Father's hands, and this body is the Father's body. Therefore, you must become a figure that does not falter even when Satan attacks. When you go out to work, you must do so with the heart of representing Abel's altar and the heart of representing Noah's work. You must also carry the heart of how much God must have grieved over Ham's fall. You must resolve that you will not fail like Ham or other ancestors by experiencing such feelings.

You must be able to say, "I am being persecuted on behalf of historical figures." You must achieve a victory that can make the Father rejoice because of me. Otherwise, you cannot stand before the Father. In doing the Father's work, you must become the servant of servants, the best among servants, the adopted child among adopted children, and the son among sons. We Unification family members must be able to say, "I am the one who suffers the most in my region." Even if the leader of the earth falls to Satan, I must have the confidence that I can defeat Satan. If that happens, I can receive the blessings of that leader.

Blessings come to those who suffer.
God has had much suffering but little joy. The end times are when suffering and joy, unhappiness and happiness appear together. Blessings do not come to those who are comfortable but to those who are hungry, distressed, and weeping. As the heart becomes better, the blessings increase accordingly. The time is now when the actions of one person can affect descendants for thousands of generations. Blessings do not come to those who have not passed through suffering. Blessings do not come to those who have not shed blood, sweat, and tears in the place of suffering. You must go through the most painful position among servants and the most painful position among adopted children to receive more blessings.

Those who suffer more than those who live well receive blessings. The highest standard is the one who suffers the most. That is why the Teacher pushes you into places of suffering.

In that area, you must be able to say, "I am the only one who can do this." Only then will you fulfill your responsibilities. You must become the servant of servants, the adopted child of adopted children, and the son of sons, advancing to the eternal position of blessing that acknowledges even your descendants. 

As you go, you must go as a servant, as an adopted child, as a son, with the qualifications of the Holy Spirit and Jesus, and ultimately, you must go as a Father. The position of sons and daughters is a field of indemnity for oneself, while the positions of the Holy Spirit and Jesus are fields of indemnity for the Father. You must fulfill the Father's responsibilities to fulfill your own, becoming a complete being in relation to the past, present, and future.
Do not seek cooperation while walking the path. When each of you goes to the place you are responsible for, you must have the determination that this place cannot be without me. I will vigorously step forward to every corner of the land for my father's work. Only then can we receive blessings.

Now, you must swear that you will fight for heaven and earth in front of the tasks we must undertake. *

About Substantial Resurrection
<Summary of the Message> Today is the day of substantial resurrection, which we designated as a new memorial day last year. You must know that this day will be commemorated even in the future.

The noun resurrection is established on the premise of joy. God's ideal of creation is that all creatures must have substantial value for heaven, earth, people, and God to be joyful. If all creation could have merged at such an ideal standard, hopeful standard, victorious standard, and the highest glorious standard, it would have been indescribably happy.

The time to resurrect
All things created by God's hand, all things realized by God's word, imagine that glory. Today's heaven and earth are not like that. It is a regretful and resentful matter. The motivation and purpose of creation were not such, but due to the unexpected fall of humanity, the motivation and purpose of creation have been violated. The fall has become the source of pain, sorrow, and unhappiness, and has become the cause of everything that humans dislike. An enemy is not just someone wielding a sword. The fall! This is indeed the enemy of humanity, the enemy of all things, and the enemy of the Creator.

Where did this enemy begin? It started with our ancestors thousands of years ago. Therefore, while desperate struggles are certainly necessary, to uproot the root of this sin, we must trace back to the origin of the fall and blow it up and cut it off. Only then can we not relate to earthly humans. Because it still remains, sin is rampant in the world.

Believers should not fight over the results but should make finding the root of the fall their primary goal. We must find the enemy's stronghold, the source of the fall, and resolve that issue between God, humanity, and Satan. Otherwise, the thread of unhappiness will not be unraveled.

Until now, countless people have pursued the highest good. Jesus said, "What will it profit a man if he gains the whole world and loses his own soul?" No one has yet emerged who can say, "Look at me and envy me." To become such a valuable being, one must uproot the roots of hereditary sin from oneself on this earth. I am my own enemy.

The responsibility lies with everyone. Since we have not resolved it to this day, all that exists is an enemy. Therefore, we must examine all scriptures and point out the histories of failure. There has never been a time in human history when an enemy did not appear. More than any family or social environment, my individual self is the enemy; my heart is the problem.

In the end times, we, who are facing the day of judgment with the hope of resurrection, must first resolve ourselves. If we cannot resolve ourselves, the connection to resurrection has nothing to do with us. My body is the enemy. And the social environment that protects me is also in the position of an enemy. Why? Because of the fall. The motivation for the fall is that it did not pass through goodness. We are no different. So let us escape from the circumstances and conditions of the times and rise toward the Creator God.

Then, how can we regain hope? Instead of moving forward, we must turn back. We must ascend to the stage before the fallen ancestors of humanity and establish a connection with the Creator God. Then Satan will flee. To escape is to walk the path of life in the world of death. When we walk such a path, we connect with God and finally become true people, true love, true history, true brothers, true parents, true nations, and true worlds. However, this is not something we meet in front of us; we must go back to meet it. The original ideal of true peace, true freedom, true happiness, true ideals, and true values is not before us now. We must go beyond the stronghold of the fall. Today, there are many religions. They can be offerings but cannot be priests. To become a priest, one must turn back the way they came and establish a heart connection with God. Otherwise, one cannot escape judgment. In this regard, there is a difference between God's providential position and the perspective of ordinary people.

The standard of substantial resurrection
God originally desired to meet us on the foundation of a heart connection, but in ancient times, Adam and Eve and anyone else wanted to rule heaven and earth relatively. Since no one has yet established this connection, the Messiah came to establish it, and his second coming is also to re-establish this connection. It is believed that if all nations are simply led, it will become the ideal world, but in fact, it is the opposite.

The history of Israel began with Abraham. From the perspective of the time, history seems linear, but overall, history is cyclical. The Messiah came as the center to make it cyclical. The Messiah came to establish the standard that can draw the source and the line of history to make it cyclical.

The people of Israel did not know this. If they had known this, they could have presented the true self. Finding the true self, the original self, is resurrection. This was to start from Jesus and expand to family, nation, and country. If that had happened, the hoped-for true world would have followed.

If one does not share the same heart, life, and feelings with Jesus, one cannot walk together. Salvation is walking with the Messiah. If one establishes an inseparable relationship with the Messiah in heart, life, and feelings, one will automatically return. Learning the Bible is connecting with the life of the Messiah. In fact, all the environments until now have been enemies. Therefore, we must abandon everything and aim for something different. Only then will the history of salvation, restoration, recreation, and resurrection be realized.

The path is to go backward but ultimately connect with the central point. It cannot be anything but God's grateful providence. Since we cannot return vertically, God sent Jesus to connect us with his life and allow us to return. For Jesus to conclude the providence of salvation, he must subdue Satan, the enemy of 4,000 years of history, and resolve the grievances that have been tied up at every turn and say goodbye to Satan.

We cling to Jesus because he enables us to uproot even the roots of the fall. Therefore, the standard of faith life is Jesus. When the ancestors of humanity fell, their heart, personality, and substance all fell. That is why Jesus came to resurrect the heart, personality, and substance. However, he established the standard to resurrect the substance and personality but could not establish the standard to resurrect the heart. Thus, it remained as the standard of hope for the bride and groom.

The stages of substantial resurrection
We must have the original heart that has not fallen and be united with God. Moreover, the heart, personality, and substance must become one and connect with God's unchanging expectation. This is the ultimate purpose of salvation. Jesus established the standard for the salvation of the conscience but could not establish the standard for the salvation of the substance. Therefore, today's Christians, who stand on the standard of conscience, must strive for substantial salvation. Otherwise, they cannot fulfill the history of the second coming. Jesus hopes that we will become his substitute substance. Therefore, today’s believers must walk the path that Jesus must walk. Even if we walk the path of suffering and carry the cross to Golgotha without receiving punishment, we must become a valuable substance on that foundation for Jesus to return.

Because the hope and sovereignty that Jesus desires have not aligned, the second coming has been prolonged until now. If there had been someone among Jesus' disciples who could become Jesus' substitute substance, the history of the second coming would have ended then. The day when the saints unite with their original conscience and establish the standard of the bride and groom is the day of the second coming. On this standard, Jesus will return and fulfill his will; this is the history of the second coming. A person who has not established the standard of substantial resurrection cannot become a bride. 

The hope of the Trinity is in the one who will come again. Moreover, the hopes of all those who have come and gone throughout history, as well as our present and future generations, are the same. Yet, unaware of this, people say, "As long as I die and go to heaven, that's enough." However, no matter how difficult it is, it is the duty of Christians to reach that standard.

For 6,000 years, all the elements of suffering and unhappiness of all things, and the conditions of countless pains and groans of humanity must be borne all at once, and we must enter Satan's stronghold and subdue Satan. In other words, we must become offerings. We must die not for our own sake but to resolve the conditions of all the pains of the ancestors and all things in the historical process.

Since humanity has fallen, to restore oneself, one must fundamentally advance from servant to adopted child, from adopted child to true child, from true child to bride and groom, and from bride and groom to true parents. Because of the fall, the lower position is in the position of an offering to the higher position. Therefore, while one can be seen as existing for the higher position, ultimately, one exists for God.

The path of restoration is indeed a path full of sorrow. A priest must not only fulfill the responsibilities of the time but must also indemnify all historical standards and come forth without disappearing to qualify as a priest. Jesus came to the earth and touched the hearts of the ancestors. Thus, Jesus becomes not only the Jesus of the time but also the historical Jesus. In serving God, we must bring the historical God and serve him as the God of the time. Only then can one become the greatest filial child.

To become a being capable of substantial resurrection in the future, one must indemnify the historical standard and win without falling in the battles of reality. Only then can one achieve substantial resurrection. The day that happens is the day of substantial resurrection. Once this standard is established, the world of sorrow will say, "Farewell. We are returning," and the era of substance will come. Through the historical struggle process, we must complete the standard of the bride and groom, which is the hope of Jesus, so that the heavenly kingdom we desire on earth can be realized.

We must keep all of Jesus' words. However, Jesus could not speak the final words. He could not speak the words of the heart. Therefore, he could not convey the circumstances. He could not teach the duties of brothers, the duties of children, and the duties of parents, nor could he teach the image of God and the ceremony of blessing in the scriptures.

To complete all historical standards and be able to keep anything, we must be able to meet the day of the second coming. Now, if there is someone who has received the mission of Jesus on this earth and has received the heart of God, that person is the main character of this world. Substantial resurrection must also pass through the heart. That day is the day when heaven and earth will turn.

For the day of substantial resurrection to come, there must be substantial parents, and substantial children must be established. You must advance to the place of glory through substantial resurrection. To do this, you must fight with blood and sweat. Thus, you must establish the sovereignty of glory. This path is one that must be taken whether one lives or dies.

Achieve substantial resurrection
In conclusion, until now, humanity has lived facing death. In reality, there can be no resurrection without death. Jesus' resurrection also came after death, so we too must go through the path of the cross, even if briefly, to achieve resurrection. Jesus bore the cross from a national standard at that time. Therefore, people have not yet transcended the national cross. The one who transcends this national standard and bears the cross of history and the times at the global standard is the Lord of the second coming.

We must not fall here. No matter what suffering we endure, we must never fall. The national standard is the limit. Once we surpass that standard, the global standard will naturally come in. We must surpass the standard of Jesus' suffering for the standard of glory centered on substance to approach.

From Adam to Jesus, 4,000 years, from Abraham to Jesus, 40 generations, according to this official standard, the completion of the will is also centered around 40 peaks.

The time when we can repay God before the day of the glorious resurrection centered on substance will be the end. To strike Satan in the name of God's sons and daughters is evangelism. The place of evangelism is a place of tears, a place where historical ancestors bless us for fighting well, and a place where future descendants look forward with hopeful eyes. In other words, that place is a place of rebirth from the position of a servant to that of an adopted child, from the position of an adopted child to that of a true child. It is God's wish that we establish this connection of rebirth and achieve substantial resurrection. We must establish the standard of resurrection horizontally through historical standards.

In the future, we will become absolute beings who can only sing of joy without knowing death, who cannot be exchanged for anything. You must establish the standard of hope to live eternally with God and achieve substantial resurrection, which God desires. Only then will you clearly understand that you can go before God. 
* 

Who was I?
<Summary of the Message> This year is the last year of a profoundly significant three-year period. This spring is an even more crucial time. Just as the past two years were significant, this year also holds profound importance. If you have gathered here, I hope you will remain safe until the end, bearing the responsibility of representing the entire family.

The title of today's message is "Who was I?" Each of you has lived differently, and tribes have lived differently based on their traditions. However, the common point is that we have lived within the history of sin. From the perspective of God's ideal of creation, the original existence of "I" holds infinite value, but the current "I" is a worthless existence.

Each individual is connected to the past, present, and future. Therefore, one's individual existence does not remain isolated. It is a historical individual. I am a descendant who has not shed original sin, inheriting the ties of sin. Thus, I have the responsibility to conclude the ties of the fall. This must be understood. I am the substitute for the numerous providential figures who have appeared throughout history since Adam. I possess both a good position and a position contrary to it. Now, I must settle the sins and take only the position of good. However, I have not yet become a self that has settled the sins. 

This mission remains for us to establish a standard of goodness before the Father at some point in time. Unless I become a self that God can trust, I will become a betrayer before the hardworking God and cause disappointment. I must understand that I am not just myself but also in the position of ancestors who did not fail. From this moment on, I must become a self that does not betray God and does not cause trouble for God. Otherwise, there is no significance in gathering here.

Who was I? I am a self that could not see the noun "blessing." The more I feel such things, the more I must entrust myself to the Father.
From now on,  
I must become a pure position with absolutely nothing personal.  
Soon, I must completely entrust myself to the Father from the standpoint of having nothing. The existence of "me" does not exist. I must realize that my past self is unacceptable and entrust it to God. God will take responsibility for good and evil and I must stand in the position of nothingness to move towards goodness.  
The fact that Adam made God sorrowful through the fall, Cain's sin of not obeying Abel, Ham's mistake in the providence centered on Noah, the history of twists and turns centered on Abraham, the history of sorrow centered on Moses, the history of resentment centered on Jesus, all these resentful and indignant histories, as well as your own position must be indemnified. I must indemnify the sorrowful events of Adam and Abel, the sorrowful events of Noah and Ham, and the sorrowful events of Abraham and Moses so that God can look upon them with hope. This is your responsibility. You must empathize with the circumstances and feelings of Adam, Abel, Noah, Abraham, Moses, or Jesus and say, "Father, I will not become like them. I will not become like John the Baptist or Jesus. I will not become a group that makes God sorrowful." You must have the determination to return hope to God with the loyalty that ancestors have not been able to show until now. Moreover, God, what did You want to give to Adam? Leave a connection of blessings. You must be able to do this.  
You must establish the emotional connection that the mission bearers like Noah, Abraham, and Moses wanted to establish. You must inherit the feelings that historical ancestors could not inherit. You are neither the fallen Adam and Eve, nor Cain and Abel, nor Noah or Ham, nor any of the ancestors of history. However, you must connect the hearts of Adam to Noah, Abraham, Moses, and Jesus. You and the teacher have the responsibility to connect the hearts of the historical mission bearers who have been separated from Adam. The teacher must inherit the heart from Adam to Jesus and must establish a victorious connection. This is the historical content that has been fought for until today. Connecting from Adam to the end and presenting it before heaven and earth is the ideal of the Second Coming and the will of the True Parents. If you do not feel the ideals and will of the True Parents, you cannot be blessed. Until now, I have been a historical traitor and an unforgivable sinner. Therefore, I want to connect the substantial parents only to those who have prepared an environment where they can resolve their groans and resentments and can serve the center of reality.  
The True Parents exist to inherit God's legacy, and you exist to inherit the legacy of the True Parents. We must understand the sad content of the heart and providential history of the True Parents. We must become one with the True Parents to advance to the position of blessing. To do this, I must make the sorrow, pain, and joy of the True Parents, as well as the sorrow, pain, and joy of Jesus, my own. If I do not live as one completely and do not become the position of a substitute, it is of no use. Historically, I cannot stand in the position of blessing without being the one who substitutes for the True Parents before Adam, Noah, Abraham, Moses, Jesus, or before heaven and earth. The man is the embodiment of the father, and the woman is the embodiment of the mother. This term "embodiment" is filled with historical tears and historical sorrows and twists. Therefore, if we do not indemnify these historical tears, sorrows, and twists, we cannot proceed.  
I should not say, "Why am I not being blessed despite being like this?" We must graft ourselves onto the heart, reality, and all the words of the True Parents that span the past, present, and future. If we do not fall behind the blessed predecessors who have been blessed on behalf of the True Parents, and if we say that we will take on their responsibilities if they cannot, we will undoubtedly receive the same blessings as them. We must have the determination that although I was lacking in the past, I must not become one who is lacking until the end. The individual purpose is not permitted. You cannot be blessed unless you substitute for the True Parents.  
I ask you to spend the next 20 days in the position of the second parents, that is, in a privileged position. The man is in the position of substituting for the father, and the woman is in the position of substituting for the mother. Through this training period, I ask you to experience the heart of the parents and the heart of the siblings.  
Work from the position of repentance.  
<Summary of the words> Let us become people who boast of lineage, reality, and heart. Be cautious in what you see, hear, and say. By doing so, you must take pride in becoming an ancestor. You must become someone who has confidence in this regard.  
Mistakes made after this year cannot be forgiven. The only thing that can be boasted of in the world is becoming an ancestor of goodness.  
Pray and prepare three days before the end of each month. On the day before, all the members in Gyeonggi Province must gather and discuss each other's righteousness. We must clarify public and private matters. Heaven cannot recognize even one-third of the private.  
Standing before the public is truly a fearful thing. You must act in accordance with the will before you can avoid slander. When doing something joyful, it must be done from the position of repentance. Even if the teacher wants to go sightseeing alone, he cannot.  
Couples should not speak carelessly unless they are confident in judging from the position of judges. Speaking carelessly is because they have not experienced the hardships of evangelism together.  
You must establish a worldview centered on yourself. Before you can love your own children, you must establish children of faith. If you fall behind in evangelism, it is as if you have no ancestors, and thereafter you cannot set an example.  
Even mothers with babies must evangelize. Those who will go to heaven love God more than their own babies. God also valued His ideals more than Adam and Eve. You must empathize with God's heart while looking at your baby. Children tend to resemble their parents, whether good or bad. If you do not repent despite having conditions you must fulfill, your children cannot emulate good things.  
This June 4th celebration must be done by you. Since the teacher is in the position of a parent, he can only hold a celebration for Abel-like children after holding a celebration for Cain-like children. The teacher should not pay for it. You must do it. After finishing the meal, I do not wish to drive you out immediately, but I cannot help but block Satan.  
Women must restore wealth even if they have to do business. The man is the bone, and the woman is the flesh. The first, second, and third families working together is like heaven and earth working together. To establish our lives, we must establish the position of all members at the lowest level before establishing our own position.  
<Meaning of the Holy Offering>  
<Summary of the words> It is now 1:40 AM; this time is like a bachelor entering the bride's room.  
We must achieve the purpose of love by uniting left and right centered on God.  
What is here is alcohol. One of the meanings of this alcohol is something even Mr. Yoo Hyowon does not know. This alcohol contains words like "those who drink the living water of Jesus will have eternal life."  
The time before and after this is different. Drinking this alcohol is more important than the bride and groom establishing a relationship of love. This can represent a life-giving connection.  
This alcohol is like a life nucleus. After this meal, there must be no falsehood. Do not ask about the past; from now on, you must become a blessed couple.  
June 3, 1962, 1:40 AM, former headquarters church.  
* These words were spoken during the 72-family blessing ceremony and have been organized from the records of former association president Yoo Hyowon. The title was added by the editor.  
<Who am I?>  
<Summary of the words> (After the teacher recognized those who have been members for less than six months and first-time visitors)  
You have come here today to receive training for a greater purpose. However, if you live a self-centered life from now on, the significance of receiving training for a greater purpose will be lost. You must abandon yourself and absolutely obey the will.  
From now on, you will live in a communal life for 40 days, so today you are in a solemn moment of stepping into the public role. You must be absorbed in the public purpose and each become a material to achieve that purpose. I believe you have already made this resolution. Therefore, from now on, even if you have eyes, you cannot see as you please; even if you have a mouth, you cannot speak as you please; even if you have ears, you cannot hear as you please. I want to give the members of the headquarters the trial of treating you poorly to train you.  
When you left your local area to come to the headquarters that you longed for so much, you probably had many expectations, but in reality, it will not meet those expectations. The appearance is so shabby and there is nothing to see. However, the inner spirit must be able to grasp heaven and earth. If anyone has a will, whether man or woman, it is worth trying once.  
You cannot rise to a position where you can command the world all at once. Even if you can rise, you should not. It is only possible after becoming a person of character who has both internal and external environments. Money is not the issue; it is always a matter of being human. You must not become someone who boasts of yourself. You must become someone who can give public orders regarding history. Being public means not serving oneself but serving the whole, the nation, and the world. To become such a public person, you must be able to do anything. If there are no men, women must be able to do even men's work.  
Your hands are not yours. Even when you eat with your hands, you must think that you are eating on behalf of the 30 million people, eating on behalf of the hands of all humanity. Even if it is a simple meal of barley rice and soybean paste stew, you must eat from a public standpoint. You must move your whole body in that way. Therefore, there can be no complaints or dissatisfaction. Sometimes, you may be commanded to fast for three days.  
Training is about polishing and refining, isn't it? What standard will you use for polishing and refining? Among you, there are two types of people. One is the outer person who is just a piece of meat, and the other is the inner person. From the fallen standpoint, there is the fallen outer person and the fallen inner person.  
These must resemble the original personality. The original personality is like a child whom all things worship and whom God embraces and kisses. Therefore, you must receive training based on the original personality.  
You are, in reality, a pitiful existence. Therefore, you must start training from the lowest level. From tomorrow, the real training begins. To become someone who can embrace the world and even subdue Satan, you must overcome even the baptism of hell's bottom. Training is for finding this nature of self.  
So, who am I? The center of today's message is this. The fallen human has nothing to boast about. The more you boast, the more disgraceful it is. The appearance you think is great is, in reality, pitiful.  
Look up to the heavens and imagine that there is the protagonist of creation there. What can you present before Him? Do you have confidence that you can bring joy to all things? You probably do not. When centered on God, no one can claim to be a filial child or a loyal subject. You do not have the qualifications to present yourself before the heavenly principles. Moreover, you have nothing to boast about even before human ethics and morals. If the label of unfilial is attached, no matter how good you are personally, you cannot present yourself before family, nation, world, heaven and earth, and the Creator. Sin is not keeping one's loyalty personally and doing things that cannot be tolerated socially. When such sins are committed, God cannot say, "Oh, I will forgive you."  
Do you have anything to present before the public God? You probably do not. God, who comes out with a public worldview, will ultimately judge the world as the Creator. This end time is precisely that judgment time.  
To avoid this judgment, you must swear that you will keep all the words that God has given over the past 6,000 years throughout your life, and you must be able to say that you have done so. The peak of judgment requires absolute obedience to the commands coming down from heaven, and even if you cannot do it during your lifetime, you must make a will to your descendants to ensure it is accomplished.  
God seeks those who obey historical commands.  
Father, why have You become so miserable! Just give me the commands. I will keep them. You must be able to do this. Even in thought, you must do so.  
Then, what kind of figure am I? My figure is even more unsatisfactory. It is a complete mess. Therefore, I must separate the sins that are stirring within me and burn them in fire, and I must at least have the intention to purify my heart. Only then can I say, "Please give me a global command before heaven." to enter the paradise of the earth and the world of freedom.  
We are beings that cannot be accepted. God has been betrayed by such unacceptable humans until now. This body! This body has become a sacrifice for Satan. God has come out hoping that humans would become the original substance, but since they have not become that substance, humans are betrayers of the word, betrayers of the substance, betrayers of the heart, and betrayers of the lineage.  
Then, what will God do by training you, the descendants of historical betrayers? He will train you to send you out before Satan. Therefore, you will face harsh and frightening trials. You are in a position where you must create a person who is truly human and send them out before Satan. You must stand before the countless ancestors who have come and gone throughout history, such as Abraham and Moses, and say, "What have you done? I will do all that you could not do." You must also call out to the historical Satans.  
Today, you gathering here and learning through training is an incredibly fortunate thing. At this time, you must walk the path of victory with the title of filial child. Under the determination to take responsibility for the 6,000 years of sinful history, you must become a prince of obedience and a prince of submission before God. Just like Jesus prayed, "Not my will, but Yours be done," after establishing the standard of a filial child, you must say, "Satan has finally bowed down before us," to enter the kingdom of heaven.  
Thus, you must become the ancestor of the word, the ancestor of the substance, the ancestor of the heart, the ancestor of obedience, and the ancestor of the lineage.  
Thinking of God's will, each of you must realize that you are historical betrayers and must bear historical indignation to fight and win against Satan. Only by receiving Satan's surrender will you know who you are. You must become the ancestor of the new word, the ancestor of the new heart, the ancestor of the new substance, and the ancestor of the new lineage. You must become the ancestor of new victory. Originally, we should have been like this, but due to the fall, we could not be, so we must feel indignant about all this and say, "I will do it all."
We must step forward and declare that we will accomplish this. Is this easy? However, in our time, we must bring an end to the history of return with our own hands. *
